File: shared\data\src\lib\utils\cancellation.utils.ts
/*
 * Copyright (c) 2025 FMR Corp.
 * All Rights Reserved.
 *
 * Fidelity Confidential Information.
 * Created on Sep 22, 2025
 */

import {
  CancellationReason,
  BATCH_ADJUSTMENT_REASONS,
  SINGLE_ADJUSTMENT_REASONS,
  CANCELLATION_REASONS,
} from '../constants/cancellation-reasons';

/**
 * Helper function to get appropriate cancellation reasons based on context
 * @param isBatchOperation - true for multiple items, false for single item
 * @returns the appropriate reason codes array
 */
export function getCancellationReasons(
  isBatchOperation: boolean,
): CancellationReason[] {
  return isBatchOperation
    ? BATCH_ADJUSTMENT_REASONS
    : SINGLE_ADJUSTMENT_REASONS;
}

/**
 * Returns the description for a cancel reason code.
 * Searches all known reason lists.
 */
export function getCancelReasonDisplayText(code: string): string {
  if (!code || code.trim() === '') {
    return '';
  }

  const allReasons: CancellationReason[] = [
    ...CANCELLATION_REASONS,
    ...BATCH_ADJUSTMENT_REASONS,
    ...SINGLE_ADJUSTMENT_REASONS,
  ];

  if (code.includes(',')) {
    const codes = code
      .split(',')
      .map((c) => c.trim())
      .filter((c) => c !== '');

    const descriptions = codes.map((c) => {
      const found = allReasons.find((r) => r.code === c);
      return found ? found.description : c;
    });

    return descriptions.join(', ');
  } else {
    const found = allReasons.find((r) => r.code === code.trim());
    return found ? found.description : code;
  }
}

import { getCancellationReasons } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';
import { ComponentFixture, TestBed } from '@angular/core/testing';
import { CancelOutrightComponent } from './cancel-outright.component';
import { MatDialogRef, MAT_DIALOG_DATA } from '@angular/material/dialog';
import { HttpClient } from '@angular/common/http';
import { MatSnackBar } from '@angular/material/snack-bar';
import { FormBuilder } from '@angular/forms';
import { ChangeDetectorRef } from '@angular/core';
import { Store } from '@ngrx/store';
import { BrowserAnimationsModule } from '@angular/platform-browser/animations';

describe('CancelOutrightComponent', () => {
  let component: CancelOutrightComponent;
  let fixture: ComponentFixture<CancelOutrightComponent>;

  beforeEach(async () => {
    await TestBed.configureTestingModule({
      imports: [CancelOutrightComponent, BrowserAnimationsModule],
      providers: [
        { provide: MatDialogRef, useValue: { close: jest.fn() } },
        {
          provide: MAT_DIALOG_DATA,
          useValue: {
            selectedTrades: [],
            selectedExecutions: [],
            cancelType: 'trades',
            cancelServiceUrl: '',
          },
        },
        {
          provide: HttpClient,
          useValue: { post: () => ({ pipe: () => ({}) }) },
        },
        { provide: MatSnackBar, useValue: { open: () => {} } },
        { provide: FormBuilder, useValue: new FormBuilder() },
        { provide: ChangeDetectorRef, useValue: { markForCheck: () => {} } },
        {
          provide: Store,
          useValue: {
            select: () => ({ pipe: () => ({ subscribe: () => {} }) }),
          },
        },
      ],
    }).compileComponents();

    fixture = TestBed.createComponent(CancelOutrightComponent);
    component = fixture.componentInstance;
    fixture.detectChanges();
  });

  it('should create', () => {
    expect(component).toBeTruthy();
  });

  describe('onConfirmCancel', () => {
    it('should exit early if canSubmit returns false', async () => {
      const canSubmitSpy = jest
        .spyOn(component, 'canSubmit')
        .mockReturnValue(false);
      component.isProcessing = false;
      await component.onConfirmCancel();
      expect(component.isProcessing).toBe(false);
      canSubmitSpy.mockRestore();
    });
  });

  it('should call setupFormValidation on ngOnInit', () => {
    const spy = jest.spyOn(component as any, 'setupFormValidation');
    component.ngOnInit();
    expect(spy).toHaveBeenCalled();
    spy.mockRestore();
  });

  describe('canSubmit', () => {
    it('should return true if form is valid and not processing', () => {
      component.cancelForm.get('reason')?.setValue('SOME_REASON');
      component.cancelForm.get('customReason')?.setValue('');
      component.isProcessing = false;
      expect(component.canSubmit()).toBe(true);
    });

    it('should return false if form is invalid', () => {
      component.cancelForm.setErrors({ some: 'error' });
      component.isProcessing = false;
      expect(component.canSubmit()).toBe(false);
    });

    it('should return false if processing', () => {
      component.cancelForm.setErrors(null); // valid
      component.isProcessing = true;
      expect(component.canSubmit()).toBe(false);
    });
  });

  describe('getCancelTypeDisplayName', () => {
    it('should return "Trade" for cancelType "trades"', () => {
      component.data.cancelType = 'trades';
      expect(component.getCancelTypeDisplayName()).toBe('Trade');
    });

    it('should return "Execution" for cancelType "executions"', () => {
      component.data.cancelType = 'executions';
      expect(component.getCancelTypeDisplayName()).toBe('Execution');
    });

    it('should return "Items" for cancelType "mixed"', () => {
      component.data.cancelType = 'mixed';
      expect(component.getCancelTypeDisplayName()).toBe('Items');
    });

    it('should return "Items" for unknown cancelType', () => {
      // @ts-expect-error testing fallback
      component.data.cancelType = 'unknown';
      expect(component.getCancelTypeDisplayName()).toBe('Items');
    });
  });

  describe('getTotalItemsCount', () => {
    it('should return 0 when both arrays are empty', () => {
      component.data.selectedTrades = [];
      component.data.selectedExecutions = [];
      expect(component.getTotalItemsCount()).toBe(0);
    });

    it('should return the length of selectedTrades when selectedExecutions is empty', () => {
      component.data.selectedTrades = [
        { entityId: 't1' } as any,
        { entityId: 't2' } as any,
      ];
      component.data.selectedExecutions = [];
      expect(component.getTotalItemsCount()).toBe(2);
    });

    it('should return the length of selectedExecutions when selectedTrades is empty', () => {
      component.data.selectedTrades = [];
      component.data.selectedExecutions = [{ executionId: 'e1' } as any];
      expect(component.getTotalItemsCount()).toBe(1);
    });

    it('should return the sum of both arrays lengths', () => {
      component.data.selectedTrades = [{ entityId: 't1' } as any];
      component.data.selectedExecutions = [
        { executionId: 'e1' } as any,
        { executionId: 'e2' } as any,
      ];
      expect(component.getTotalItemsCount()).toBe(3);
    });
  });

  describe('togglePreview', () => {
    it('should toggle showPreview from false to true and back', () => {
      expect(component.showPreview).toBe(false);
      component.togglePreview();
      expect(component.showPreview).toBe(true);
      component.togglePreview();
      expect(component.showPreview).toBe(false);
    });
  });

  describe('trackTradeById', () => {
    it('should return the entityId of the trade', () => {
      const trade = { entityId: 'trade-123' } as any;
      expect(component.trackTradeById(0, trade)).toBe('trade-123');
    });
  });

  describe('trackExecutionById', () => {
    it('should return the executionId of the execution', () => {
      const execution = { executionId: 'exec-456' } as any;
      expect(component.trackExecutionById(0, execution)).toBe('exec-456');
    });
  });

  describe('onCancel', () => {
    it('should call dialogRef.close', () => {
      const closeSpy = jest.spyOn((component as any).dialogRef, 'close');
      component.onCancel();
      expect(closeSpy).toHaveBeenCalled();
      closeSpy.mockRestore();
    });
  });

  describe('cancellationReasons', () => {
    afterEach(() => {
      jest.clearAllMocks();
    });

    it('should call getCancellationReasons with false for single item', () => {
      (getCancellationReasons as jest.Mock).mockImplementation(() => []);
      component.data.selectedTrades = [{ entityId: 't1' } as any];
      component.data.selectedExecutions = [];
      (component as any).getTotalItemsCount = () => 1;
      component.cancellationReasons;
      expect(getCancellationReasons).toHaveBeenCalledWith(false);
    });

    it('should call getCancellationReasons with true for multiple items', () => {
      (getCancellationReasons as jest.Mock).mockImplementation(() => []);
      component.data.selectedTrades = [
        { entityId: 't1' } as any,
        { entityId: 't2' } as any,
      ];
      component.data.selectedExecutions = [];
      (component as any).getTotalItemsCount = () => 2;
      component.cancellationReasons;
      expect(getCancellationReasons).toHaveBeenCalledWith(true);
    });
  });
  describe('getFinalReason', () => {
    it('should return the reason code even when OTR with custom reason', () => {
      component.cancelForm.get('reason')?.setValue('OTR');
      component.cancelForm.get('customReason')?.setValue('My custom reason');
      expect((component as any).getFinalReason()).toBe('OTR');
    });

    it('should return the reason code for non-OTR reasons', () => {
      component.cancelForm.get('reason')?.setValue('SOME_REASON');
      component.cancelForm.get('customReason')?.setValue('Should not use this');
      expect((component as any).getFinalReason()).toBe('SOME_REASON');
    });
  });
  describe('getEntityId (private)', () => {
    it('should return entityId for trade object', () => {
      const trade = { entityId: 'trade-1' };
      expect((component as any).getEntityId(trade)).toBe('trade-1');
    });

    it('should return executionId for execution object', () => {
      const execution = { executionId: 'exec-1' };
      expect((component as any).getEntityId(execution)).toBe('exec-1');
    });
  });
  describe('getEntityId (private)', () => {
    it('should return entityId for trade object', () => {
      const trade = { entityId: 'trade-1' };
      expect((component as any).getEntityId(trade)).toBe('trade-1');
    });

    it('should return executionId for execution object', () => {
      const execution = { executionId: 'exec-1' };
      expect((component as any).getEntityId(execution)).toBe('exec-1');
    });
  });
  describe('getEntityLevel (private)', () => {
    it('should return "T" for trade object', () => {
      const trade = { entityId: 'trade-1' };
      expect((component as any).getEntityLevel(trade)).toBe('T');
    });

    it('should return "E" for execution object', () => {
      const execution = { executionId: 'exec-1' };
      expect((component as any).getEntityLevel(execution)).toBe('E');
    });
  });
  describe('getEntityLevel (private)', () => {
    it('should return "T" for trade object', () => {
      const trade = { entityId: 'trade-1' };
      expect((component as any).getEntityLevel(trade)).toBe('T');
    });

    it('should return "E" for execution object', () => {
      const execution = { executionId: 'exec-1' };
      expect((component as any).getEntityLevel(execution)).toBe('E');
    });
  });
  describe('getItemStatus (private)', () => {
    it('should return tradeStatus for trade object', () => {
      const trade = { tradeStatus: 'TRADE_STATUS' };
      expect((component as any).getItemStatus(trade)).toBe('TRADE_STATUS');
    });

    it('should return executionStatusCode for execution object', () => {
      const execution = { executionStatusCode: 'EXEC_STATUS' };
      expect((component as any).getItemStatus(execution)).toBe('EXEC_STATUS');
    });

    it('should return empty string for unknown object', () => {
      const unknown = { foo: 'bar' };
      expect((component as any).getItemStatus(unknown)).toBe('');
    });
  });
  describe('getItemStatus (private)', () => {
    it('should return tradeStatus for trade object', () => {
      const trade = { tradeStatus: 'TRADE_STATUS' };
      expect((component as any).getItemStatus(trade)).toBe('TRADE_STATUS');
    });

    it('should return executionStatusCode for execution object', () => {
      const execution = { executionStatusCode: 'EXEC_STATUS' };
      expect((component as any).getItemStatus(execution)).toBe('EXEC_STATUS');
    });

    it('should return empty string for unknown object', () => {
      const unknown = { foo: 'bar' };
      expect((component as any).getItemStatus(unknown)).toBe('');
    });
  });
  describe('getRecordVersion (private)', () => {
    it('should return recordVersionNumber if present and a number', () => {
      const item = { recordVersionNumber: 42 };
      expect((component as any).getRecordVersion(item)).toBe(42);
    });

    it('should return 0 if recordVersionNumber is missing', () => {
      const item = { foo: 'bar' };
      expect((component as any).getRecordVersion(item)).toBe(0);
    });

    it('should return 0 if recordVersionNumber is not a number', () => {
      const item = { recordVersionNumber: 'not-a-number' };
      expect((component as any).getRecordVersion(item)).toBe(0);
    });
  });
  describe('getRecordVersion (private)', () => {
    it('should return recordVersionNumber if present and a number', () => {
      const item = { recordVersionNumber: 42 };
      expect((component as any).getRecordVersion(item)).toBe(42);
    });

    it('should return 0 if recordVersionNumber is missing', () => {
      const item = { foo: 'bar' };
      expect((component as any).getRecordVersion(item)).toBe(0);
    });

    it('should return 0 if recordVersionNumber is not a number', () => {
      const item = { recordVersionNumber: 'not-a-number' };
      expect((component as any).getRecordVersion(item)).toBe(0);
    });
  });
  describe('getCurrentUserCorpId (private)', () => {
    it('should return the corpId if set', () => {
      (component as any).corpId = 'CORP123';
      expect((component as any).getCurrentUserCorpId()).toBe('CORP123');
    });

    it('should return null if corpId is not set', () => {
      (component as any).corpId = null;
      expect((component as any).getCurrentUserCorpId()).toBeNull();
    });
  });
  describe('generateRequestId (private)', () => {
    it('should return a string starting with "cancel-" and containing a timestamp and random part', () => {
      const id = (component as any).generateRequestId();
      expect(id).toMatch(/^cancel-\d+-[a-z0-9]+$/);
    });
  });
  describe('createCancelRequest (private)', () => {
    it('should return a request object with reasonCode for non-OTR reason', () => {
      component.cancelForm.get('reason')?.setValue('SOME_REASON');
      component.cancelForm.get('customReason')?.setValue('');
      const item = { entityId: 'trade-1', recordVersionNumber: 7 };
      const reason = 'SOME_REASON';
      const req = (component as any).createCancelRequest(item, reason);
      expect(req).toHaveProperty('requestId');
      expect(req.reasonCode).toBe('SOME_REASON');
      expect(req.entity.entityId).toBe('trade-1');
      expect(req.entity.recordVersionNumber).toBe(7);
      expect(req.reasonText).toBeUndefined();
    });

    it('should set both reasonCode and reasonText when reason is OTR with custom text', () => {
      component.cancelForm.get('reason')?.setValue('OTR');
      component.cancelForm
        .get('customReason')
        ?.setValue('Custom cancellation reason');
      const item = { entityId: 'trade-1', recordVersionNumber: 7 };
      const reason = 'OTR';
      const req = (component as any).createCancelRequest(item, reason);
      expect(req).toHaveProperty('requestId');
      expect(req.reasonCode).toBe('OTR');
      expect(req.reasonText).toBe('Custom cancellation reason');
      expect(req.entity.entityId).toBe('trade-1');
      expect(req.entity.recordVersionNumber).toBe(7);
    });

    it('should work correctly for execution items with OTR and custom reason', () => {
      component.cancelForm.get('reason')?.setValue('OTR');
      component.cancelForm
        .get('customReason')
        ?.setValue('Execution custom reason');
      const item = { executionId: 'exec-1', recordVersionNumber: 5 };
      const reason = 'OTR';
      const req = (component as any).createCancelRequest(item, reason);
      expect(req).toHaveProperty('requestId');
      expect(req.reasonCode).toBe('OTR');
      expect(req.reasonText).toBe('Execution custom reason');
      expect(req.entity.entityId).toBe('exec-1');
      expect(req.entity.recordVersionNumber).toBe(5);
    });
  });
  describe('createUserEnvDetails (private)', () => {
    it('should return correct details for trade object', () => {
      (component as any).corpId = 'CORP123';
      const trade = { entityId: 'trade-1' };
      const details = (component as any).createUserEnvDetails(trade);
      expect(details).toEqual({
        userCorpId: 'CORP123',
        entityType: 'trade',
        mode: 'cancel',
      });
    });

    it('should return correct details for execution object', () => {
      (component as any).corpId = 'CORP123';
      const execution = { executionId: 'exec-1' };
      const details = (component as any).createUserEnvDetails(execution);
      expect(details).toEqual({
        userCorpId: 'CORP123',
        entityType: 'execution',
        mode: 'cancel',
      });
    });
  });
  describe('getCancelUrl (private)', () => {
    it('should return the cancelServiceUrl if set', () => {
      component.data.cancelServiceUrl = 'http://test-url';
      expect((component as any).getCancelUrl()).toBe('http://test-url');
    });

    it('should throw an error if cancelServiceUrl is not set', () => {
      component.data.cancelServiceUrl = '';
      expect(() => (component as any).getCancelUrl()).toThrow(
        'Cancel service URL is not set.',
      );
    });
  });
});

File: shared\ui\src\lib\cancel-outright\cancel-outright.component.ts
import {
  Component,
  Inject,
  OnInit,
  ChangeDetectionStrategy,
  OnDestroy,
  ChangeDetectorRef,
} from '@angular/core';
import { Store } from '@ngrx/store';
import { Observable, Subject, takeUntil } from 'rxjs';
import { CommonModule } from '@angular/common';
import {
  FormBuilder,
  FormGroup,
  Validators,
  ReactiveFormsModule,
} from '@angular/forms';
import {
  MAT_DIALOG_DATA,
  MatDialog,
  MatDialogConfig,
  MatDialogModule,
  MatDialogRef,
} from '@angular/material/dialog';
import { MatSnackBar, MatSnackBarModule } from '@angular/material/snack-bar';
import { MatFormFieldModule } from '@angular/material/form-field';
import { MatSelectModule } from '@angular/material/select';
import { MatInputModule } from '@angular/material/input';
import { MatCheckboxModule } from '@angular/material/checkbox';
import { MatButtonModule } from '@angular/material/button';
import { MatDividerModule } from '@angular/material/divider';
import { MatIconModule } from '@angular/material/icon';
import { MatCardModule } from '@angular/material/card';
import { MatListModule } from '@angular/material/list';

import {
  TradeModel,
  ExecutionModel,
  CancellationReason,
  getCancellationReasons,
} from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';
import * as fromUser from '@fmr-pr000539/eqt-ngrx-user-module';
import {
  CancelReply,
  CancelService,
  ProcessCancelReplyResult,
  UserEnvDetails,
  XaEntityRequest,
} from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/data-access/cancel';
import { MultiCancelDialogData } from './models/multi-cancel-dialog-data.interface';
import { CancelResult } from './models/cancel-result.interface';
@Component({
  // eslint-disable-next-line @angular-eslint/component-selector
  selector: 'exac-ui-multi-cancel-dialog',
  templateUrl: './cancel-outright.component.html',
  styleUrls: ['./cancel-outright.component.scss'],
  changeDetection: ChangeDetectionStrategy.OnPush,
  imports: [
    CommonModule,
    ReactiveFormsModule,
    MatDialogModule,
    MatSnackBarModule,
    MatFormFieldModule,
    MatSelectModule,
    MatInputModule,
    MatCheckboxModule,
    MatButtonModule,
    MatDividerModule,
    MatIconModule,
    MatCardModule,
    MatListModule,
  ],
})
export class CancelOutrightComponent implements OnInit, OnDestroy {
  public cancelForm: FormGroup;
  public showPreview = false;
  public isProcessing = false;
  public cancelErrorMessages: string[] = [];

  public corpId$: Observable<string | null>;
  private corpId: string | null = null;
  private readonly destroy$ = new Subject<void>();

  public constructor(
    private readonly fb: FormBuilder,
    private readonly dialogRef: MatDialogRef<
      CancelOutrightComponent,
      CancelResult
    >,
    private readonly snackBar: MatSnackBar,
    private readonly cancelService: CancelService,
    private readonly cdr: ChangeDetectorRef,
    private readonly store: Store,
    @Inject(MAT_DIALOG_DATA) public readonly data: MultiCancelDialogData,
  ) {
    this.cancelForm = this.createForm();
    this.corpId$ = this.store.select(fromUser.getCorpId);

    this.corpId$.pipe(takeUntil(this.destroy$)).subscribe((id) => {
      this.corpId = id;
    });
  }

  public ngOnInit(): void {
    this.setupFormValidation();
  }

  public static open(
    dialog: MatDialog,
    data: MultiCancelDialogData,
    config: Partial<MatDialogConfig<MultiCancelDialogData>> = {},
  ): MatDialogRef<CancelOutrightComponent, CancelResult> {
    const defaultConfig: MatDialogConfig<MultiCancelDialogData> = {
      data,
      panelClass: 'cancel-dialog-container',
      width: '500px',
      disableClose: true,
      autoFocus: false,
      restoreFocus: false,
    };

    return dialog.open<
      CancelOutrightComponent,
      MultiCancelDialogData,
      CancelResult
    >(CancelOutrightComponent, {
      ...defaultConfig,
      ...config,
    });
  }

  public ngOnDestroy(): void {
    this.destroy$.next();
    this.destroy$.complete();
  }

  public get cancellationReasons(): CancellationReason[] {
    const isBatchOperation = this.getTotalItemsCount() > 1;
    return getCancellationReasons(isBatchOperation);
  }

  public getCancelTypeDisplayName(): string {
    switch (this.data.cancelType) {
      case 'trades':
        return 'Trade';
      case 'executions':
        return 'Execution';
      case 'mixed':
        return 'Items';
      default:
        return 'Items';
    }
  }

  public getTotalItemsCount(): number {
    return (
      this.data.selectedTrades.length + this.data.selectedExecutions.length
    );
  }

  public togglePreview(): void {
    this.showPreview = !this.showPreview;
  }

  public canSubmit(): boolean {
    return this.cancelForm.valid && !this.isProcessing;
  }

  public trackTradeById(index: number, trade: TradeModel): string {
    return trade.entityId;
  }

  public trackExecutionById(index: number, execution: ExecutionModel): string {
    return execution.executionId;
  }

  public onCancel(): void {
    this.dialogRef.close();
  }

  // eslint-disable-next-line
  public async onConfirmCancel(): Promise<void> {
    if (!this.canSubmit()) return;

    if (!this.getCurrentUserCorpId()) {
      this.snackBar.open(
        'User identity is not available. Please re-login or contact support.',
        'Close',
        { duration: 7000, panelClass: 'error-snackbar' },
      );
      return;
    }

    this.isProcessing = true;
    this.cancelErrorMessages = [];

    try {
      const reason = this.getFinalReason();
      const cancelledItems: (TradeModel | ExecutionModel)[] = [];
      const failedItems: (TradeModel | ExecutionModel)[] = [];

      const allItems = [
        ...this.data.selectedTrades,
        ...this.data.selectedExecutions,
      ];

      for (const item of allItems) {
        let response: CancelReply | undefined = undefined;
        let error: unknown = undefined;

        try {
          if (this.isItemCancelled(item)) {
            failedItems.push(item);
            continue;
          }

          const cancelRequest = this.createCancelRequest(item, reason);
          const entityLevel = this.getEntityLevel(item);
          const userEnvDetails = this.createUserEnvDetails(item);
          const cancelUrl = this.getCancelUrl();

          response = (await this.cancelService
            .cancelEntity(cancelRequest, entityLevel, userEnvDetails, cancelUrl)
            .toPromise()) as CancelReply;
        } catch (err: unknown) {
          error = err;
        }
        let processed: ProcessCancelReplyResult | undefined;
        if (response) {
          processed = this.cancelService.processCancelReply(response);
        } else if (error && typeof error === 'object' && 'error' in error) {
          const errorReply = (error as { error?: CancelReply }).error;
          if (
            errorReply &&
            typeof errorReply === 'object' &&
            'transactionSuccessful' in errorReply
          ) {
            processed = this.cancelService.processCancelReply(
              errorReply as CancelReply,
            );
          } else {
            processed = undefined;
          }
        }

        if (processed && processed.modalType === 'SUCCESS') {
          cancelledItems.push(item);
        } else {
          failedItems.push(item);
          // eslint-disable-next-line
          if (processed?.cxlEdits?.length) {
            this.cancelErrorMessages.push(
              ...processed.cxlEdits.map((e) => e.tradingMessage),
            );
          } else {
            this.cancelErrorMessages.push(
              'Cancellation failed for unknown reason.',
            );
          }
          this.cdr.markForCheck();
        }
      }

      if (failedItems.length === 0) {
        this.showSuccessToast(cancelledItems.length);
        this.dialogRef.close({
          success: true,
          cancelledItems,
          failedItems: [],
          reason,
        });
      }
    } finally {
      this.isProcessing = false;
    }
  }

  private showSuccessToast(count: number): void {
    this.snackBar.open(`Successfully cancelled ${count} item(s)`, 'Close', {
      duration: 5000,
      panelClass: 'success-snackbar',
    });
  }

  private createForm(): FormGroup {
    return this.fb.group({
      reason: ['', Validators.required],
      customReason: [''],
    });
  }

  private setupFormValidation(): void {
    const reasonControl = this.cancelForm.get('reason');
    const customReasonControl = this.cancelForm.get('customReason');

    reasonControl?.valueChanges
      .pipe(takeUntil(this.destroy$))
      .subscribe((reason) => {
        if (reason === 'OTR') {
          customReasonControl?.setValidators([Validators.required]);
        } else {
          customReasonControl?.clearValidators();
        }
        customReasonControl?.updateValueAndValidity();
      });
  }

  private getFinalReason(): string {
    const { reason } = this.cancelForm.value as {
      reason: string;
      customReason: string;
    };
    return reason;
  }

  private isItemCancelled(item: TradeModel | ExecutionModel): boolean {
    const status = this.getItemStatus(item);
    return this.cancelService.isTradeCancelled(status);
  }

  private getItemStatus(item: TradeModel | ExecutionModel): string {
    if ('tradeStatus' in item) return item.tradeStatus || '';
    if ('executionStatusCode' in item) return item.executionStatusCode || '';
    return '';
  }

  private createCancelRequest(
    item: TradeModel | ExecutionModel,
    reason: string,
  ): XaEntityRequest {
    const { customReason } = this.cancelForm.value as {
      reason: string;
      customReason: string;
    };

    const request: XaEntityRequest = {
      requestId: this.generateRequestId(),
      reasonCode: reason,
      entity: {
        entityId: this.getEntityId(item),
        recordVersionNumber: this.getRecordVersion(item),
      },
    };

    if (reason === 'OTR' && customReason) {
      request.reasonText = customReason;
    }

    return request;
  }

  private getEntityLevel(item: TradeModel | ExecutionModel): string {
    return 'entityId' in item ? 'T' : 'E';
  }

  private createUserEnvDetails(
    item: TradeModel | ExecutionModel,
  ): UserEnvDetails {
    return {
      userCorpId: this.getCurrentUserCorpId() ?? '',
      entityType: this.getEntityLevel(item) === 'T' ? 'trade' : 'execution',
      mode: 'cancel',
    };
  }

  private getCancelUrl(): string {
    if (!this.data.cancelServiceUrl) {
      throw new Error('Cancel service URL is not set.');
    }
    return this.data.cancelServiceUrl;
  }

  private generateRequestId(): string {
    return `cancel-${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 9)}`;
  }

  private getRecordVersion(item: TradeModel | ExecutionModel): number {
    if (
      'recordVersionNumber' in item &&
      typeof item.recordVersionNumber === 'number'
    ) {
      return item.recordVersionNumber;
    }
    return 0;
  }

  private getCurrentUserCorpId(): string | null {
    return this.corpId;
  }

  private getEntityId(item: TradeModel | ExecutionModel): string {
    return 'entityId' in item
      ? item.entityId
      : (item as ExecutionModel).executionId;
  }
}

          <span class="history-title">Previous Note</span>
        </mat-card-title>
        <mat-card-content>
          {{ currentNote }}
        </mat-card-content>
      </mat-card>
    }
  </div>
  <div class="td-actions">
    <button mat-stroked-button (click)="onCancel()" [disabled]="isProcessing">
      Close
    </button>
    <button
      mat-flat-button
      (click)="onSubmit()"
      [disabled]="noteForm.invalid || isProcessing"
      class="confirm"
    >

    </button>
  </div>
}

describe('UpdateTraderNoteComponent', () => {
  let component: UpdateTraderNoteComponent;
  let fixture: ComponentFixture<UpdateTraderNoteComponent>;

  class MockDialogRef {
    close = jest.fn();
  }
  class MockSnackBar {
    open = jest.fn();
  }
  class MockChangeService {}
  class MockChangeDetectorRef {
    markForCheck = jest.fn();
  }
  class MockStore {
    select = jest
      .fn()
      .mockReturnValue({ pipe: () => ({ subscribe: () => {} }) });
  }

  beforeEach(async () => {
    await TestBed.configureTestingModule({
      imports: [
        UpdateTraderNoteComponent,
        ReactiveFormsModule,
        NoopAnimationsModule,
      ],

        { provide: ChangeDetectorRef, useClass: MockChangeDetectorRef },

    }).compileComponents();

    fixture = TestBed.createComponent(UpdateTraderNoteComponent);
    component = fixture.componentInstance;
    fixture.detectChanges();
  });

  it('should create', () => {
    expect(component).toBeTruthy();
  });

  it('should close dialog with success: false on cancel', () => {
    component.onCancel();
    const dialogRef = TestBed.inject(MatDialogRef);
    expect(dialogRef.close).toHaveBeenCalledWith({ success: false });
  });

    component.data.executions = [mockExecution, mockExecution, mockExecution];
    expect(component.executionCount).toBe(3);
  });

  it('should return true for isSingleExecution when one execution', () => {
    component.data.executions = [mockExecution];
    expect(component.isSingleExecution).toBe(true);
  });

  it('should return false for isSingleExecution when multiple executions', () => {
    component.data.executions = [mockExecution, mockExecution];
    expect(component.isSingleExecution).toBe(false);
  });

  it('should patch reasonCode on ngOnInit', () => {
    component.data.executions = [mockExecution];
    component.isProcessing = false;
    component.ngOnInit();
    expect(component.noteForm.get('reasonCode')?.value).toBeDefined();
  });

  it('should disable traderNote control if isProcessing is true on ngOnInit', () => {
    component.isProcessing = true;
    component.ngOnInit();
    expect(component.noteForm.get('traderNote')?.disabled).toBe(true);
  });

  it('should complete destroy$ on ngOnDestroy', () => {
    const spyNext = jest.spyOn((component as any).destroy$, 'next');
    const spyComplete = jest.spyOn((component as any).destroy$, 'complete');
    component.ngOnDestroy();
    expect(spyNext).toHaveBeenCalled();
    expect(spyComplete).toHaveBeenCalled();
  });

  it('should create a form with reasonCode and traderNote controls', () => {
    const form = (component as any).createForm();
    expect(form.contains('reasonCode')).toBe(true);
    expect(form.contains('traderNote')).toBe(true);
  });

  it('should not proceed onSubmit if form is invalid', async () => {
    // Arrange
    component.noteForm.get('reasonCode')?.setValue('');
    component.noteForm.get('traderNote')?.setValue('');
    const spySingle = jest.spyOn(component as any, 'updateSingleExecution');
    const spyMultiple = jest.spyOn(
      component as any,
      'updateMultipleExecutions',
    );

    // Act
    await component.onSubmit();

    // Assert
    expect(spySingle).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
    expect(spyMultiple).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
    expect(component.isProcessing).toBe(false);
  });

  it('should call updateSingleExecution and handleSingleResponse for single execution onSubmit', async () => {
    // Arrange
    component.data.executions = [mockExecution];
    component.noteForm.get('reasonCode')?.setValue('reason');
    component.noteForm.get('traderNote')?.setValue('note');
    jest.spyOn(component, 'isSingleExecution', 'get').mockReturnValue(true);
    const spyUpdate = jest
      .spyOn(component as any, 'updateSingleExecution')
      .mockResolvedValue('response' as any);
    const spyHandle = jest
      .spyOn(component as any, 'handleSingleResponse')
      .mockImplementation();

    // Act
    await component.onSubmit();

    // Assert
    expect(spyUpdate).toHaveBeenCalledWith(mockExecution, 'note', 'reason');
    expect(spyHandle).toHaveBeenCalledWith('response');
  });

  it('should call updateMultipleExecutions and handleBatchResponse for multiple executions onSubmit', async () => {
    // Arrange

    component.noteForm.get('reasonCode')?.setValue('reason');
    component.noteForm.get('traderNote')?.setValue('note');
    jest.spyOn(component, 'isSingleExecution', 'get').mockReturnValue(false);
    const spyUpdate = jest
      .spyOn(component as any, 'updateMultipleExecutions')
      .mockResolvedValue('response' as any);
    const spyHandle = jest
      .spyOn(component as any, 'handleBatchResponse')
      .mockImplementation();

      'note',
      'reason',
    );
    expect(spyHandle).toHaveBeenCalledWith('response');
  });

  it('should call handleError if updateSingleExecution throws in onSubmit', async () => {
    // Arrange
    component.data.executions = [mockExecution];
    component.noteForm.get('reasonCode')?.setValue('reason');
    component.noteForm.get('traderNote')?.setValue('note');

    jest
      .spyOn(component as any, 'updateSingleExecution')

    await component.onSubmit();

  it('should call handleError if updateMultipleExecutions throws in onSubmit', async () => {

      cxlEdits: [{ tradingMessage: 'msg1' }, { tradingMessage: 'msg2' }],

      'markForCheck',
    );

    // Act
    (component as any).handleSingleResponse(response);

    // Assert

    const processed = { cxlEdits: [] };
    const mockChangeService = TestBed.inject(ChangeService) as any;
    mockChangeService.processChangeReply = jest.fn().mockReturnValue(processed);
    const spyMarkForCheck = jest.spyOn(
      (component as any)['cdr'],
      'markForCheck',
    );

    // Act
    (component as any).handleSingleResponse(response);

    // Assert

    expect(spyMarkForCheck).toHaveBeenCalled();
  });

  it('should handle single response: no edits, unknown error', () => {
    // Arrange
    const response = { transactionSuccessful: false } as any;
    const processed = { cxlEdits: [] };
    const mockChangeService = TestBed.inject(ChangeService) as any;
    mockChangeService.processChangeReply = jest.fn().mockReturnValue(processed);
    const spyMarkForCheck = jest.spyOn(
      (component as any)['cdr'],
      'markForCheck',
    );

    // Act
    (component as any).handleSingleResponse(response);

    // Assert
    expect(component.errorMessages).toEqual([ERROR_UPDATE_FAILED_UNKNOWN]);
    expect(spyMarkForCheck).toHaveBeenCalled();
  });

  it('should handle batch response: all success', () => {
    // Arrange
    jest.clearAllMocks();
    const response = [{}, {}] as any;
    const summary = { successCount: 2, failureCount: 0, allEdits: [] };
    const mockChangeService = TestBed.inject(ChangeService) as any;
    mockChangeService.processBatchChangeReplies = jest
      .fn()
      .mockImplementation((resp: any) => {
        if (Array.isArray(resp) && resp.length === summary.successCount) {
          return summary;
        }
        return { successCount: 0, failureCount: resp.length, allEdits: [] };
      });
    const snackBar = TestBed.inject(MatSnackBar);
    const dialogRef = TestBed.inject(MatDialogRef);
    (component as any).snackBar = snackBar;
    (component as any).dialogRef = dialogRef;

    // Act
    (component as any).handleBatchResponse(response);

    // Assert
    expect(snackBar.open).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
      SUCCESS_UPDATE_BATCH(2),
      SNACKBAR_CLOSE,
      { duration: DEFAULT_MODAL_DURATION },
    );
    expect(dialogRef.close).toHaveBeenCalledWith({
      success: true,
      updatedCount: 2,
    });
  });

  it('should handle batch response: partial success', () => {
    // Arrange
    jest.clearAllMocks();
    const response = [{}, {}, {}] as any;
    const summary = {
      successCount: 2,
      failureCount: 1,
      allEdits: [{ tradingMessage: 'fail1' }, { tradingMessage: 'fail2' }],
    };
    const mockChangeService = TestBed.inject(ChangeService) as any;
    mockChangeService.processBatchChangeReplies = jest
      .fn()
      .mockReturnValue(summary);
    const snackBar = TestBed.inject(MatSnackBar);
    const dialogRef = TestBed.inject(MatDialogRef);
    (component as any).snackBar = snackBar;
    (component as any).dialogRef = dialogRef;
    const spyMarkForCheck = jest.spyOn(
      (component as any)['cdr'],
      'markForCheck',
    );

    // Act
    (component as any).handleBatchResponse(response);

    // Assert
    expect(component.errorMessages).toEqual(['fail1', 'fail2']);
    expect(spyMarkForCheck).toHaveBeenCalled();
    expect(snackBar.open).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
    expect(dialogRef.close).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
  });

  it('should handle single response: all success', () => {
    // Arrange
    jest.clearAllMocks();
    const response = { transactionSuccessful: true } as any;
    const processed = { cxlEdits: [] };
    const mockChangeService = TestBed.inject(ChangeService) as any;
    mockChangeService.processChangeReply = jest.fn().mockReturnValue(processed);
    const snackBar = TestBed.inject(MatSnackBar);
    const dialogRef = TestBed.inject(MatDialogRef);
    (component as any).snackBar = snackBar;
    (component as any).dialogRef = dialogRef;

    // Act
    (component as any).handleSingleResponse(response);

      SNACKBAR_CLOSE,
      { duration: DEFAULT_MODAL_DURATION },
    );

      success: true,
      updatedCount: 1,
    });
  });

  it('should handle batch response: partial success', () => {
    // Arrange
    jest.clearAllMocks();
    const response = [{}, {}, {}] as any;
    const summary = {
      successCount: 2,
      failureCount: 1,
      allEdits: [{ tradingMessage: 'fail1' }, { tradingMessage: 'fail2' }],
    };
    const mockChangeService = TestBed.inject(ChangeService) as any;
    mockChangeService.processBatchChangeReplies = jest

      .mockReturnValue(summary);

    const dialogRef = TestBed.inject(MatDialogRef);
    (component as any).snackBar = snackBar;
    (component as any).dialogRef = dialogRef;

    // Act
    (component as any).handleBatchResponse(response);

    // Assert
    expect(component.errorMessages).toEqual(['fail1', 'fail2']);
    expect(spyMarkForCheck).toHaveBeenCalled();
    expect(snackBar.open).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
    expect(dialogRef.close).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
  });

  describe('getChangeUrl', () => {
    it('should return correct url when changeServiceUrl is provided', () => {
      // Arrange
      (component as any).data.changeServiceUrl = 'mock-url/%TYPE%/cancel';
      // Act
      const url = (component as any).getChangeUrl();
      // Assert
      expect(url).toBe('mock-url/executions');
    });

    it('should throw error when changeServiceUrl is missing', () => {
      // Arrange
      (component as any).data.changeServiceUrl = undefined;
      // Act & Assert
      expect(() => (component as any).getChangeUrl()).toThrow(
        ERROR_CHANGE_SERVICE_URL_REQUIRED,
      );
    });
  });
  describe('buildChangeRequest', () => {
    it('should build a valid ChangeRequest', () => {
      const execution = {
        executionId: 'id1',
        recordVersionNumber: 2,
      } as any;
      const traderNote = 'note';
      const reasonCode = 'reason';
      (component as any).corpId = 'CORP';

      const result = (component as any).buildChangeRequest(
        execution,
        traderNote,
        reasonCode,
      );

      expect(result).toEqual({
        entity: {
          entityId: 'id1',
          recordVersionNumber: 2,
        },
        adjustableData: {
          traderNote: 'note',
        },
        reasonCode: 'reason',
        corpID: 'CORP',
        originatingSystemCode: 'EXAC',
      });
    });

    it('should include parentDesk FMREQ for BOS trading desk', () => {
      const execution = {
        executionId: 'id1',
        recordVersionNumber: 2,
        tradingDesk: 'BOS',
      } as any;
      (component as any).corpId = 'CORP';

      const result = (component as any).buildChangeRequest(
        execution,
        'note',
        'reason',
      );

      expect(result.parentDesk).toBe('FMREQ');
    });

    it('should include parentDesk FMREQ for FMRLON trading desk', () => {
      const execution = {
        executionId: 'id1',
        recordVersionNumber: 2,
        tradingDesk: 'FMRLON',
      } as any;
      (component as any).corpId = 'CORP';

      const result = (component as any).buildChangeRequest(
        execution,
        'note',
        'reason',
      );

      expect(result.parentDesk).toBe('FMREQ');
    });

    it('should include parentDesk FMREQ for FMRHK trading desk', () => {
      const execution = {
        executionId: 'id1',
        recordVersionNumber: 2,
        tradingDesk: 'FMRHK',
      } as any;
      (component as any).corpId = 'CORP';

      const result = (component as any).buildChangeRequest(
        execution,
        'note',
        'reason',
      );

      expect(result.parentDesk).toBe('FMREQ');
    });

    it('should include parentDesk FMRHI for BHI trading desk', () => {
      const execution = {
        executionId: 'id1',
        recordVersionNumber: 2,
        tradingDesk: 'BHI',
      } as any;
      (component as any).corpId = 'CORP';

      const result = (component as any).buildChangeRequest(
        execution,
        'note',
        'reason',
      );

      expect(result.parentDesk).toBe('FMRHI');
    });

    it('should not include parentDesk for unmapped trading desk', () => {
      const execution = {
        executionId: 'id1',
        recordVersionNumber: 2,
        tradingDesk: 'OTHER',
      } as any;
      (component as any).corpId = 'CORP';

      const result = (component as any).buildChangeRequest(
        execution,
        'note',
        'reason',
      );

      expect(result.parentDesk).toBeUndefined();
    });

    it('should throw error if executionId is empty', () => {
      const execution = {
        executionId: '',
        recordVersionNumber: 2,
      } as any;

      expect(() =>
        (component as any).buildChangeRequest(execution, 'note', 'reason'),
      ).toThrow(ERROR_EXECUTION_ID_REQUIRED);
    });

    it('should throw error if recordVersionNumber is missing', () => {
      const execution = {
        executionId: 'id1',
        recordVersionNumber: null,
      } as any;

      expect(() =>
        (component as any).buildChangeRequest(execution, 'note', 'reason'),
      ).toThrow(ERROR_RECORD_VERSION_MISSING('id1'));
    });
  });
});

  SINGLE_UPDATE_FAILED,
  MAX_TRADER_NOTE_LENGTH,
  BATCH_UPDATE_FAILED,
} from './constants/default.constant';

@Component({
  // eslint-disable-next-line @angular-eslint/component-selector
  selector: 'exac-ui-update-trader-note-dialog',
  templateUrl: './update-trader-note.component.html',
  styleUrls: ['./update-trader-note.component.scss'],
  changeDetection: ChangeDetectionStrategy.OnPush,
  imports: [
    ReactiveFormsModule,
    MatDialogModule,
    MatSnackBarModule,
    MatFormFieldModule,
    MatSelectModule,
    MatInputModule,
    MatButtonModule,
    MatDividerModule,
    MatIconModule,
    MatCardModule,
    MatListModule,
  ],
})
export class UpdateTraderNoteComponent implements OnInit, OnDestroy {
  public noteForm: FormGroup;
  public isProcessing = false;
  public errorMessages: string[] = [];
  public currentNote: string | null = null;
  public readonly MAX_TRADER_NOTE_LENGTH = MAX_TRADER_NOTE_LENGTH;
  private readonly traderNoteWhitespaceValidator = (
    control: AbstractControl,
  ): ValidationErrors | null => {
    const value = control.value as string;
    if (value.trim().length === 0) {
      return { whitespace: true };
    }
    return null;
  };

  public corpId$: Observable<string | null>;
  private corpId: string | null = null;
  private readonly destroy$ = new Subject<void>();
  private readonly changeUrl: string;

  public constructor(
    private readonly fb: FormBuilder,
    private readonly dialogRef: MatDialogRef<
      UpdateTraderNoteComponent,
      UpdateTraderNoteResult
    >,
    private readonly changeService: ChangeService,
    private readonly snackBar: MatSnackBar,
    private readonly cdr: ChangeDetectorRef,
    private readonly store: Store,
    @Inject(MAT_DIALOG_DATA) public readonly data: UpdateTraderNoteDialogData,
  ) {
    this.noteForm = this.createForm();
    this.updateTraderNoteControlState();
    this.corpId$ = this.store.select(fromUser.getCorpId);

    this.corpId$.pipe(takeUntil(this.destroy$)).subscribe((id) => {
      this.corpId = id;
    });

    this.changeUrl = this.getChangeUrl();
  }

  public ngOnInit(): void {
    if (this.data.executions.length === 1) {
      const existingNote = this.data.executions[0].traderNote;
      if (existingNote) {
        this.currentNote = existingNote;
      }
    }
    this.noteForm.patchValue({ reasonCode: DEFAULT_REASON_CODE });
    this.updateTraderNoteControlState();
  }

  public ngOnDestroy(): void {
    this.destroy$.next();
    this.destroy$.complete();
  }

  private createForm(): FormGroup {
    return this.fb.group({
      reasonCode: ['', Validators.required],
      traderNote: [
        '',
        [
          Validators.required,
          Validators.maxLength(MAX_TRADER_NOTE_LENGTH),
          this.traderNoteWhitespaceValidator,
        ],
      ],
    });
  }

  public get executionCount(): number {
    return this.data.executions.length;
  }

  public get isSingleExecution(): boolean {
    return this.executionCount === 1;
  }

  public onCancel(): void {
    this.dialogRef.close({ success: false });
  }

  public async onSubmit(): Promise<void> {
    if (this.noteForm.invalid) {
      return;
    }

    this.isProcessing = true;
    this.errorMessages = [];
    this.cdr.markForCheck();

    const { traderNote, reasonCode } = this.noteForm.value as {
      traderNote?: string;
      reasonCode: string;
    };
    const safeTraderNote = traderNote?.trim() || '';

    try {
      let response: ChangeReply | ChangeReply[];

      if (this.isSingleExecution) {
        response = await this.updateSingleExecution(
          this.data.executions[0],
          safeTraderNote,
          reasonCode,
        );
        this.handleSingleResponse(response);
      } else {
        response = await this.updateMultipleExecutions(
          this.data.executions,
          safeTraderNote,
          reasonCode,
        );
        this.handleBatchResponse(response);
      }
    } catch (error) {
      this.handleError(error);
    } finally {
      this.isProcessing = false;
      this.cdr.markForCheck();
    }
  }

  private handleBatchResponse(response: ChangeReply[]): void {
    const summary = this.changeService.processBatchChangeReplies(response);
    if (summary.successCount > 0 && summary.failureCount === 0) {
      this.snackBar.open(
        SUCCESS_UPDATE_BATCH(summary.successCount),
        SNACKBAR_CLOSE,
        { duration: DEFAULT_MODAL_DURATION },
      );
      this.dialogRef.close({
        success: true,
        updatedCount: summary.successCount,
      });
    } else if (summary.successCount > 0 && summary.failureCount > 0) {
      this.errorMessages = summary.allEdits.length
        ? summary.allEdits.map((e) => e.tradingMessage)
        : [ERROR_SOME_UPDATES_FAILED];
      this.cdr.markForCheck();
    } else if (summary.failureCount > 0) {
      this.errorMessages = summary.allEdits.length
        ? summary.allEdits.map((e) => e.tradingMessage)
        : [ERROR_ALL_UPDATES_FAILED];
      this.cdr.markForCheck();
    }
  }

  private handleSingleResponse(response: ChangeReply): void {
    const processed = this.changeService.processChangeReply(response);
    if (response.transactionSuccessful === true) {
      this.snackBar.open(SUCCESS_UPDATE_SINGLE, SNACKBAR_CLOSE, {
        duration: DEFAULT_MODAL_DURATION,
      });
      this.dialogRef.close({ success: true, updatedCount: 1 });
    } else if (processed.cxlEdits.length) {
      this.errorMessages = processed.cxlEdits.map((e) => e.tradingMessage);
      this.cdr.markForCheck();
    } else if (response.editMessages?.length) {
      this.errorMessages = response.editMessages.map((e) => e.tradingMessage);
      this.cdr.markForCheck();
    } else {
      this.errorMessages = [ERROR_UPDATE_FAILED_UNKNOWN];
      this.cdr.markForCheck();
    }
  }

  private handleError(error: unknown): void {
    const errorMsg = this.changeService.processChangeReplyError(
      error as { status?: number },
    );
    this.errorMessages = [errorMsg];
    this.cdr.markForCheck();
  }

  private async updateSingleExecution(
    execution: ExecutionModel,
    traderNote: string,
    reasonCode: string,
  ): Promise<ChangeReply> {
    if (!execution.executionId || execution.executionId.trim() === '') {
      throw new Error(ERROR_EXECUTION_ID_REQUIRED);
    }

    const request = this.buildChangeRequest(execution, traderNote, reasonCode);

    try {
      return (await this.changeService
        .changeExecution(request, execution.executionId, this.changeUrl)
        .toPromise()) as ChangeReply;
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error(
        SINGLE_UPDATE_FAILED(
          error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
        ),
      );
    }
  }

  private async updateMultipleExecutions(
    executions: ExecutionModel[],
    traderNote: string,
    reasonCode: string,
  ): Promise<ChangeReply[]> {
    if (executions.length === 0) {
      throw new Error(ERROR_NO_EXECUTIONS_BATCH);
    }

    const requests = executions.map((execution) =>
      this.buildChangeRequest(execution, traderNote, reasonCode),
    );

    try {
      return (await this.changeService
        .batchChangeExecutions(requests, this.changeUrl)
        .toPromise()) as ChangeReply[];
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error(
        BATCH_UPDATE_FAILED(
          error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
        ),
      );
    }
  }

  private buildChangeRequest(
    execution: ExecutionModel,
    traderNote: string,
    reasonCode: string,
  ): ChangeRequest {
    if (execution.executionId.trim() === '') {
      throw new Error(ERROR_EXECUTION_ID_REQUIRED);
    }

    if (execution.recordVersionNumber == null) {
      throw new Error(ERROR_RECORD_VERSION_MISSING(execution.executionId));
    }

    const parentDesk = ParentDeskMapper.getParentDesk(execution.tradingDesk);

    const changeRequest: ChangeRequest = {
      entity: {
        entityId: execution.executionId,
        recordVersionNumber: execution.recordVersionNumber,
      },
      adjustableData: {
        traderNote: traderNote,
      },
      reasonCode: reasonCode,
      corpID: this.corpId || 'UNKNOWN',
      originatingSystemCode: 'EXAC',
      ...(parentDesk && { parentDesk }),
    };
    return changeRequest;
  }

  public processBatchChangeReplies(
    changeReplies: ChangeReply[],
  ): BatchChangeReplySummary {
    return this.changeService.processBatchChangeReplies(changeReplies);
  }

  private updateTraderNoteControlState(): void {
    const traderNoteControl = this.noteForm.get('traderNote');
    if (!traderNoteControl) {
      return;
    }

    if (this.isProcessing) {
      traderNoteControl.disable();
    } else {
      traderNoteControl.enable();
    }
  }

  private getChangeUrl(): string {
    if (this.data.changeServiceUrl) {
      let url = this.data.changeServiceUrl.replace('%TYPE%', 'executions');
      url = url.replace(/\/(cancel|executions)$/, '');
      return url;
    }
    throw new Error(ERROR_CHANGE_SERVICE_URL_REQUIRED);
  }
}

export const DEFAULT_REASON_CODE = 'TDR';
export const DEFAULT_MODAL_DURATION = 5000;

export const MAX_TRADER_NOTE_LENGTH = 500;

export const SUCCESS_UPDATE_SINGLE =
  'Successfully updated trader note for 1 execution';
export const SUCCESS_UPDATE_BATCH = (count: number): string =>
  `Successfully updated trader notes for ${count} execution(s)`;
export const ERROR_EXECUTION_ID_REQUIRED = 'Execution ID is required';
export const ERROR_NO_EXECUTIONS_BATCH =
  'No executions provided for batch update.';
export const ERROR_UPDATE_FAILED_UNKNOWN = 'Update failed for unknown reason.';
export const ERROR_ALL_UPDATES_FAILED = 'All updates failed.';
export const ERROR_SOME_UPDATES_FAILED = 'Some updates failed.';
export const ERROR_RECORD_VERSION_MISSING = (id: string): string =>
  `Record version number is missing for execution ${id}. Please refresh the grid to get the latest execution data.`;
export const ERROR_CHANGE_SERVICE_URL_REQUIRED =
  'Change service URL (changeServiceUrl) is required but was not provided in dialog data. Please ensure the calling component supplies the correct endpoint from IConfig.';
export const SNACKBAR_CLOSE = 'Close';

export const SINGLE_UPDATE_FAILED = (errorMsg: string): string =>
  `Single update failed: ${errorMsg}`;
export const BATCH_UPDATE_FAILED = (errorMsg: string): string =>
  `Batch update failed: ${errorMsg}`;

import { ComponentFixture, TestBed } from '@angular/core/testing';

import { ExacShellComponent } from './exac-shell.component';
import { StoreModule } from '@ngrx/store';
import { RouterTestingModule } from '@angular/router/testing';
import { MockStore, provideMockStore } from '@ngrx/store/testing';
import { LoggerUtil } from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/util/common';
import { RuntimeConfigExt } from '@fmr-pr000539/eqt-ames-conf-preset';
import { CUSTOM_ELEMENTS_SCHEMA } from '@angular/core';
import { Title } from '@angular/platform-browser';
import { ActivatedRoute, convertToParamMap } from '@angular/router';

describe('TracShellComponent', () => {
  let component: ExacShellComponent;
  let store: MockStore;
  let fixture: ComponentFixture<ExacShellComponent>;
  let titleService: Title;

  function setupWithQuery(queryParams?: any) {
    TestBed.configureTestingModule({
      imports: [RouterTestingModule, StoreModule.forRoot({})],
      declarations: [ExacShellComponent],
      providers: [
        RuntimeConfigExt,
        LoggerUtil,
        provideMockStore(),
        {
          provide: ActivatedRoute,
          useValue: {
            snapshot: {
              queryParamMap: convertToParamMap(queryParams),
            },
          },
        },
      ],
      schemas: [CUSTOM_ELEMENTS_SCHEMA],
      teardown: { destroyAfterEach: false },
    }).compileComponents();

    fixture = TestBed.createComponent(ExacShellComponent);
    component = fixture.componentInstance;
    titleService = TestBed.inject(Title);
    store = TestBed.inject(MockStore);
    fixture.detectChanges();
  }

  it('should create', () => {
    setupWithQuery();
    expect(component).toBeTruthy();
  });

  it('should create component', () => {
    setupWithQuery();
    expect(component).toBeTruthy();
  });

  it('should render Access Denied page', () => {
    setupWithQuery();
    const fixture = TestBed.createComponent(ExacShellComponent);
    fixture.detectChanges();
    const compiled = fixture.nativeElement as HTMLElement;
    expect(compiled.querySelector('h1')?.textContent).toContain(
      'Access Denied',
    );
  });

  it(`should have as title 'Fund Executions - vx.x.x when Funds context'`, () => {
    setupWithQuery();
    //Arrange
    const settings = require('../../../../../../../package.json');

    //Act
    component.ngOnInit();

    //Assert
    expect(titleService.getTitle()).toEqual(
      `Fund Executions - v${settings.version}`,
    );
  });

  it(`should have as title 'Block Executions - vx.x.x when Block context is present in the query param "grid-view=executions"'`, () => {
    //Arrange
    setupWithQuery({ 'grid-view': 'executions' });
    const settings = require('../../../../../../../package.json');

    //Act
    component.ngOnInit();

    //Assert
    expect(titleService.getTitle()).toEqual(
      `Block Executions - v${settings.version}`,
    );
  });
});

File: shell-view\feature\src\lib\exac-shell\exac-shell.component.ts
import { Observable, Subject } from 'rxjs';
import { takeUntil } from 'rxjs/operators';
import { Component, OnDestroy, OnInit } from '@angular/core';
import * as fromUser from '@fmr-pr000539/eqt-ngrx-user-module';
import { requestAuthorizedFunctions } from '@fmr-pr000539/eqt-ngrx-user-module';
import { ArrowAuthDetails } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';
import { select, Store } from '@ngrx/store';
import { isAuthorizedToView } from './selectors/exac-shell.selectors';
import { LoggerUtil } from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/util/common';
import { Title } from '@angular/platform-browser';
import { ActivatedRoute } from '@angular/router';
import { getCancelAndAdjustServiceUrl } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/trades-search/data-access';

@Component({
  selector: 'exac-shell',
  templateUrl: './exac-shell.component.html',
  styleUrls: ['./exac-shell.component.scss'],
  standalone: false,
})
export class ExacShellComponent implements OnInit, OnDestroy {
  public isAuthorizedToView$: Observable<boolean>;
  public isArrowLoading$: Observable<boolean>;
  // Get cancel and adjust service URL from the same configuration as app 113173
  public cancelAndAdjustServiceUrl$ = this.store.pipe(
    select(getCancelAndAdjustServiceUrl),
  );
  public cancelAndAdjustServiceUrl = '';
  private readonly destroy$ = new Subject<void>();

  public constructor(
    private readonly store: Store<any>,
    private readonly titleService: Title,
    private readonly logger: LoggerUtil,
    private readonly route: ActivatedRoute,
  ) {
    this.isArrowLoading$ = store.pipe(select(fromUser.getIsArrowLoading));
    this.isAuthorizedToView$ = store.pipe(
      select(isAuthorizedToView),
    ) as Observable<boolean>;
  }

  public ngOnInit(): void {
    const isExecutionsGridContext =
      this.route.snapshot.queryParamMap.get('grid-view') === 'executions';
    this.setTitle(
      isExecutionsGridContext ? 'Block Executions' : 'Fund Executions',
    );

    this.store.dispatch(
      requestAuthorizedFunctions({
        authorizedApplication: ArrowAuthDetails.AppName as string,
        callerName: 'Execution Activity',
      }),
    );

    // Subscribe to cancel service URL from configuration (same as app 113173)
    this.cancelAndAdjustServiceUrl$
      .pipe(takeUntil(this.destroy$))
      .subscribe((url: string) => {
        if (url) {
          this.cancelAndAdjustServiceUrl = url;
          this.logger.logInfo(
            `Using cancel and adjust service URL from config: ${url}`,
          );
        }
      });
  }

  public ngOnDestroy(): void {
    this.destroy$.next();
    this.destroy$.complete();
  }

  private setTitle(defaultTitle: string): void {
    // prettier-ignore
    // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unsafe-member-access,@typescript-eslint/no-unsafe-assignment,@typescript-eslint/no-var-requires,@typescript-eslint/no-unsafe-call
    const appVersion: string = require('../../../../../../../package.json').version;
    this.logger.logInfo(`AppVersion=${appVersion}`);
    this.titleService.setTitle(`${defaultTitle} - v${appVersion}`);
  }
}

File: shell-view\feature\src\lib\exac-shell\selectors\exac-shell.selectors.spec.ts
import { exacShellSelectors } from './exac-shell.selectors';

describe('tracShellSelectors', () => {
  describe('checkAuthorizationSelectors', () => {
    //Arrange
    let mockState = {};

    it('should return FALSE as arrow is still loading', () => {
      // Act
      const result = exacShellSelectors.isAuthorizedToView.projector(
        mockState as any,
        true,
      );

      // Assert
      expect(result).toEqual(false);
    });

    it('should return FALSE as arrow auth roles are undefined', () => {
      // Act
      const result = exacShellSelectors.isAuthorizedToView.projector(
        mockState as any,
        false,
      );

      // Assert
      expect(result).toBeFalsy();
    });

    it('should return TRUE as arrow auth roles are present in the store', () => {
      //Arrange
      mockState = {
        InsightOMS: {
          ViewOrders: true,
        },
      };

      // Act
      const result = exacShellSelectors.isAuthorizedToView.projector(
        mockState as any,
        false,
      );

      // Assert
      expect(result).toBeTruthy();
    });
  });
});

File: shell-view\feature\src\lib\exac-shell\selectors\exac-shell.selectors.ts
import { createSelector, MemoizedSelector } from '@ngrx/store';
import { ArrowAuthDetails } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';
import * as fromUser from '@fmr-pr000539/eqt-ngrx-user-module';
import { isUndefined } from 'lodash';

export const isAuthorizedToView = getAuthRoles(
  ArrowAuthDetails.AppName as string,
  ArrowAuthDetails.ViewOrdersRole as string,
);

function getAuthRoles(
  arrowApp: string,
  arrowFunction: string,
): MemoizedSelector<any, any> {
  return createSelector(
    fromUser.getArrowState,
    fromUser.getIsArrowLoading,
    (arrowState, isArrowLoading) => {
      if (isArrowLoading) {
        return false;
      }
      const authRoles = arrowState[arrowApp];

      return !isUndefined(authRoles) && authRoles[arrowFunction];
    },
  );
}

export const exacShellSelectors = {
  isAuthorizedToView,
};

File: trades-grid\data\README.md
# exac-trades-grid-data

This library was generated with [Nx](https://nx.dev).

## Running unit tests

Run `nx test exac-trades-grid-data` to execute the unit tests.

## CI/CD process

Each branch created will have it's
own [CI pipeline](https://itec-jenkins.fmr.com/cm202/job/FIMT/job/PL201940/job/PR000539/job/EQT-Ng-Monorepo/job/pr000539-eqt-ng-monorepo-ci/) on
jenkins. Kick off the job in the branch interested in with following parameters:

- VERSION_TYPE = patch
- NODE_VERSION = 16.17.0
- PROTOTYPE_BUILD = checked if we want to trigger CD after
- PROTOTYPE_BUILD_ENV = SIT to deploy to SIT as trade activity is currently working on SIT

If [CD pipeline](https://itec-jenkins.fmr.com/cm202/job/FIMT/job/PL201940/job/PR000539/job/EQT-Ng-Monorepo/job/pr000539-eqt-ng-monorepo-cd-prototype-single-env/)
fails we can kick off manually:

- cloudArtifact = /@fmr-ap160539/exac-activity-cloud-pipeline/-/exac-activity-cloud-pipeline-[version].tgz
- deploymentType = auto
- operations = delete, delete-all, generate-certificate, deploy

import { NgModule } from '@angular/core';
import { CommonModule } from '@angular/common';
import { StoreModule } from '@ngrx/store';
import { TradesGridStoreConstants } from './constants/trades-grid.constants';
import * as tradesGridReducer from './store-trades/trades-grid.reducer';
import * as executionsGridReducers from './store-executions/executions-grid.reducer';
import { EffectsModule } from '@ngrx/effects';
import { TradesGridEffects } from './store-trades/trades-grid.effects';
import { TradeActivityService } from './services/trade-activity.service';
import { ExecutionsGridEffects } from './store-executions/executions-grid.effects';
import { ExecutionsGridStoreConstants } from './constants/executions-grid.constants';

@NgModule({
  imports: [
    CommonModule,
    StoreModule.forFeature(
      TradesGridStoreConstants.FeatureKey,
      tradesGridReducer.tradesReducer,
    ),
    StoreModule.forFeature(
      ExecutionsGridStoreConstants.FeatureKey,
      executionsGridReducers.executionsReducer,
    ),
    EffectsModule.forFeature([TradesGridEffects, ExecutionsGridEffects]),
  ],
  providers: [TradeActivityService],
})
export class ExacTradesGridDataAccessModule {}

File: trades-grid\data-access\src\lib\model\grid-store.model.ts
/*
 * Copyright (c) 2025 FMR Corp.
 * All Rights Reserved.
 *
 * Fidelity Confidential Information.
 * Created on May 26, 2025
 */

import {
  createEntityAdapter,
  EntityAdapter,
  EntityState,
  IdSelector,
} from '@ngrx/entity';

export interface BaseGridState<T> extends EntityState<T> {
  selectedId?: string | number;
  loaded: boolean;
  isLoadingData: boolean;
  error?: string | null;
}

export function createGridEntityAdapter<T>(
  selectedIdFn: IdSelector<T>,
): EntityAdapter<T> {
  return createEntityAdapter<T>({ selectId: selectedIdFn });
}

/*

import { TestBed } from '@angular/core/testing';
import { TradeActivityService } from './trade-activity.service';
import { HttpClient } from '@angular/common/http';
import { LoggerUtil } from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/util/common';
import { Store } from '@ngrx/store';
import { of, Subject } from 'rxjs';

jest.mock('@fmr-pr000539/shared/util/ag-grid', () => ({
  setAgGridLicence: jest.fn(),
}));

describe('TradeActivityService', () => {
  let service: TradeActivityService;
  let httpClientMock: jest.Mocked<HttpClient>;
  let loggerMock: jest.Mocked<LoggerUtil>;
  let storeMock: jest.Mocked<Store>;
  let serviceUrlSubject: Subject<string>;

  beforeEach(() => {
    httpClientMock = {
      post: jest.fn(),
      get: jest.fn(),
    } as any;

    loggerMock = {
      logInfo: jest.fn(),
    } as any;

    serviceUrlSubject = new Subject<string>();

    storeMock = {
      pipe: jest.fn().mockReturnValue(serviceUrlSubject.asObservable()),
    } as any;

    TestBed.configureTestingModule({
      providers: [
        TradeActivityService,
        { provide: HttpClient, useValue: httpClientMock },
        { provide: LoggerUtil, useValue: loggerMock },
        { provide: Store, useValue: storeMock },
      ],
    });

    service = TestBed.inject(TradeActivityService);
  });

  it('should call getTrades and return data', () => {
    const mockUrl = 'http://mock-api/';
    const mockRequest = {
      fmrIssueCusips: ['DDB509000'],
      startDate: '2023-07-15',
      endDate: '2023-07-24',
    };
    const mockResponse = [{ id: 'a1' }] as any;

    storeMock.pipe.mockReturnValue(of(mockUrl));
    httpClientMock.post.mockReturnValue(of(mockResponse));

    service.getTrades(mockRequest).subscribe((result) => {
      expect(result).toEqual(mockResponse);
      expect(httpClientMock.post).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
        `${mockUrl}trades`,
        mockRequest,
        expect.objectContaining({ headers: expect.anything() }),
      );
      expect(loggerMock.logInfo).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });
  });

  it('should call getExecutions and return data', () => {
    const mockUrl = 'http://mock-api/';
    const mockRequest = {
      fmrIssueCusips: ['DDB509000'],
      startDate: '2023-07-15',
      endDate: '2023-07-24',
    };
    const mockResponse = [{ id: 'a1' }] as any;

    storeMock.pipe.mockReturnValue(of(mockUrl));
    httpClientMock.post.mockReturnValue(of(mockResponse));

    service.getTrades(mockRequest).subscribe((result) => {
      expect(result).toEqual(mockResponse);
      expect(httpClientMock.post).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
        `${mockUrl}executions`,
        mockRequest,
        expect.objectContaining({ headers: expect.anything() }),
      );
      expect(loggerMock.logInfo).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });
  });

  it('should call getAllocationsByExecutionId and return non-null response', () => {
    const mockUrl = 'http://mock-api/';
    const mockResponse = [{ id: 'a1' }] as any;

    storeMock.pipe.mockReturnValue(of(mockUrl));
    httpClientMock.get.mockReturnValue(of(mockResponse));

    service.getAllocationsByExecutionId('exec-123').subscribe((result) => {
      expect(result).toEqual(mockResponse);
      expect(httpClientMock.get).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
        `${mockUrl}allocations?executionId=exec-123`,
        expect.objectContaining({ headers: expect.anything() }),
      );
    });
  });

  it('should return empty array if response is null', () => {
    storeMock.pipe.mockReturnValue(of('http://mock-api/'));
    httpClientMock.get.mockReturnValue(of(null));

    service.getAllocationsByExecutionId('exec-123').subscribe((result) => {
      expect(result).toEqual([]);
    });
  });
});

File: trades-grid\data-access\src\lib\services\trade-activity.service.ts
/*
 * Copyright (c) 2025 FMR Corp.
 * All Rights Reserved.
 *
 * Fidelity Confidential Information.
 * Created on May 26, 2025

/**
 * @author a526677@fmr.com
 */
import { Injectable } from '@angular/core';
import { filter, mergeMap, Observable } from 'rxjs';
import { HttpClient, HttpHeaders } from '@angular/common/http';
import { select, Store } from '@ngrx/store';
import { LoggerUtil } from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/util/common';
import { v4 } from 'uuid';
import { tradesSelectors } from '../store-trades/trades-grid.selectors';
import { setAgGridLicence } from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/util/ag-grid';
import {
  ExecutionSearchRequest,
  TradeSearchRequest,
} from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/trades-grid/data';
import {
  AllocationModel,
  ExecutionModel,
  TradeModel,
} from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';
import { map } from 'rxjs/operators';

@Injectable()
export class TradeActivityService {
  protected serviceUrl$ = this.store.pipe(
    select(tradesSelectors.getTradeActivityServiceUrl),
    filter((url) => !!url),
  );

  public constructor(
    private readonly store: Store,
    private readonly logger: LoggerUtil,
    private readonly httpClient: HttpClient,
  ) {
    setAgGridLicence(store);
  }

  public getTrades(request: TradeSearchRequest): Observable<TradeModel[]> {
    const endpoint = 'trades';
    const headers = new HttpHeaders().set('X-REQUEST-STATS-TRANSID', v4());
    return this.serviceUrl$.pipe(
      mergeMap((url) => {
        const postUrl = `${url}${endpoint}`;
        this.logger.logInfo(`${TradeActivityService.name}.POST: ${postUrl}`);
        this.logger.logInfo(
          `TradeActivityService request: ${JSON.stringify(request)}`,
        );
        return this.httpClient.post<TradeModel[]>(postUrl, request, {
          headers,
        });
      }),
    );
  }

  public getExecutions(
    request?: ExecutionSearchRequest,
  ): Observable<ExecutionModel[]> {
    const endpoint = 'executions';
    const headers = new HttpHeaders().set('X-REQUEST-STATS-TRANSID', v4());
    return this.serviceUrl$.pipe(
      mergeMap((url) => {
        const postUrl = `${url}${endpoint}`;
        this.logger.logInfo(`${TradeActivityService.name}.POST: ${postUrl}`);
        this.logger.logInfo(
          `TradeActivityService request: ${JSON.stringify(request)}`,
        );
        return this.httpClient.post<ExecutionModel[]>(postUrl, request, {
          headers,
        });
      }),
    );
  }

  public getAllocationsByExecutionId(
    executionId: string,
  ): Observable<AllocationModel[]> {
    const headers = new HttpHeaders().set('X-REQUEST-STATS-TRANSID', v4());
    return this.serviceUrl$.pipe(
      mergeMap((url) => {
        const fullUrl = `${url}allocations?executionId=${executionId}`;
        this.logger.logInfo(`${TradeActivityService.name}.GET: ${fullUrl}`);
        return this.httpClient
          .get<AllocationModel[] | null>(fullUrl, {
            headers,
          })
          .pipe(
            map((response) => {
              return response ? response : [];
            }),
          );
      }),
    );
  }
}

/**
 * @author a526677@fmr.com

import { createAction, props } from '@ngrx/store';
import { ExecutionSearchRequest } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/trades-grid/data';
import { ExecutionsGridStoreConstants } from '../constants/executions-grid.constants';
import { ExecutionModel } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';

const getExecutions = createAction(
  `${ExecutionsGridStoreConstants.ActionKey} ${ExecutionsGridStoreConstants.GetExecutions}`,
  props<{ payload: { request: ExecutionSearchRequest } }>(),
);

const getExecutionsFailure = createAction(
  `${ExecutionsGridStoreConstants.ActionKey} ${ExecutionsGridStoreConstants.GetExecutionsFailure}`,
  props<{ payload: { error: any } }>(),
);

const getExecutionsSuccess = createAction(
  `${ExecutionsGridStoreConstants.ActionKey} ${ExecutionsGridStoreConstants.GetExecutionsSuccess}`,
  props<{ payload: { executions: ExecutionModel[] } }>(),
);

const clearExecutions = createAction(
  `${ExecutionsGridStoreConstants.ActionKey} ${ExecutionsGridStoreConstants.ClearExecutions}`,
);

const setExecutionsTooltipStrategy = createAction(
  `${ExecutionsGridStoreConstants.ActionKey} ${ExecutionsGridStoreConstants.TooltipStrategy}`,
  props<{ strategy: string }>(),
);

export const executionGridActions = {
  getExecutions,
  getExecutionsFailure,
  getExecutionsSuccess,
  clearExecutions,
  setExecutionsTooltipStrategy,
};

/*

/**

import { Observable, of } from 'rxjs';
import { TestBed } from '@angular/core/testing';
import { provideMockActions } from '@ngrx/effects/testing';
import { TradeActivityService } from '../services/trade-activity.service';
import { MockStore, provideMockStore } from '@ngrx/store/testing';
import { Store } from '@ngrx/store';
import { createEntityAdapter, EntityAdapter, EntityState } from '@ngrx/entity';
import {
  ExecutionModel,
  mockExecutions,
  mockTrades,
} from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';
import { cold, hot } from 'jest-marbles';
import { TradeSearchRequest } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/trades-grid/data';
import { ExecutionsGridEffects } from './executions-grid.effects';
import { executionsSelectors } from './executions-grid.selectors';
import { executionGridActions } from './executions-grid.actions';

describe('TradesGridEffects', () => {
  let actions$: Observable<any>;
  let effects: ExecutionsGridEffects;
  let store: MockStore<any>;
  let tradeDataService: TradeActivityService;
  const executionsDataResponse = mockExecutions;
  let entityAdapter: EntityAdapter<ExecutionModel>;
  let initialEntityState: EntityState<ExecutionModel>;

  beforeEach(() => {
    TestBed.configureTestingModule({
      providers: [
        ExecutionsGridEffects,
        provideMockActions(() => actions$),
        {
          provide: TradeActivityService,
          useValue: {
            getExecutions: jest.fn(() => of(executionsDataResponse)),
          },
        },
        provideMockStore({
          selectors: [
            {
              selector: executionsSelectors.getAllExecutions,
              value: mockTrades,
            },
          ],
        }),
      ],
      teardown: { destroyAfterEach: false },
    });
    effects = TestBed.inject(ExecutionsGridEffects);
    store = TestBed.inject(MockStore);
    tradeDataService = TestBed.inject(TradeActivityService);

    entityAdapter = createEntityAdapter<ExecutionModel>();
    initialEntityState = entityAdapter.getInitialState();
    const entityState = entityAdapter.setAll(
      mockExecutions,
      initialEntityState,
    );
    store.setState({
      executionsGrid: { ids: {}, entities: {}, loaded: false, error: null },
    });
  });

  it('should be created', () => {
    // Assert
    expect(effects).toBeTruthy();
  });

  it('getExecutions should return getExecutionsSuccess on success', () => {
    // Arrange
    const getExecutionsAction = executionGridActions.getExecutions({
      payload: { request: {} as TradeSearchRequest },
    });
    const getExecutionsSuccessAction =
      executionGridActions.getExecutionsSuccess({
        payload: { executions: mockExecutions },
      });

    const expected = cold('-b|', { b: getExecutionsSuccessAction });

    // Act
    actions$ = hot('-a|', { a: getExecutionsAction });

    // Assert
    expect(effects.getExecutions$).toBeObservable(expected);
  });

  it('getTrades should return getTradeFailure on failure', () => {
    // Arrange
    const getExecutionsAction = executionGridActions.getExecutions({
      payload: { request: {} as TradeSearchRequest },
    });
    const expectedError = { code: 500, description: 'internal error' };

    const getExecutionsFailureAction =
      executionGridActions.getExecutionsFailure({
        payload: { error: expectedError },
      });
    tradeDataService.getExecutions = jest.fn(() =>
      cold('#|', undefined, { error: expectedError }),
    );
    const expected = cold('-b', { b: getExecutionsFailureAction });

    // Act
    actions$ = hot('-a', { a: getExecutionsAction });

    // Assert
    expect(effects.getExecutions$).toBeObservable(expected);
  });
});

File: trades-grid\data-access\src\lib\store-executions\executions-grid.effects.ts
/*
 * Copyright (c) 2023 FMR Corp.
 * All Rights Reserved.
 *
 * Fidelity Confidential Information.
 * Created on 6/20/23, 4:51 PM
 */

import { Injectable } from '@angular/core';
import { Actions, createEffect, ofType } from '@ngrx/effects';
import { catchError, map, mergeMap } from 'rxjs/operators';
import { of } from 'rxjs';
import { TradeActivityService } from '../services/trade-activity.service';
import { HttpErrorResponse } from '@angular/common/http';
import { executionGridActions } from './executions-grid.actions';

@Injectable({
  providedIn: 'root',
})
export class ExecutionsGridEffects {
  public getExecutions$ = createEffect(() =>
    this.actions$.pipe(
      ofType(executionGridActions.getExecutions),
      mergeMap((action) =>
        this.tradeActivityService.getExecutions(action.payload.request).pipe(
          map((response) => {
            return executionGridActions.getExecutionsSuccess({
              payload: { executions: response },
            });
          }),
          catchError((err: HttpErrorResponse) => {
            return of(
              executionGridActions.getExecutionsFailure({
                // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unsafe-assignment
                payload: { error: err.error },
              }),
            );
          }),
        ),
      ),
    ),
  );

  public constructor(
    private readonly actions$: Actions,
    private readonly tradeActivityService: TradeActivityService,
  ) {}
}
