File: trades-grid\data-access\src\lib\store-executions\executions-grid.reducer.spec.ts
/*
 * Copyright (c) 2023 FMR Corp.
 * All Rights Reserved.
 *
 * Fidelity Confidential Information.
 * Created on 6/20/23, 4:51 PM
 */

/**
 * @author a779672@fmr.com
 */
import { TradeSearchRequest } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/trades-grid/data';
import {
  ExecutionsGridState,
  executionsInitialState,
  executionsModelEntityAdapter,
  executionsReducer,
} from './executions-grid.reducer';
import { mockExecutions } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';
import { executionGridActions } from './executions-grid.actions';

describe('executionsGridReducer', () => {
  let state: ExecutionsGridState;
  beforeEach(() => {
    state = { ...executionsInitialState };
  });

  describe('getExecutions', () => {
    it('should set loaded to false', () => {
      // Arrange
      const searchData = {
        fmrIssueCusips: ['DDB509000'],
        startDate: '2023-07-15',
        endDate: '2023-07-24',
      };
      const action = executionGridActions.getExecutions({
        payload: { request: searchData as TradeSearchRequest },
      });

      // Act
      const result: ExecutionsGridState = executionsReducer(state, action);

      // Assert
      expect(result.error).toBeNull();
      expect(result.loaded).toBeFalsy();
    });
  });

  describe('clearExecutions', () => {
    it('should set state to initial state', () => {
      // Arrange
      const state: ExecutionsGridState =
        executionsModelEntityAdapter.getInitialState({
          loaded: true,
          isLoadingData: true,
        });
      const action = executionGridActions.clearExecutions();

      // Act
      const result: ExecutionsGridState = executionsReducer(state, action);

      // Assert
      expect(result.error).toBeNull();
      expect(result.loaded).toBeFalsy();
      expect(result.isLoadingData).toBeFalsy();
    });
  });

  describe(executionGridActions.getExecutionsFailure.type, () => {
    it('should set the error', () => {
      // Arrange
      const expectedError = { code: 500, description: 'internal error' };
      const action = executionGridActions.getExecutionsFailure({
        payload: { error: expectedError },
      });

      // Act
      const result = executionsReducer(state, action);

      // Assert
      expect(result.error).toStrictEqual('internal error');
      expect(result.loaded).toBeTruthy();
    });
  });

  describe(executionGridActions.getExecutionsSuccess.type, () => {
    it('should set the entities', () => {
      // Arrange

      const action = executionGridActions.getExecutionsSuccess({
        payload: { executions: mockExecutions },
      });

      // Act
      const result = executionsReducer(state, action);

      // Assert
      expect(result.error).toBeNull();
      expect(result.loaded).toBeTruthy();
      expect(result.ids.length).toEqual(mockExecutions.length);
    });
  });
});

File: trades-grid\data-access\src\lib\store-executions\executions-grid.reducer.ts
/*
 * Copyright (c) 2023 FMR Corp.
 * All Rights Reserved.
 *
 * Fidelity Confidential Information.
 * Created on 6/20/23, 4:51 PM
 */

/**
 * @author a526677@fmr.com
 */
import { Action, createReducer, on } from '@ngrx/store';
import {
  BaseGridState,
  createGridEntityAdapter,
} from '../model/grid-store.model';
import { ExecutionsGridStoreConstants } from '../constants/executions-grid.constants';
import { executionGridActions } from './executions-grid.actions';
import { ExecutionModel } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';

export type ExecutionsGridState = BaseGridState<ExecutionModel>;

export interface ExecutionsGridPartialState {
  readonly [ExecutionsGridStoreConstants.FeatureKey]: ExecutionsGridState;
}

export const executionsModelEntityAdapter =
  createGridEntityAdapter<ExecutionModel>((execution) => execution.executionId);

export const executionsInitialState: ExecutionsGridState =
  executionsModelEntityAdapter.getInitialState({
    loaded: false,
    isLoadingData: false,
  });

const executionsGridReducer = createReducer(
  executionsInitialState,
  on(executionGridActions.getExecutions, (state, { payload }) => ({
    ...state,
    loaded: false,
    isLoadingData: true,
    error: null,
  })),
  on(executionGridActions.getExecutionsFailure, (state, { payload }) => {
    return executionsModelEntityAdapter.setAll([], {
      ...state,
      loaded: true,
      isLoadingData: false,
      //eslint-disable-next-line
      error: payload.error.description,
    });
  }),
  on(executionGridActions.getExecutionsSuccess, (state, { payload }) => {
    // eslint-disable-next-line
    const executions = payload.executions ? payload.executions : [];
    return executionsModelEntityAdapter.setAll(executions, {
      ...state,
      loaded: true,
      isLoadingData: false,
      error: null,
    });
  }),
  on(executionGridActions.clearExecutions, (state) => ({
    ...executionsInitialState,
    error: null,
  })),
);

export function executionsReducer(
  state: ExecutionsGridState | undefined,
  action: Action,
): ExecutionsGridState {
  return executionsGridReducer(state, action);
}

/*

File: trades-grid\data-access\src\lib\store-trades\trades-grid.actions.ts
/*

/**
 * @author a526677@fmr.com
 */
import { createAction, props } from '@ngrx/store';
import { TradesGridStoreConstants } from '../constants/trades-grid.constants';
import { TradeModel } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';
import { TradeSearchRequest } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/trades-grid/data';

const getTrades = createAction(
  `${TradesGridStoreConstants.ActionKey} ${TradesGridStoreConstants.GetTrades}`,
  props<{ payload: { request: TradeSearchRequest } }>(),
);

const getTradesFailure = createAction(
  `${TradesGridStoreConstants.ActionKey} ${TradesGridStoreConstants.GetTradesFailure}`,
  props<{ payload: { error: any } }>(),
);

const getTradesSuccess = createAction(
  `${TradesGridStoreConstants.ActionKey} ${TradesGridStoreConstants.GetTradesSuccess}`,
  props<{ payload: { trades: TradeModel[] } }>(),
);

const clearTrades = createAction(
  `${TradesGridStoreConstants.ActionKey} ${TradesGridStoreConstants.ClearTrades}`,
);

const setTradesTooltipStrategy = createAction(
  `${TradesGridStoreConstants.ActionKey} ${TradesGridStoreConstants.TooltipStrategy}`,
  props<{ strategy: string }>(),
);

export const tradesGridActions = {
  getTrades,
  getTradesFailure,
  getTradesSuccess,
  clearTrades,
  setTradesTooltipStrategy,
};

File: trades-grid\data-access\src\lib\store-trades\trades-grid.effects.spec.ts
/*
 * Copyright (c) 2023 FMR Corp.
 * All Rights Reserved.
 *
 * Fidelity Confidential Information.
 * Created on 6/20/23, 4:51 PM
 */

/**
 * @author a526677@fmr.com
 */
import { Observable, of } from 'rxjs';
import { TradesGridEffects } from './trades-grid.effects';
import { TestBed } from '@angular/core/testing';
import { provideMockActions } from '@ngrx/effects/testing';
import { TradeActivityService } from '../services/trade-activity.service';
import { MockStore, provideMockStore } from '@ngrx/store/testing';
import { Store } from '@ngrx/store';
import { createEntityAdapter, EntityAdapter, EntityState } from '@ngrx/entity';
import { mockTrades, TradeModel } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';
import { cold, hot } from 'jest-marbles';
import { TradeSearchRequest } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/trades-grid/data';
import { tradesSelectors } from './trades-grid.selectors';
import { tradesGridActions } from './trades-grid.actions';

describe('TradesGridEffects', () => {
  let actions$: Observable<any>;
  let effects: TradesGridEffects;
  let store: MockStore<any>;
  let tradeDataService: TradeActivityService;
  const tradeDataResponse = mockTrades;
  let entityAdapter: EntityAdapter<TradeModel>;
  let initialEntityState: EntityState<TradeModel>;

  beforeEach(() => {
    TestBed.configureTestingModule({
      providers: [
        TradesGridEffects,
        provideMockActions(() => actions$),
        {
          provide: TradeActivityService,
          useValue: {
            getTrades: jest.fn(() => of(tradeDataResponse)),
          },
        },
        provideMockStore({
          selectors: [
            {
              selector: tradesSelectors.getAllTrades,
              value: mockTrades,
            },
          ],
        }),
      ],
      teardown: { destroyAfterEach: false },
    });
    effects = TestBed.inject(TradesGridEffects);
    store = TestBed.inject(MockStore);
    tradeDataService = TestBed.inject(TradeActivityService);

    entityAdapter = createEntityAdapter<TradeModel>();
    initialEntityState = entityAdapter.getInitialState();
    const entityState = entityAdapter.setAll(mockTrades, initialEntityState);
    store.setState({
      tradesGrid: { ids: {}, entities: {}, loaded: false, error: null },
    });
  });

  it('should be created', () => {
    // Assert
    expect(effects).toBeTruthy();
  });

  it('getTrades should return getTradeSuccess on success', () => {
    // Arrange
    const getTradesAction = tradesGridActions.getTrades({
      payload: { request: {} as TradeSearchRequest },
    });
    const getTradesSuccessAction = tradesGridActions.getTradesSuccess({
      payload: { trades: mockTrades },
    });

    const expected = cold('-b|', { b: getTradesSuccessAction });

    // Act
    actions$ = hot('-a|', { a: getTradesAction });

    // Assert
    expect(effects.getTrades$).toBeObservable(expected);
  });

  it('getTrades should return getTradeFailure on failure', () => {
    // Arrange
    const getTradesAction = tradesGridActions.getTrades({
      payload: { request: {} as TradeSearchRequest },
    });
    const expectedError = { code: 500, description: 'internal error' };

    const getTradesFailureAction = tradesGridActions.getTradesFailure({
      payload: { error: expectedError },
    });
    tradeDataService.getTrades = jest.fn(() =>
      cold('#|', undefined, { error: expectedError }),
    );
    const expected = cold('-b', { b: getTradesFailureAction });

    // Act
    actions$ = hot('-a', { a: getTradesAction });

    // Assert
    expect(effects.getTrades$).toBeObservable(expected);
  });
});

File: trades-grid\data-access\src\lib\store-trades\trades-grid.effects.ts
/*
 * Copyright (c) 2023 FMR Corp.
 * All Rights Reserved.
 *
 * Fidelity Confidential Information.
 * Created on 6/20/23, 4:51 PM
 */

/**
 * @author a526677@fmr.com
 */
import { Injectable } from '@angular/core';
import { Actions, createEffect, ofType } from '@ngrx/effects';
import { catchError, map, mergeMap } from 'rxjs/operators';
import { of } from 'rxjs';
import { TradeActivityService } from '../services/trade-activity.service';
import { HttpErrorResponse } from '@angular/common/http';
import { tradesGridActions } from './trades-grid.actions';

@Injectable({
  providedIn: 'root',
})
export class TradesGridEffects {
  public getTrades$ = createEffect(() =>
    this.actions$.pipe(
      ofType(tradesGridActions.getTrades),
      mergeMap((action) =>
        this.tradeActivityService.getTrades(action.payload.request).pipe(
          map((response) => {
            return tradesGridActions.getTradesSuccess({
              payload: { trades: response },
            });
          }),
          catchError((err: HttpErrorResponse) => {
            return of(
              tradesGridActions.getTradesFailure({
                // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unsafe-assignment
                payload: { error: err.error },
              }),
            );
          }),
        ),
      ),
    ),
  );

  public constructor(
    private readonly actions$: Actions,
    private readonly tradeActivityService: TradeActivityService,
  ) {}
}

File: trades-grid\data-access\src\lib\store-trades\trades-grid.reducer.spec.ts
/*
 * Copyright (c) 2023 FMR Corp.
 * All Rights Reserved.
 *
 * Fidelity Confidential Information.
 * Created on 6/20/23, 4:51 PM
 */

/**
 * @author a526677@fmr.com
 */
import {
  TradesGridState,
  tradesInitialState,
  tradesModelEntityAdapter,
  tradesReducer,
} from './trades-grid.reducer';
import { mockTrades, TradeModel } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';
import { TradeSearchRequest } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/trades-grid/data';
import { tradesGridActions } from './trades-grid.actions';

describe('tradesGridReducer', () => {
  let state: TradesGridState;
  beforeEach(() => {
    state = { ...tradesInitialState };
  });

  describe('getTrades', () => {
    it('should set loaded to false', () => {
      // Arrange
      const searchData = {
        fmrIssueCusips: ['DDB509000'],
        startDate: '2023-07-15',
        endDate: '2023-07-24',
      };
      const action = tradesGridActions.getTrades({
        payload: { request: searchData as TradeSearchRequest },
      });

      // Act
      const result: TradesGridState = tradesReducer(state, action);

      // Assert
      expect(result.error).toBeNull();
      expect(result.loaded).toBeFalsy();
    });
  });

  describe('clearTrades', () => {
    it('should set state to initial state', () => {
      // Arrange
      const state: TradesGridState = tradesModelEntityAdapter.getInitialState({
        loaded: true,
        isLoadingData: true,
      });
      const action = tradesGridActions.clearTrades();

      // Act
      const result: TradesGridState = tradesReducer(state, action);

      // Assert
      expect(result.error).toBeNull();
      expect(result.loaded).toBeFalsy();
      expect(result.isLoadingData).toBeFalsy();
    });
  });

  describe(tradesGridActions.getTradesFailure.type, () => {
    it('should set the error', () => {
      // Arrange
      const expectedError = { code: 500, description: 'internal error' };
      const action = tradesGridActions.getTradesFailure({
        payload: { error: expectedError },
      });

      // Act
      const result = tradesReducer(state, action);

      // Assert
      expect(result.error).toStrictEqual('internal error');
      expect(result.loaded).toBeTruthy();
    });
  });

  describe(tradesGridActions.getTradesSuccess.type, () => {
    it('should set the entities', () => {
      // Arrange
      const trades: TradeModel[] = mockTrades;

      const action = tradesGridActions.getTradesSuccess({
        payload: { trades: trades },
      });

      // Act
      const result = tradesReducer(state, action);

      // Assert
      expect(result.error).toBeNull();
      expect(result.loaded).toBeTruthy();
      expect(result.ids.length).toEqual(trades.length);
    });
  });
});

File: trades-grid\data-access\src\lib\store-trades\trades-grid.reducer.ts
/*
 * Copyright (c) 2023 FMR Corp.
 * All Rights Reserved.
 *
 * Fidelity Confidential Information.
 * Created on 6/20/23, 4:51 PM
 */

/**
 * @author a526677@fmr.com
 */
import { Action, createReducer, on } from '@ngrx/store';
import { TradesGridStoreConstants } from '../constants/trades-grid.constants';
import {
  BaseGridState,
  createGridEntityAdapter,
} from '../model/grid-store.model';
import { tradesGridActions } from './trades-grid.actions';
import { TradeModel } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';

export type TradesGridState = BaseGridState<TradeModel>;

export interface TradesGridPartialState {
  readonly [TradesGridStoreConstants.FeatureKey]: TradesGridState;
}

export const tradesModelEntityAdapter = createGridEntityAdapter<TradeModel>(
  (trade) => trade.entityId,
);

export const tradesInitialState: TradesGridState =
  tradesModelEntityAdapter.getInitialState({
    loaded: false,
    isLoadingData: false,
  });

const tradesGridReducer = createReducer(
  tradesInitialState,
  on(tradesGridActions.getTrades, (state, { payload }) => ({
    ...state,
    loaded: false,
    isLoadingData: true,
    error: null,
  })),
  on(tradesGridActions.getTradesFailure, (state, { payload }) => {
    return tradesModelEntityAdapter.setAll([], {
      ...state,
      loaded: true,
      isLoadingData: false,
      //eslint-disable-next-line
      error: payload.error.description,
    });
  }),
  on(tradesGridActions.getTradesSuccess, (state, { payload }) => {
    // eslint-disable-next-line
    const trades = payload.trades ? payload.trades : [];
    return tradesModelEntityAdapter.setAll(trades, {
      ...state,
      loaded: true,
      isLoadingData: false,
      error: null,
    });
  }),
  on(tradesGridActions.clearTrades, (state) => ({
    ...tradesInitialState,
    error: null,
  })),
);

export function tradesReducer(
  state: TradesGridState | undefined,
  action: Action,
): TradesGridState {
  return tradesGridReducer(state, action);
}

        (component as any).handleBottomEdgeDoubleClick(),

File: trades-grid\feature\src\lib\allocation-detail-renderer\allocation-detail-renderer.component.ts
import {
  ChangeDetectionStrategy,
  ChangeDetectorRef,
  Component,
  DestroyRef,
  ElementRef,
  inject,
  OnDestroy,
  ViewChild,
} from '@angular/core';
import { ICellRendererAngularComp } from '@ag-grid-community/angular';
import {
  autoGroupColumnDef,
  defaultColDef,
} from '../column-definitions/shared-definition-options';
import { allocationsColumnDefs } from '../column-definitions/allocations-column-defs';
import { IprefName } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/trades-grid/data';
import { TradesGridComponent } from '../trades-grid/trades-grid.component';
import { Icon, IPrefOptions } from '@fmr-pr000539/eqt-common-grid';
import {
  GridApi,
  GridReadyEvent,
  ICellRendererParams,
  IRowNode,
} from '@ag-grid-community/core';
import { ExecutionModel } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';
import { AllocationsStore } from './allocation-store/allocations.store';
import { filter } from 'rxjs';
import { takeUntilDestroyed } from '@angular/core/rxjs-interop';
import { SizeChangedEvent } from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/ui/vertical-resize';
import {
  calcFullGridHeight,
  overrideGridOptions,
} from './allocation-detail-renderer.utils';

@Component({
  changeDetection: ChangeDetectionStrategy.Default,
  templateUrl: 'allocation-detail-renderer.component.html',
  styleUrl: 'allocation-detail-renderer.component.scss',
  providers: [AllocationsStore],
  standalone: false,
})
export class AllocationDetailRendererComponent
  implements ICellRendererAngularComp, OnDestroy
{
  public readonly tradesGridInstance = inject(TradesGridComponent);
  public readonly allocationsStore = inject(AllocationsStore);
  public readonly cd = inject(ChangeDetectorRef);
  public readonly destroyRef = inject(DestroyRef);

  public title = 'Fund Allocations';
  public columnDefs = allocationsColumnDefs;
  public iPrefAppName = IprefName.Allocations;
  public iPrefOptions: IPrefOptions = { disabledGridEvents: ['filter'] };
  public data$ = this.allocationsStore.filteredAllocations$;
  public gridOptions: unknown = overrideGridOptions(this.tradesGridInstance);

  public params?: ICellRendererParams;
  @ViewChild('allocationDetailElem', { read: ElementRef })
  protected allocationDetailElem?: ElementRef<HTMLDivElement>;

  /** Height before a double-click expand; null means we are in "natural" state. */
  private heightBeforeExpand: number | null = null;
  private innerGridApi?: GridApi;

  protected readonly autoGroupColumnDef = autoGroupColumnDef;
  protected readonly defaultColDef = defaultColDef;
  protected readonly Icon = Icon;

  public agInit(params: ICellRendererParams): void {
    this.params = params;
    this.hideAllOtherDetails();
    this.setCorrectHeightOnRowsRetrieved();
  }

  public refresh(params: any): boolean {
    return false;
  }

  public ngOnDestroy(): void {
    // AG Grid persists row heights on the node itself, not on the component.
    // Resetting to null here ensures the next time this detail row is opened
    // it starts at the default detailRowHeight instead of the last resized value.
    if (this.params?.node) {
      this.params.node.setRowHeight(null);
      // No need to call onRowHeightChanged — the row is being torn down.
    }
    this.heightBeforeExpand = null;
    this.innerGridApi = undefined;
  }

  public onGridReady(event: GridReadyEvent): void {
    this.innerGridApi = event.api;
    event.api.setSideBarVisible(true);
    const executionId = (this.params?.data as ExecutionModel | undefined)
      ?.executionId;
    if (executionId) this.allocationsStore.loadAllocations(executionId);
    // Defer detectChanges to the next macrotask — calling it synchronously here
    // triggers NG0100 because onGridReady fires during the parent's CD cycle.
    setTimeout(() => this.cd.detectChanges(), 0);
  }

  protected setCorrectHeightOnRowsRetrieved(): void {
    this.data$
      .pipe(filter(Boolean), takeUntilDestroyed(this.destroyRef))
      .subscribe(() => {
        // calculate grid height and dispatch new height to master row detail
        // Wait for Angular and AG Grid to finish rendering the new domLayout
        setTimeout(() => {
          if (!this.allocationDetailElem?.nativeElement) return;

          // Get the actual computed height of the rendered detail element
          const actualHeight =
            this.allocationDetailElem.nativeElement.offsetHeight;
          const detailRowNode = this.params?.node;

          detailRowNode?.setRowHeight(actualHeight);
          this.params?.api.onRowHeightChanged();
          this.cd.detectChanges();
        }, 0);
      });
  }

  protected hideAllOtherDetails(): void {
    this.params?.api.forEachNode((rowNode: IRowNode<any>) => {
      if (
        rowNode.master &&
        !rowNode.group &&
        rowNode.id !== this.params?.node.parent?.id
      ) {
        rowNode.setExpanded(false);
      }
      if (rowNode.id === this.params?.node.parent?.id) {
        rowNode.setExpanded(true);
      }
    });
    // Defer to avoid NG0100 — agInit is called during the parent's CD cycle.
    setTimeout(() => this.cd.detectChanges(), 0);
  }

  protected handleAllocationsVerticalResize(event: SizeChangedEvent): void {
    const newHeight = event.height;
    if (newHeight && newHeight > 0) {
      // A manual resize resets the double-click state
      this.heightBeforeExpand = null;
      this.params?.node.setRowHeight(newHeight);
      this.params?.api.onRowHeightChanged();
    }
  }

  protected handleBottomEdgeDoubleClick(): void {
    const elem = this.allocationDetailElem?.nativeElement;
    if (!elem || !this.innerGridApi) return;

    if (this.heightBeforeExpand === null) {
      // ── Expand to fit content ────────────────────────────────────────────
      this.heightBeforeExpand = elem.offsetHeight;

      const contentHeight = calcFullGridHeight(elem, this.innerGridApi);
      elem.style.height = `${contentHeight}px`;

      this.params?.node.setRowHeight(contentHeight);
      this.params?.api.onRowHeightChanged();
      this.cd.detectChanges();
    } else {
      // ── Restore previous height ──────────────────────────────────────────
      const restore = this.heightBeforeExpand;
      this.heightBeforeExpand = null;

      elem.style.height = `${restore}px`;
      this.params?.node.setRowHeight(restore);
      this.params?.api.onRowHeightChanged();
      this.cd.detectChanges();
    }
  }
}

import {
  calcFullGridHeight,
  overrideGridOptions,
} from './allocation-detail-renderer.utils';
import { TradesGridComponent } from '../trades-grid/trades-grid.component';

describe('AllocationDetailRenderer Utils', () => {
  describe('overrideGridOptions', () => {
    it('should override the grid options correctly', () => {
      const mockTradesGridInstance = {
        gridOptions: {
          someOption: 'someValue',
        },
      } as any;

      const newGridOptions = overrideGridOptions(mockTradesGridInstance);

      expect(newGridOptions.suppressAggFuncInHeader).toBe(true);
      expect(newGridOptions.masterDetail).toBe(false);
      expect(newGridOptions.rowGroupPanelShow).toBe('never');
      expect(newGridOptions.someOption).toBe('someValue');
    });
  });

  describe('calcFullGridHeight', () => {
    let sectionElem: HTMLElement;
    let mockInnerGridApi: any;

    beforeEach(() => {
      sectionElem = document.createElement('div');
      document.body.appendChild(sectionElem);

      mockInnerGridApi = {
        getSizesForCurrentTheme: jest.fn().mockReturnValue({ rowHeight: 30 }),
        forEachNodeAfterFilterAndSort: jest.fn(),
      };
    });

    afterEach(() => {
      document.body.removeChild(sectionElem);
    });

    it('should return the offsetHeight of the section element if innerGridApi is not provided', () => {
      Object.defineProperty(sectionElem, 'offsetHeight', {
        configurable: true,
        value: 500,
      });
      const height = calcFullGridHeight(sectionElem);
      expect(height).toBe(500);
    });

    it('should calculate the height correctly based on row heights', () => {
      const header = document.createElement('div');
      header.className = 'ag-header';
      sectionElem.appendChild(header);
      Object.defineProperty(header, 'offsetHeight', {
        configurable: true,
        value: 50,
      });

      mockInnerGridApi.forEachNodeAfterFilterAndSort.mockImplementation(
        (callback: (node: any) => void) => {
          [{ rowHeight: 40 }, { rowHeight: 40 }, { rowHeight: 40 }].forEach(
            callback,
          );
        },
      );

      const height = calcFullGridHeight(sectionElem, mockInnerGridApi);
      expect(height).toBe(50 + 3 * 40 + 4); // header + rows + buffer
    });

    it('should use themeRowHeight if node.rowHeight is not available', () => {
      const header = document.createElement('div');
      header.className = 'ag-header';
      sectionElem.appendChild(header);
      Object.defineProperty(header, 'offsetHeight', {
        configurable: true,
        value: 50,
      });

      mockInnerGridApi.forEachNodeAfterFilterAndSort.mockImplementation(
        (callback: (node: any) => void) => {
          [{}, {}, {}].forEach(callback);
        },
      );

      const height = calcFullGridHeight(sectionElem, mockInnerGridApi);
      expect(height).toBe(50 + 3 * 30 + 4); // header + rows (theme) + buffer
    });

    it('should include footer height if footer element exists', () => {
      const header = document.createElement('div');
      header.className = 'ag-header';
      sectionElem.appendChild(header);
      Object.defineProperty(header, 'offsetHeight', {
        configurable: true,
        value: 50,
      });

      const footer = document.createElement('div');
      footer.className = 'ag-paging-panel';
      sectionElem.appendChild(footer);
      Object.defineProperty(footer, 'offsetHeight', {
        configurable: true,
        value: 40,
      });

      mockInnerGridApi.forEachNodeAfterFilterAndSort.mockImplementation(
        (callback: (node: any) => void) => {
          [{}, {}, {}].forEach(callback);
        },
      );

      const height = calcFullGridHeight(sectionElem, mockInnerGridApi);
      expect(height).toBe(50 + 3 * 30 + 40 + 4); // header + rows + footer + buffer
    });
  });
});

File: trades-grid\feature\src\lib\allocation-detail-renderer\allocation-detail-renderer.utils.ts
import { GridApi } from '@ag-grid-community/core';
import {
  excelStyles,
  initialGroupOrderComparator,
} from '../column-definitions/shared-definition-options';
import { TradesGridComponent } from '../trades-grid/trades-grid.component';

/**
 * Calculates the height required to show all rows in the inner ag-grid
 * without virtual scrolling, by summing displayed row heights and adding
 * chrome (header, optional pagination/status bars) measured from the DOM.
 */
export function calcFullGridHeight(
  sectionElem: HTMLElement,
  innerGridApi?: GridApi,
): number {
  if (!innerGridApi) return sectionElem.offsetHeight;

  const DEFAULT_HEADER_HEIGHT = 32;
  const BUFFER = 4;

  // Use the theme's configured row height as the fallback
  const themeRowHeight = innerGridApi.getSizesForCurrentTheme().rowHeight;

  // Sum every displayed row's actual pixel height (handles variable row heights / groups)
  let totalRowsHeight = 0;
  innerGridApi.forEachNodeAfterFilterAndSort((node) => {
    const rh = node.rowHeight;
    totalRowsHeight += rh != null ? rh : themeRowHeight;
  });

  // Measure non-row chrome from the live DOM so we stay theme-agnostic
  const headerEl = sectionElem.querySelector<HTMLElement>('.ag-header');
  const headerHeight = headerEl ? headerEl.offsetHeight : DEFAULT_HEADER_HEIGHT;

  const footerEl = sectionElem.querySelector<HTMLElement>(
    '.ag-floating-bottom, .ag-paging-panel, .ag-status-bar',
  );
  const footerHeight = footerEl ? footerEl.offsetHeight : 0;

  return headerHeight + totalRowsHeight + footerHeight + BUFFER;
}

export function overrideGridOptions(
  tradesGridInstance: TradesGridComponent,
): any {
  return {
    ...tradesGridInstance.gridOptions,
    suppressAggFuncInHeader: true,

/*

import { AllocationsStore } from './allocations.store';
import { TestBed } from '@angular/core/testing';
import { TradeActivityService } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/trades-grid/data-access';
import { of, take, throwError } from 'rxjs';
import { HttpErrorResponse } from '@angular/common/http';
import { AllocationModel } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';

const tradeActivityServiceMock = {
  getAllocationsByExecutionId: jest.fn(),
};

let store: AllocationsStore;

beforeEach(() => {
  TestBed.configureTestingModule({
    providers: [
      AllocationsStore,
      { provide: TradeActivityService, useValue: tradeActivityServiceMock },
    ],
  });

  store = TestBed.inject(AllocationsStore);
});

it('should load allocations successfully', (done) => {
  tradeActivityServiceMock.getAllocationsByExecutionId.mockReturnValue(
    of(mockAllocations),
  );

  store.loadAllocations(of('exec-123'));

  store.allocations$.subscribe((allocations) => {
    expect(allocations).toEqual(mockAllocations);
    done();
  });
});

it('should handle error when loading allocations fails', () => {
  const errorResponse = new HttpErrorResponse({ error: 'Error', status: 500 });
  tradeActivityServiceMock.getAllocationsByExecutionId.mockReturnValue(
    throwError(() => errorResponse),
  );

  store.loadAllocations(of('exec-123'));

  store.error$.pipe(take(1)).subscribe((error) => {
    expect(error).toBe('Http failure response for (unknown url): 500 Error');
  });
});

it('should set loading state', (done) => {
  store.setIsLoading(true);
  store.isLoading$.subscribe((loading) => {
    expect(loading).toBe(true);
    done();
  });
});

it('should toggle showUnallocatedMembers', (done) => {
  store.setShowUnallocatedMembers(true);
  store.showUnallocatedMembers$.subscribe((show) => {
    expect(show).toBe(true);
    done();
  });
});

it('should filter unallocated members', (done) => {
  store.setAllocations(mockAllocations as unknown as AllocationModel[]);
  store.setShowUnallocatedMembers(false);
  store.filteredAllocations$.subscribe((allocations) => {
    expect(allocations?.length).toBe(1); // Only one allocation has tradeQuantity > 0
    done();
  });
});

it('should return all members when showUnallocated boolean = true', (done) => {
  store.setAllocations(mockAllocations as unknown as AllocationModel[]);
  store.setShowUnallocatedMembers(true);
  store.filteredAllocations$.subscribe((allocations) => {
    expect(allocations?.length).toBe(mockAllocations.length);
    done();
  });
});

File: trades-grid\feature\src\lib\allocation-detail-renderer\allocation-store\allocations.store.ts
/*
 * Copyright (c) 2025 FMR Corp.
 * All Rights Reserved.
 *
 * Fidelity Confidential Information.
 * Created on Sept 02, 2025
 */

import { AllocationModel } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';
import { ComponentStore } from '@ngrx/component-store';
import { Injectable } from '@angular/core';
import { TradeActivityService } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/trades-grid/data-access';
import { Observable, switchMap, tap, catchError, EMPTY } from 'rxjs';
import { HttpErrorResponse } from '@angular/common/http';

export interface AllocationState {
  allocations: AllocationModel[] | null;
  isLoading: boolean;
  error: string | null;
  showUnallocatedMembers: boolean;
}

@Injectable()
export class AllocationsStore extends ComponentStore<AllocationState> {
  // Selectors
  public readonly allocations$ = this.select((state) => state.allocations);
  public readonly isLoading$ = this.select((state) => state.isLoading);
  public readonly error$ = this.select((state) => state.error);

  /**
   * Toggle selector for the Unallocated members visibility.
   */
  public readonly showUnallocatedMembers$ = this.select(
    (state) => state.showUnallocatedMembers,
  );

  /**
   * It returns allocations filtered by "showUnallocatedMembers" selector.
   */
  public readonly filteredAllocations$ = this.select(
    this.allocations$,
    this.showUnallocatedMembers$,
    (allocations, showUnallocatedMembers) => {
      if (!allocations) return null;
      if (showUnallocatedMembers) return allocations;
      return allocations.filter((allocation) => allocation.tradeQuantity);
    },
  );

  // Actions or Updaters
  public readonly setIsLoading = this.updater((state, isLoading: boolean) => ({
    ...state,
    isLoading,
    error: null,
  }));

  public readonly setAllocations = this.updater(
    (state, allocations: AllocationModel[]) => ({
      ...state,
      allocations,
      isLoading: false,
    }),
  );
  public readonly setError = this.updater((state, error: string) => ({
    ...state,
    error,
    isLoading: false,
  }));
  public readonly setShowUnallocatedMembers = this.updater(
    (state, showUnallocatedMembers: boolean) => ({
      ...state,
      showUnallocatedMembers,
    }),
  );

  // Effects
  public readonly loadAllocations = this.effect(
    (executionId$: Observable<string>) =>
      executionId$.pipe(
        tap(() => this.setIsLoading(true)),
        switchMap((executionId) =>
          this.tradeActivityService
            .getAllocationsByExecutionId(executionId)
            .pipe(
              tap((allocations) => this.setAllocations(allocations)),
              catchError((error: HttpErrorResponse) => {
                this.setError(error.message);
                return EMPTY;
              }),
            ),
        ),
      ),
  );

  public constructor(
    private readonly tradeActivityService: TradeActivityService,
  ) {
    super({
      allocations: null,
      isLoading: false,
      error: null,
      showUnallocatedMembers: false,
    });
  }
}

      'limitPriceAmount',

      'executionCommissionRate',
      'executionCommissionAmount',
      'researchCommissionRate',

      'executionClearingBrokerRate',
      'clearingBrokerAmt',
      'executingBrokerRate',
      'executingBrokerAmt',
      'executionExchangeFeeRate',
      'exchangeFee',
      'executionBlockPremiumRate',
      'blockPremium',
      'rollRebateRate',
      'rollRebate',
      'giveUpFeeRate',
      'giveUpFee',
    ];
    const actualColIds = allocationsColumnDefs.map((col) => col.colId);
    expect(actualColIds).toEqual(expectedColIds);
  });

  it('should have correct properties for "Status" column', () => {
    const column = allocationsColumnDefs.find(
      (col) => col.colId === 'tradeStatus',
    );
    expect(column).toBeDefined();
    expect(column?.headerName).toBe('Status');
    expect(column?.field).toBe('tradeStatus');
    expect(column?.filter).toBe('agSetColumnFilter');
  });

  it('should have correct properties for "Trade Quantity" column and format number correctly', () => {
    const column = allocationsColumnDefs.find(
      (col) => col.colId === 'tradeQuantity',
    );
    expect(column).toBeDefined();
    expect(column?.headerName).toBe('Trade Quantity');
    expect(column?.field).toBe('tradeQuantity');
    expect(column?.filter).toBe('agNumberColumnFilter');
    const cellRenderer = column?.cellRenderer as (
      params: ICellRendererParams,
    ) => string;
    const params = { value: 12345.678 } as ICellRendererParams;
    expect(cellRenderer(params)).toBe('12,345.68');
  });

  it('should have correct properties for "Limit Price" column and format number correctly', () => {
    const column = allocationsColumnDefs.find(
      (col) => col.colId === 'limitPriceAmount',
    );
    expect(column).toBeDefined();
    const cellRenderer = column?.cellRenderer as (
      params: ICellRendererParams,
    ) => string;
    const params = { value: 123.456789 } as ICellRendererParams;
    expect(cellRenderer(params)).toBe('123.456789');
  });

  it('should handle valueGetter for "Gross Amount"', () => {
    const column = allocationsColumnDefs.find(
      (col) => col.colId === 'tradeGrossAmount',
    );
    expect(column).toBeDefined();
    const valueGetter = column?.valueGetter as (params: any) => any;
    const params = {
      node: { group: false },
      data: {
        executionCurrencyCode: 'USD',
        side: 'Buy',
        tradeGrossAmount: 5000,
      },
    };
    expect(valueGetter(params)).toEqual({
      currency: 'USD',
      side: 'Buy',
      amount: 5000,
    });
  });

  it('should handle valueFormatter for "Gross Amount"', () => {
    const column = allocationsColumnDefs.find(
      (col) => col.colId === 'tradeGrossAmount',
    );
    expect(column).toBeDefined();
    const valueFormatter = column?.valueFormatter as (
      params: ValueFormatterParams,
    ) => string;
    const params = {
      value: { amount: 5000.123 },
    } as ValueFormatterParams;
    expect(valueFormatter(params)).toBe('5,000.12');
  });

  it('should format "Cancel Date/Time" correctly', () => {
    const column = allocationsColumnDefs.find(
      (col) => col.colId === 'cancelTimeStamp',
    );
    expect(column).toBeDefined();
    const valueFormatter = column?.valueFormatter as (
      params: ValueFormatterParams<AllocationModel, string>,
    ) => string;

  });

    {
      colId: 'exchangeFee',
      headerName: 'Exchange Fee Amount',
      field: 'exchangeFee',
    },
    {
      colId: 'executionBlockPremiumRate',
      headerName: 'Block Premium Rate',
      field: 'executionBlockPremiumRate',
    },
    {
      colId: 'blockPremium',
      headerName: 'Block Premium Amount',
      field: 'blockPremium',
    },
    {
      colId: 'rollRebateRate',
      headerName: 'Roll Rebate Rate',
      field: 'rollRebateRate',
    },
    {
      colId: 'rollRebate',
      headerName: 'Roll Rebate Amount',
      field: 'rollRebate',
    },
    {
      colId: 'giveUpFeeRate',
      headerName: 'Give Up/In Fee Rate',
      field: 'giveUpFeeRate',
    },
    {
      colId: 'giveUpFee',
      headerName: 'Give Up/In Fee Amount',
      field: 'giveUpFee',
    },
  ])(
    'should have correct properties for "$headerName" number-filter column',
    ({ colId, headerName, field }) => {
      const column = allocationsColumnDefs.find((col) => col.colId === colId);
      expect(column).toBeDefined();
      expect(column?.headerName).toBe(headerName);
      expect(column?.field).toBe(field);
      expect(column?.filter).toBe('agNumberColumnFilter');
      expect(column?.cellRenderer).toBeDefined();
    },
  );

  it.each([
    { colId: 'tradeGrossAmountRootCurrency', value: 9876.543 },
    { colId: 'totalTaxAmount', value: 100.005 },
    { colId: 'totalFeeAmount', value: 200.125 },
    { colId: 'totalInterestBoughtSoldAmount', value: 50.999 },
    { colId: 'executionPricePerUnit', value: 12.34 },
    { colId: 'totalCommissionAmount', value: 300.1 },
  ])(
    'should format number to 2 decimal places for "$colId" cellRenderer',
    ({ colId, value }) => {
      const column = allocationsColumnDefs.find((col) => col.colId === colId);
      const cellRenderer = column?.cellRenderer as (
        params: ICellRendererParams,
      ) => string;
      const result = cellRenderer({ value } as ICellRendererParams);
      expect(result).toBe(
        value.toLocaleString('en-US', {
          minimumFractionDigits: 2,
          maximumFractionDigits: 2,
        }),
      );
    },
  );

  it.each([
    {
      colId: 'settlementDate',
      headerName: 'Settle Date',
      field: 'settlementDate',
    },
    { colId: 'tradeDate', headerName: 'Trade Date', field: 'tradeDate' },
  ])(
    'should have correct properties for "$headerName" date-filter column',
    ({ colId, headerName, field }) => {
      const column = allocationsColumnDefs.find((col) => col.colId === colId);
      expect(column).toBeDefined();
      expect(column?.headerName).toBe(headerName);
      expect(column?.field).toBe(field);
      expect(column?.filter).toBe('agDateColumnFilter');
    },
  );

  it('should return null from valueGetter for "Gross Amount" when node is a group', () => {
    const column = allocationsColumnDefs.find(
      (col) => col.colId === 'tradeGrossAmount',
    );
    expect(column).toBeDefined();
    const valueGetter = column?.valueGetter as (params: any) => any;
    const params = { node: { group: true }, data: {} };
    expect(valueGetter(params)).toBeNull();
  });

  it('should return null from valueGetter for "Gross Amount" when node is null', () => {
    const column = allocationsColumnDefs.find(
      (col) => col.colId === 'tradeGrossAmount',
    );
    expect(column).toBeDefined();
    const valueGetter = column?.valueGetter as (params: any) => any;
    const params = { node: null, data: {} };
    expect(valueGetter(params)).toBeNull();
  });

  it('should use keyCreator and filterValueGetter for "Gross Amount"', () => {
    const column = allocationsColumnDefs.find(
      (col) => col.colId === 'tradeGrossAmount',
    );
    expect(column).toBeDefined();
    const keyCreator = column?.keyCreator as (params: any) => string;
    expect(keyCreator({ value: { amount: 1234 } })).toBe(1234 as any);

    const filterValueGetter = column?.filterValueGetter as (
      params: any,
    ) => number;
    expect(filterValueGetter({ data: { tradeGrossAmount: 999 } })).toBe(999);
  });
});

/*
 * Copyright (c) 2025 FMR Corp.
 * All Rights Reserved.
 *
 * Fidelity Confidential Information.
 * Created on Aug 08, 2025
 */

import {
  ColDef,
  ICellRendererParams,
  ValueFormatterParams,
} from '@ag-grid-community/core';
import {
  getDateTimeGetter,
  numberFormatter,
} from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/util/ag-grid';
import { RowGroupTooltipComponent } from '../trades-grid/row-group-tooltip/row-group-tooltip.component'; /* eslint-disable */
import { getCancelReasonDisplayText } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';
import { PersonCacheService } from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/data-access/person';

import {
  createExecutionExecutedByColumnDef,
  createExecutionTraderColumnDef,
} from './executions';
import { AGGREGATE_UNIQUE_VALUES } from './constants';

/* eslint-disable */
export function getExecutionsColumnDef(
  personCacheService: PersonCacheService,
): ColDef[] {
  return [
    {
      headerName: 'Execution ID',
      colId: 'executionId',
      field: 'executionId',
      minWidth: 180,
      maxWidth: 250,
      filter: 'agSetColumnFilter',
    },
    {
      headerName: 'Trade Date',
      field: 'tradeDate',

import {
  ColDef,
  FirstDataRenderedEvent,
  GridOptions,
  ProcessCellForExportParams,
  ValueFormatterParams,
  ValueGetterParams,
} from '@ag-grid-community/core';
import {
  ExcelStyle,
  InitialGroupOrderComparatorParams,
} from 'ag-grid-community';
import { AllocationRenderComponent } from '../trades-grid/cell-renderers/allocation-render.component';
import { ExecutionModel, TradeModel } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';
import { isTradeCancelled } from '../trades-grid/menu-utils';

export const defaultGridOptions: GridOptions<TradeModel | ExecutionModel> = {
  enableCharts: true,
  suppressAggFuncInHeader: true,
  headerHeight: 35,
  embedFullWidthRows: false,
  tooltipShowDelay: 0,
  rowSelection: 'multiple',
  isRowSelectable: (node) => !!node.data && !isTradeCancelled(node.data),
  groupSelectsChildren: true,
  groupSelectsFiltered: false,
  animateRows: true,
  debounceVerticalScrollbar: true,
  suppressColumnVirtualisation: false,
  suppressRowVirtualisation: false,
};

export const defaultColDef: ColDef = {
  resizable: true,
  sortable: true,
  flex: 1,
  floatingFilter: true,
  suppressHeaderMenuButton: true,
  enableRowGroup: true,
};

export const autoGroupColumnDef: ColDef = {
  resizable: true,
  cellStyle: { textAlign: 'left' },
  editable: (params) => !!params.node.group,
  enablePivot: true,
  lockPinned: true,
  lockPosition: true,
  suppressMovable: true,
  pinned: 'left',
  minWidth: 100,
  maxWidth: 250,
  cellRenderer: 'agGroupCellRenderer',
  sortable: true,
  cellRendererParams: {
    suppressCount: true,
    suppressDoubleClickExpand: true,
    innerRenderer: AllocationRenderComponent,
  },
};

export const initialGroupOrderComparator: (
  params: InitialGroupOrderComparatorParams,
) => number = (params: InitialGroupOrderComparatorParams) => {
  const a = params.nodeA.key ?? '';
  const b = params.nodeB.key ?? '';
  if (a === '') {
    return 1;
  }
  if (b === '') {
    return -1;
  }
  if (a < b) {
    return -1;
  }
  return a > b ? 1 : 0;
};

export const excelStyles: ExcelStyle[] = [
  {
    id: 'dateISO',
    dataType: 'DateTime',
    numberFormat: {
      format: 'yyy-mm-dd',
    },
  },
];

export const booleanColumnDisplayColumnDef: any = {
  cellDataType: false,
  valueFormatter: (params: ValueFormatterParams) => {
    if (params.value === null || params.value === undefined) return '';
    return params.value === true || params.value === 'Y' ? 'Y' : 'N';
  },
  filterValueGetter: (params: ValueGetterParams<unknown>) => {
    const val = params.getValue(params.column.getColId()) as unknown;
    if (val === null || val === undefined) return '';
    return val === true || val === 'Y' ? 'Y' : 'N';
  },
};

export function createTradesGridOptions(
  callbacks: {
    onFirstDataRendered?: (params: FirstDataRenderedEvent) => void;
    onRowClicked?: (event: any) => void;
    onSelectionChanged?: () => void;
    onColumnRowGroupChanged?: () => void;
    onCellMouseDown?: (event: any) => void;
    onColumnPinned?: () => void;
  },
  dependencies: {
    loadingOverlayComponent?: any;
    processDates?: (params: any) => any;
    formatAmountForExport?: (
      params: ProcessCellForExportParams,
    ) => string | undefined;
    aggFuncs?: Record<string, any>;
  },
): Record<string, unknown> {
  return {
    ...defaultGridOptions,
    loadingOverlayComponent: dependencies.loadingOverlayComponent,
    processCellForClipboard: dependencies.processDates,
    excelStyles: excelStyles,
    aggFuncs: dependencies.aggFuncs,
    initialGroupOrderComparator: initialGroupOrderComparator,
    onFirstDataRendered: callbacks.onFirstDataRendered,
    enableCharts: true,
    onRowClicked: callbacks.onRowClicked,
    defaultExcelExportParams: {
      processCellCallback: dependencies.formatAmountForExport,
    },
    defaultCsvExportParams: {
      processCellCallback: dependencies.formatAmountForExport,
    },
    onSelectionChanged: callbacks.onSelectionChanged,
    onColumnRowGroupChanged: callbacks.onColumnRowGroupChanged,
    onCellMouseDown: callbacks.onCellMouseDown,
    onColumnPinned: callbacks.onColumnPinned,
  };
}

export function getTradesColumnDef(

  return [
    {
      headerName: 'Trade ID',

    },
    {

      colId: 'settlementDate',
      filter: 'agDateColumnFilter',
      minWidth: 100,
    },
    {
      headerName: 'Execution Date/Time',
      field: 'creationTimestamp',
      colId: 'creationTimestamp',
      minWidth: 100,
      filter: 'agDateColumnFilter',
      valueFormatter: (params) => {
        if (params.data !== undefined) {
          return getDateTimeGetter(params.data.creationTimestamp);

          return '';

            currency: params.data.executionCurrencyCode as string,
            side: params.data.side as string,
            amount: params.data.tradeGrossAmount as number,

      tooltipValueGetter: (params) => getCancelReasonDisplayText(params.value),
    },
    {
      headerName: 'Cancelled By',
      field: 'cancelledByPersonIdSource',
      colId: 'cancelledByPersonIdSource',
      minWidth: 120,
      filter: AG_SET_COLUMN_FILTER,
      aggFunc: AGGREGATE_UNIQUE_VALUES,
      cellRenderer: (params: ICellRendererParams) => {
        if (params.node.group) {
          const aggregatedValue =
            params.node.aggData?.cancelledByPersonIdSource;
          if (!aggregatedValue) {
            return '';
          }

          return aggregatedValue
            .split(', ')
            .map((id: string) => personCacheService.getPersonInitials(id))
            .join(', ');
        }

        if (!params.value) {
          return '';
        }

        return personCacheService.getPersonInitials(params.value);
      },
      filterParams: {
        valueFormatter: (params: ValueFormatterParams) =>
          params?.value
            ? personCacheService.getPersonInitials(params.value)
            : '',
      },
      tooltipValueGetter: (params) => {
        if (params?.node?.group) {
          const aggregatedValue =
            params.node.aggData?.cancelledByPersonIdSource;
          if (!aggregatedValue) {
            return '';
          }

          return aggregatedValue
            .split(', ')
            .map((value: string) =>
              personCacheService.getFullNameFromInitial(value),
            )
            .join(', ');
        }

        const cancelledByPersonIdSource =
          params.data?.cancelledByPersonIdSource;
        if (!cancelledByPersonIdSource) {
          return '';
        }

        return personCacheService.getPersonFullName(cancelledByPersonIdSource);
      },
      valueFormatter: (params) =>
        params?.value ? personCacheService.getPersonInitials(params.value) : '',
      filterValueGetter: (params) => {
        if (params?.node?.group) {
          return params.node.aggData?.cancelledByPersonIdSource ?? '';
        }
        const cancelledByPersonIdSource =
          params.data?.cancelledByPersonIdSource;

        if (!cancelledByPersonIdSource) {
          return '';
        }

        return personCacheService.getPersonInitialsFiltering(
          cancelledByPersonIdSource,
        );
      },
      valueGetter: (params) => {
        if (params.node?.group) {
          return params.node.aggData?.cancelledByPersonIdSource ?? '';
        }

        const cancelledByPersonIdSource =
          params.data?.cancelledByPersonIdSource;
        if (!cancelledByPersonIdSource) {
          return '';
        }

        return personCacheService.getPersonInitials(cancelledByPersonIdSource);
      },
      keyCreator: (params) => params.value,
    },
    {
      headerName: 'Trading Desk',
      field: 'tradingDesk',
      colId: 'tradingDesk',
      minWidth: 120,
      filter: 'agSetColumnFilter',
    },

File: trades-grid\feature\src\lib\column-definitions\trades-grid.config.spec.ts
import { ValueGetterFunc, ValueGetterParams } from '@ag-grid-community/core';
import { fakeAsync } from '@angular/core/testing';
import { getTradesColumnDef } from './trades-column-defs';
import { PersonCacheService } from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/data-access/person';

describe('TradesGridConfig', () => {
  const mockPersonCacheService = new PersonCacheService();
  mockPersonCacheService.setPersons = jest.fn();
  mockPersonCacheService.clear = jest.fn();
  mockPersonCacheService.getPersonInitialsFiltering = jest.fn();
  mockPersonCacheService.getPersonInitials = jest.fn();
  mockPersonCacheService.getPersonFullName = jest.fn();
  describe('Grid Columns', () => {
    it('should return currency, side, amount for gross amount value getter function', fakeAsync(() => {
      // Arrange
      const valueGetter = getTradesColumnDef(mockPersonCacheService)[11]
        .valueGetter as ValueGetterFunc;
      const rowData = {
        executionCurrencyCode: 'USD',
        side: 'BUY',
        tradeGrossAmount: 50,
      };
      const params = {
        data: rowData,
        node: { group: false },
      } as ValueGetterParams;

      // Act
      const result = valueGetter(params);

      // Assert
      expect(result).toEqual({ currency: 'USD', side: 'BUY', amount: 50 });
    }));

    it('should return null quotes for null values for gross amount value getter function', fakeAsync(() => {
      // Arrange
      const valueGetter = getTradesColumnDef(mockPersonCacheService)[11]
        .valueGetter as ValueGetterFunc;
      const rowData = {
        executionCurrencyCode: 'USD',
        side: 'BUY',
        totalNetProceedsAmount: 50,
      };
      const params = {
        data: rowData,
        node: null,
      } as ValueGetterParams;

      // Act
      const result = valueGetter(params);

      // Assert
      expect(result).toEqual('');
    }));

    it('should return currency, side, amount for net amount value getter function', fakeAsync(() => {
      // Arrange
      const tradesColumns = getTradesColumnDef(mockPersonCacheService);

      // 2. Find the specific column by its ID instead of a numeric index
      const netAmountColumn = tradesColumns.find(
        (c) => c.colId === 'totalNetProceedsAmount',
      );

      // 3. Assert that the column and its valueGetter exist
      expect(netAmountColumn).toBeDefined();
      expect(typeof netAmountColumn?.valueGetter).toBe('function');

      // 4. Cast and execute the valueGetter
      const valueGetter = netAmountColumn?.valueGetter as ValueGetterFunc;

      const rowData = {
        executionCurrencyCode: 'USD',
        side: 'BUY',
        totalNetProceedsAmount: 50,
      };
      const params = {
        data: rowData,
        node: { group: false },
      } as ValueGetterParams;

      // Act
      const result = valueGetter(params);

      // Assert
      expect(result).toEqual({ currency: 'USD', side: 'BUY', amount: 50 });
    }));

    it('should return [Buy,0], for net amount value getter function when null', fakeAsync(() => {
      // Arrange
      const columns = getTradesColumnDef(mockPersonCacheService);
      const netAmountColumn = columns.find(
        (c) => c.colId === 'totalNetProceedsAmount',
      );
      expect(netAmountColumn).toBeDefined(); // Ensures the column was found
      const valueGetter = netAmountColumn?.valueGetter as ValueGetterFunc;

      const rowData = {
        executionCurrencyCode: 'USD',
        side: 'BUY',
        totalNetProceedsAmount: 50,
      };
      const params = {
        data: rowData,
        node: null,
      } as ValueGetterParams;

      // Act
      const result = valueGetter(params);

      // Assert
      expect(result).toEqual(['Buy', 0]);
    }));

    it('should return side, amount for net amount usd value getter function', fakeAsync(() => {
      // Arrange
      const tradesColumns = getTradesColumnDef(mockPersonCacheService);
      const totalNetProceedsAmountRoot = tradesColumns.find(
        (c) => c.colId === 'totalNetProceedsAmountRoot',
      );

      expect(totalNetProceedsAmountRoot).toBeDefined();

      const valueGetter =
        totalNetProceedsAmountRoot?.valueGetter as ValueGetterFunc;
      const rowData = {
        executionCurrencyCode: 'USD',
        side: 'BUY',
        totalNetProceedsAmountRoot: 50,
      };
      const params = {
        data: rowData,
        node: { group: false },
      } as ValueGetterParams;

      // Act
      const result = valueGetter(params);

      // Assert
      expect(result).toEqual({
        side: 'BUY',
        amount: 50,
      });
    }));

    it('should return [] for net amount usd value getter function when null', fakeAsync(() => {
      // Arrange
      const tradesColumns = getTradesColumnDef(mockPersonCacheService);
      const totalNetProceedsAmountRoot = tradesColumns.find(
        (c) => c.colId === 'totalNetProceedsAmountRoot',
      );

      expect(totalNetProceedsAmountRoot).toBeDefined();

      const valueGetter =
        totalNetProceedsAmountRoot?.valueGetter as ValueGetterFunc;
      const rowData = {
        executionCurrencyCode: 'USD',
        side: 'BUY',
        totalNetProceedsAmountRoot: 50,
      };
      const params = {
        data: rowData,
        node: null,
      } as ValueGetterParams;

      // Act
      const result = valueGetter(params);

      // Assert
      expect(result).toEqual([]);
    }));

    it('should return amount for executed price value getter function', fakeAsync(() => {
      // Arrange
      // 1. Get all column definitions
      const tradesColumns = getTradesColumnDef(mockPersonCacheService);

      // 2. Find the specific column by its ID instead of a numeric index
      const executionPricePerUnitColumn = tradesColumns.find(
        (c) => c.colId === 'executionPricePerUnit',
      );

      // 3. Assert that the column and its valueGetter exist
      expect(executionPricePerUnitColumn).toBeDefined();
      expect(typeof executionPricePerUnitColumn?.valueGetter).toBe('function');

      // 4. Cast and execute the valueGetter
      const valueGetter =
        executionPricePerUnitColumn?.valueGetter as ValueGetterFunc;
      const rowData = {
        executionPricePerUnit: 50,
      };
      const params = {
        data: rowData,
        node: { group: false },
      } as ValueGetterParams;

      // Act
      const result = valueGetter(params);

      // Assert
      expect(result).toEqual({ amount: 50 });
    }));
  });
});

import { createExecutionExecutedByColumnDef } from './executedby-column';

describe('createExecutionExecutedByColumnDef', () => {
  let mockPersonCacheService: PersonCacheService;

  beforeEach(() => {
    mockPersonCacheService = {
      getFullNameFromInitial: jest.fn(),
    } as unknown as PersonCacheService;
  });

  describe('column definition properties', () => {

      // Arrange
      // (setup done in beforeEach)

      // Assert
      expect(colDef.headerName).toBe('Executed By');
      expect(colDef.field).toBe('executionTraderInitials');
      expect(colDef.colId).toBe('executionTraderInitials');

      expect(colDef.aggFunc).toBe(AGGREGATE_UNIQUE_VALUES);
    });
  });

  describe('cellRenderer', () => {

      // Arrange
      const colDef = createExecutionExecutedByColumnDef(mockPersonCacheService);
      const params = {
        value: 'EXE',
        node: { group: false },
      };

      // Act
      const result = colDef.cellRenderer(params);

      // Assert
      expect(result).toBe('EXE');

    it('should return aggData value when node is a group', () => {
      // Arrange

      const params = {
        node: {
          group: true,
          aggData: { executionTraderInitials: 'AGG' },
        },
      };

      // Act
      const result = colDef.cellRenderer(params);

      // Assert
      expect(result).toBe('AGG');
    });

      // Arrange

        value: 'EXE',

        location: 'body',
        api: {},
        columnApi: {},
        context: {},
      };

        mockPersonCacheService.getFullNameFromInitial as jest.Mock
      ).mockReturnValue('Executed Name');

      // Act

      ).toHaveBeenCalledWith('EXE1');

      ).toHaveBeenCalledWith('EXE2');

        value: undefined,
        node: { group: false },
        location: 'body',
        api: {},

        context: {},
      };
      (
        mockPersonCacheService.getFullNameFromInitial as jest.Mock
      ).mockReturnValue('');

File: trades-grid\feature\src\lib\column-definitions\executions\executedby-column.ts
import { ColDef, ICellRendererParams } from '@ag-grid-community/core';
import { PersonCacheService } from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/data-access/person';
import {
  AG_SET_COLUMN_FILTER,
  AGGREGATE_UNIQUE_VALUES,
  SMALL_COLUMN_SIZE,
} from '../constants';

export function createExecutionExecutedByColumnDef(
  personCacheService: PersonCacheService,
): ColDef {
  const mappingValue = 'executionTraderInitials';
  const colDef: ColDef = {
    headerName: 'Executed By',
    field: mappingValue,
    colId: mappingValue,
    minWidth: SMALL_COLUMN_SIZE,
    filter: AG_SET_COLUMN_FILTER,
    aggFunc: AGGREGATE_UNIQUE_VALUES,
    cellRenderer: (params: ICellRendererParams) => {
      if (params.node.group) {
        // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unsafe-return, @typescript-eslint/no-unsafe-member-access
        return params.node.aggData?.[mappingValue] || '';
      }
      // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unsafe-return
      return params.value || '';
    },
    tooltipValueGetter: (params): string => {
      if (params.node?.group) {
        // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unsafe-assignment, @typescript-eslint/no-unsafe-member-access
        const aggData = params.node.aggData as
          | Record<string, string>
          | undefined;
        const aggValue: string | undefined = aggData?.[mappingValue];
        if (!aggValue) {
          return '';
        }
        // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unsafe-return, @typescript-eslint/no-unsafe-call, @typescript-eslint/no-unsafe-member-access
        return aggValue
          .split(', ')
          .map((value: string) =>
            personCacheService.getFullNameFromInitial(value),
          )
          .join(', ');
      }
      if (!params.value) {
        return '';
      }
      // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unsafe-argument
      return personCacheService.getFullNameFromInitial(params.value);
    },
  };
  return colDef;
}

    aggFunc: AGGREGATE_UNIQUE_VALUES,
    cellRenderer: (params: ICellRendererParams) => {

        // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unsafe-return, @typescript-eslint/no-unsafe-member-access
        return params.node.aggData?.[mappingValue] || '';

File: trades-grid\feature\src\lib\trades-grid\grid-aggregations-utils.ts
import { IAggFunc, IAggFuncParams } from '@ag-grid-community/core';
import { TradeGridValueGetterModel } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';
import { aggregateUniqueValues } from './utils/aggregation-helpers';

export function isUniqueCurrency(params: IAggFuncParams): boolean {
  const dataSet: Set<string> = new Set();
  params.values.forEach((value: TradeGridValueGetterModel) => {
    // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/prefer-optional-chain, @typescript-eslint/no-unnecessary-condition
    if (value && value.currency) {
      dataSet.add(value.currency as string);
    }
  });
  return dataSet.size <= 1;
}

// eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
export function calcNetAmount(params: IAggFuncParams): any {
  let sumAmount = 0;
  let isNan = false;
  params.values.forEach((value: TradeGridValueGetterModel) => {
    // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unnecessary-condition
    if (value && typeof value.amount === 'number' && !isNaN(value.amount)) {
      if (value.side == 'SEL' || value.side == 'SRT') {
        sumAmount -= value.amount;
      } else {
        sumAmount += value.amount;
      }
    } else {
      isNan = true;
    }
  });
  // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unnecessary-condition
  if (isNan) return '-';
  else return sumAmount;
}

// eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
export function calcAvgPrice(params: IAggFuncParams): any {
  let isNan = false;
  let sumOfPriceAndQuantity = 0;
  let sumOfQuantity = 0;
  params.values.forEach((value: TradeGridValueGetterModel) => {
    // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unsafe-argument, @typescript-eslint/no-unnecessary-condition
    if (
      // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unnecessary-condition
      value &&
      typeof value.executionQuantity === 'number' &&
      typeof value.amount === 'number' &&
      !isNaN(value.executionQuantity) &&
      !isNaN(value.amount)
    ) {
      sumOfPriceAndQuantity += (value.executionQuantity *
        value.amount) as number;
      sumOfQuantity += value.executionQuantity as number;
    } else {
      isNan = true;
    }
  });
  // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unnecessary-condition
  if (!isNan && sumOfQuantity > 0) {
    const tradeGridValue = params.values[0] as TradeGridValueGetterModel;
    return {
      amount: (sumOfPriceAndQuantity / sumOfQuantity) as number,
      // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unnecessary-condition
      executionQuantity: tradeGridValue?.executionQuantity as number,
      // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unnecessary-condition
      currency: tradeGridValue?.currency as string,
    };
  } else {
    return { amount: '-' };
  }
}

function aggregateBrokers(params: IAggFuncParams): string {
  const result: string[] = [];
  params.values.forEach((value: string) => {
    if (value && !result.includes(value)) {
      result.push(value);
    }
  });
  result.sort();
  return result.toString().replace(/,/g, ', ');
}

// eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
function aggregateTradeSum(params: IAggFuncParams): any {
  let isNan = false;
  if (isUniqueCurrency(params) && params.values.length > 0) {
    let sum = 0;
    params.values.forEach((value: TradeGridValueGetterModel) => {
      // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unnecessary-condition
      if (value && typeof value.amount === 'number' && !isNaN(value.amount)) {
        sum += value.amount as number;
      } else {
        isNan = true;
      }
    });
    // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unnecessary-condition
    if (!isNan) {
      const tradeGridValue = params.values[0] as TradeGridValueGetterModel;
      // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unnecessary-condition
      return { currency: tradeGridValue?.currency as string, amount: sum };
    } else return { amount: '-' };
  } else {
    return { amount: '-' };
  }
}

// eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
function aggregateTradeNet(params: IAggFuncParams): any {
  if (isUniqueCurrency(params) && params.values.length > 0) {
    const tradeGridValue = params.values[0] as TradeGridValueGetterModel;
    return {
      // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unnecessary-condition
      currency: tradeGridValue?.currency as string,
      amount: calcNetAmount(params) as string,
    };
  } else {
    return { amount: '-' };
  }
}

// eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
function aggregateAvgExecutedPrice(params: IAggFuncParams): any {
  if (isUniqueCurrency(params) && params.values.length > 0) {
    const avgPrice = calcAvgPrice(params) as {
      amount: number | string;
      executionQuantity?: number;
      currency?: string;
    };
    // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unnecessary-condition
    if (typeof avgPrice === 'object' && avgPrice && 'amount' in avgPrice) {
      return {
        amount: avgPrice.amount,
        executionQuantity: avgPrice.executionQuantity,
        currency: avgPrice.currency,
      };
    } else {
      return { amount: '-' };
    }
  } else {
    return { amount: '-' };
  }
}

export function createAggFunctions(): { [key: string]: IAggFunc } {
  return {
    cancelledReason: (params: IAggFuncParams) =>
      aggregateUniqueValues(params.values as string[]),
    cancelledBy: (params: IAggFuncParams) =>
      aggregateUniqueValues(params.values as string[]),
    aggregateUniqueValues: (params: IAggFuncParams) =>
      aggregateUniqueValues(params.values as string[]),
    brokers: aggregateBrokers,
    tradeSum: aggregateTradeSum,
    tradeNet: aggregateTradeNet,
    tradeNetUSD: (params: IAggFuncParams) => {
      return { amount: calcNetAmount(params) as string };
    },
    avgExecutedPrice: aggregateAvgExecutedPrice,
  };
}

File: trades-grid\feature\src\lib\trades-grid\grid-column-utils.ts
import { ColDef, GridApi, IRowNode } from '@ag-grid-community/core';
import { defaultColDef } from '../column-definitions/shared-definition-options';
import { ExecutionModel, TradeModel } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';
import {
  fallbackCopy,
  flashAffectedRows,
} from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/util/ag-grid';

const commonColDef: ColDef = {
  ...defaultColDef,
  flex: 1,
  pinned: 'left',
  width: 50,
  minWidth: 30,
  maxWidth: 50,
  headerName: '',
  lockPosition: true,
  lockPinned: true,
  suppressMovable: true,
  suppressSizeToFit: true,
  suppressCellFlash: true,
  resizable: false,
  filter: false,
  suppressColumnsToolPanel: false,
};

export function createCheckboxColumn(): ColDef {
  return {
    ...commonColDef,
    colId: 'checkbox',
    headerCheckboxSelection: true,
    headerCheckboxSelectionFilteredOnly: true,
    checkboxSelection: true,
    showDisabledCheckboxes: true,
    field: 'checkbox',
    suppressNavigable: true,
    filter: false,
  };
}
export function createAllocationColumn(): ColDef {
  return {
    ...commonColDef,
    colId: 'allocations',
    field: 'allocations',
    cellRenderer: 'agGroupCellRenderer',
    suppressHeaderMenuButton: true,
  };
}

export function ensureColumnOrder(gridApi: GridApi): void {
  const specialColumnOrder = ['checkbox', 'allocations'];

  const existingSpecialColumns = specialColumnOrder.filter((colId) =>
    gridApi.getColumn(colId),
  );
  if (existingSpecialColumns.length === 0) return;

  const allColumns = gridApi.getAllDisplayedColumns();
  const leftPinnedColumns = allColumns.filter(
    (col) => col.getPinned() === 'left',
  );

  const specialColumnPositions = existingSpecialColumns.map((colId) => {
    const column = gridApi.getColumn(colId);
    return leftPinnedColumns.findIndex((col) => col === column);
  });

  const needsReordering = !specialColumnPositions.every(
    (pos, index) => pos === index,
  );

  if (needsReordering) {
    gridApi.moveColumns(existingSpecialColumns, 0);
  }
}

export function handleCopyTradeBlockAndExecutionId(
  gridApi: GridApi,
  event: KeyboardEvent,
  isExecutionContext: boolean,
): void {
  if (event.ctrlKey && event.key === 'i') {
    event.preventDefault();
    const selectedNodes = gridApi.getSelectedNodes();
    if (selectedNodes.length === 0) {
      const elementType = isExecutionContext ? 'execution' : 'trade';
      console.log(`No ${elementType} is selected, can't copy`);
      return;
    }
    let result = '';
    for (const selectedNode of selectedNodes) {
      let text;
      if (isExecutionContext) {
        text = extractExecutionBlockIdFromExecution(selectedNode);
      } else {
        text = extractTradeExecutionIdFromTrade(selectedNode);
      }
      result += text;
    }

    navigator.clipboard.writeText(result).catch(() => fallbackCopy(result));

    if (result.length > 0) {
      flashAffectedRows(selectedNodes, gridApi);
    }
  }
}

function extractTradeExecutionIdFromTrade(focused: IRowNode): string {
  const trade: TradeModel = focused.data as TradeModel;

  const tradeId = trade.entityId;
  const executionId = trade.execId ?? 'N/A';
  return `TradeId=${tradeId}, ExecutionId=${executionId}\n`;
}

function extractExecutionBlockIdFromExecution(focused: IRowNode): string {
  const execution: ExecutionModel = focused.data as ExecutionModel;

  const executionId = execution.executionId;
  const blockId = execution.blockId ?? 'N/A';
  return `ExecutionId=${executionId}, BlockId=${blockId}\n`;
}

File: trades-grid\feature\src\lib\trades-grid\grid-export-utils.ts
import { ProcessCellForExportParams } from '@ag-grid-community/core';

export function formatAmountForExport(params: ProcessCellForExportParams): any {
  if (
    params.column
      .getId()
      .match(
        /^(tradeGrossAmount|totalNetProceedsAmount|totalNetProceedsAmountRoot|executionPricePerUnit)$/,
      )
  ) {
    return params.value &&
      typeof params.value === 'object' &&
      params.value !== null &&
      'amount' in params.value
      ? (params.value as { amount: unknown }).amount
      : params.value;
  }
  return params.value;
}

export function processDates(params: ProcessCellForExportParams): string {
  if (
    params.column.getId().match(/^(tradeDate|settlementDate|cancelTimeStamp)$/)
  ) {
    return new Date(params.value as Date).toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
      year: 'numeric',
      month: '2-digit',
      day: '2-digit',
      timeZone: 'UTC',
    });
  } else if (
    params.column
      .getId()
      .match(
        /^(tradeGrossAmount|totalNetProceedsAmount|totalNetProceedsAmountRoot|executionPricePerUnit)$/,
      )
  ) {
    // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unsafe-member-access
    return params.value.amount as string;
  }
  return params.value as string;
}

import { getAdditionalMenuItems } from './menu-utils';
import { HarmonixService } from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/util/common';
import { Context } from 'openfin/_v2/fdc3/context';
import { IMenuActionParams, IRowNode } from '@ag-grid-community/core';

describe('menu-utils', () => {
  let mockHarmonixService: jest.Mocked<HarmonixService>;
  let mockContextItem: jest.Mock;
  let mockApi: any;
  let mockParams: IMenuActionParams<any, any>;

  // Helper function to create a mock IRowNode
  const createMockRowNode = (overrides: Partial<IRowNode> = {}): IRowNode => {
    return {
      data: null,
      group: false,
      childrenAfterFilter: undefined,
      setSelected: jest.fn(),
      isSelected: jest.fn(),
      isRowPinned: jest.fn(),
      isExpandable: jest.fn(),
      addEventListener: jest.fn(),
      removeEventListener: jest.fn(),
      resetQuickFilterAggregates: jest.fn(),
      isPixelInRange: jest.fn(),
      setChildIndex: jest.fn(),
      clearRowTopAndRowIndex: jest.fn(),
      setUiLevel: jest.fn(),
      setExpanded: jest.fn(),
      setRowTop: jest.fn(),
      setRowHeight: jest.fn(),
      setRowIndex: jest.fn(),
      setAllChildrenCount: jest.fn(),
      ...overrides,
    } as any as IRowNode;
  };

  beforeEach(() => {
    mockHarmonixService = {
      showNotification: jest.fn().mockResolvedValue(undefined),
      raiseIntent: jest.fn().mockResolvedValue(undefined),
    } as any;

      type: 'fdc3.trade',
      id: { entityId: 'TRADE123', entityType: 'T' },
      product: { id: { entityId: 'TRADE123' }, type: 'fdc3.product' },

      getSelectedNodes: jest.fn(),

      api: mockApi,

        mockHarmonixService,

      );

      expect(items[0]).toHaveProperty('name', 'Cancel Trade');
      expect(items[1]).toHaveProperty('name', 'Cancel and Adjust');
      expect(items[2]).toBe('separator');
    });

      // Arrange

        mockHarmonixService,
        mockContextItem,
        selectedCount,
      );

      // Assert
      expect(items).toHaveLength(3);
      expect(items[0]).toHaveProperty('name', 'Cancel Trades');
      expect(items[2]).toBe('separator');
    });

    it('should return menu items with "Cancel and Adjust" label when selectedNodes is undefined', () => {
      // Arrange - no selectedCount parameter

      // Act
      const items = getAdditionalMenuItems(
        mockHarmonixService,
        mockContextItem,
      );

      // Assert
      expect(items).toHaveLength(3);
      expect(items[0]).toHaveProperty('name', 'Cancel Trade');
      expect(items[1]).toHaveProperty('name', 'Cancel and Adjust');
    });

    describe('menu action behavior', () => {
      let menuAction: any;

      beforeEach(() => {
        // Arrange - Extract menu action from items
        const items = getAdditionalMenuItems(
          mockHarmonixService,
          mockContextItem,
          1,
        );
        menuAction = (items[0] as any).action;
      });

      it('should handle multiple selected trades with batch intent', async () => {
        // Arrange
        const selectedNodes = [
          createMockRowNode({ data: { entityId: 'TRADE1' } }),
          createMockRowNode({ data: { entityId: 'TRADE2' } }),
          createMockRowNode({ data: { entityId: 'TRADE3' } }),
        ];

        const consoleLogSpy = jest.spyOn(console, 'log').mockImplementation();

          expect.any(Object),
        );

        consoleLogSpy.mockRestore();
      });

      it('should handle single regular row node', async () => {
        // Arrange
        const nodeData = { entityId: 'TRADE123' };
        const mockNode = createMockRowNode({
          data: nodeData,
          group: false,
        });
        mockApi.getSelectedNodes.mockReturnValue([]);
        mockParams.node = mockNode;

        // Act
        await menuAction(mockParams);

        // Assert
        expect(mockContextItem).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
        expect(mockHarmonixService.raiseIntent).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
        // Should warn for no rows selected
        const consoleWarnSpy = jest.spyOn(console, 'warn').mockImplementation();
        await menuAction(mockParams);
        expect(consoleWarnSpy).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
          'No rows selected for cancel action',
        );
        consoleWarnSpy.mockRestore();
      });

      it('should handle group node with single child', async () => {

        const groupNode = createMockRowNode({
          group: true,
          childrenAfterFilter: [childNode],
          data: null,
        });
        mockApi.getSelectedNodes.mockReturnValue([]);
        mockParams.node = groupNode;

        // Act
        await menuAction(mockParams);

        // Assert

        expect(mockHarmonixService.raiseIntent).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
        // Should warn for no rows selected

        expect(consoleWarnSpy).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
          'No rows selected for cancel action',
        );

      });

          group: true,
          childrenAfterFilter: [
            createMockRowNode({ data: childData1 }),
            createMockRowNode({ data: childData2 }),

        // Assert
        expect(mockContextItem).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
        expect(mockHarmonixService.raiseIntent).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
        expect(consoleWarnSpy).toHaveBeenCalledWith(

          group: false,

        mockApi.getSelectedNodes.mockReturnValue([]);
