File: trades-grid\feature\src\lib\trades-grid\menu-utils.ts
import {
  HarmonixContext,
  HarmonixService,
  TradeContext,
  TradeListContext,
  EntityType,
} from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/util/common';
import { Context } from 'openfin/_v2/fdc3/context';
import { IMenuActionParams } from '@ag-grid-community/core';

import { ExecutionModel, TradeModel } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';
import {
  MENU_LABEL_CANCEL_BLOCK_EXECUTIONS,
  MENU_LABEL_CANCEL_TRADES,
  MENU_LABEL_CANCEL_TRADE,
  MENU_LABEL_UPDATE_TRADER_NOTE,
  MENU_LABEL_UPDATE_TRADER_NOTES,
  WARN_UPDATE_NOTE_DIALOG_NOT_CONFIGURED,
} from './constants/default-menu.constants';

export function isTradeCancelled(trade: TradeModel | ExecutionModel): boolean {
  const status =
    'tradeStatus' in trade
      ? trade.tradeStatus
      : 'executionStatusCode' in trade
        ? trade.executionStatusCode
        : '';
  return status === 'XC' || status === 'XA';
}
export interface EventData {
  data: TradeModel | ExecutionModel;
  entityId?: string;
  executionId?: string;
}

export interface ClickNode {
  isSelected: () => boolean;
  setSelected: (selected: boolean, clearSelection?: boolean) => void;
  group?: boolean;
  allLeafChildren?: ClickNode[];
  childrenAfterFilter?: ClickNode[];
  data?: unknown;

  [key: string]: any;
}

function toHarmonixContext(context: Context): HarmonixContext {
  return { ...context };
}

export function createTradeContext(eventData: EventData): TradeContext {
  let entityId = eventData.entityId;
  let entityType: EntityType = EntityType.TRADE;
  // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unnecessary-condition
  if (!entityId && eventData.data) {
    if ('entityId' in eventData.data) {
      entityId = (eventData.data as TradeModel).entityId;
      entityType = EntityType.TRADE;
    } else if ('executionId' in eventData.data) {
      entityId = (eventData.data as ExecutionModel).executionId;
      entityType = EntityType.EXECUTION;
    }
  } else if (eventData.executionId) {
    entityId = eventData.executionId;
    entityType = EntityType.EXECUTION;
  }

  return {
    type: 'fdc3.trade',
    id: {
      entityId: entityId as string,
      entityType,
    },
    product: {
      id: {
        entityId: entityId as string,
      },
      type: 'fdc3.product',
    },
  };
}

export function createTradeListContext(
  selectedData: EventData[],
): TradeListContext {
  const trades = selectedData.map((eventData: EventData) => {
    const entityId = eventData.entityId || eventData.executionId;
    const entityType: EntityType = eventData.executionId
      ? EntityType.EXECUTION
      : EntityType.TRADE;

    return {
      type: 'fdc3.trade' as const,
      id: {
        entityId: entityId as string,
        entityType,
      },
    } as TradeContext;
  });

  return {
    type: 'fdc3.tradeList',
    trades,
  };
}

export function handleContextMenuSelection(clickedNode: ClickNode): void {
  const isClickedRowSelected = clickedNode.isSelected();

  if (isClickedRowSelected) {
    return;
  }

  if (clickedNode.group) {
    const allChildren = (clickedNode.allLeafChildren || []) as Array<{
      isSelected: () => boolean;
      setSelected: (selected: boolean, clearSelection?: boolean) => void;
    }>;
    const selectedChildren = allChildren.filter((child) => child.isSelected());
    const isPartiallySelected =
      selectedChildren.length > 0 &&
      selectedChildren.length < allChildren.length;
    const isNotSelected = selectedChildren.length === 0;

    if (isNotSelected || isPartiallySelected) {
      allChildren.forEach((child) => {
        child.setSelected(true, false);
      });
      clickedNode.setSelected(true, false);
    }
  } else {
    clickedNode.setSelected(true, false);
  }
}
// eslint-disable-next-line max-lines-per-function
export function getAdditionalMenuItems(
  harmonixService: HarmonixService,
  contextItem: (event: any) => Context,
  selectedNodes?: number,
  openCancelDialog?: () => void,
  selectedType: 'trade' | 'execution' = 'trade',
  openUpdateNoteDialog?: () => void,
): any[] {
  const menuLabel =
    selectedType === 'execution'
      ? MENU_LABEL_CANCEL_BLOCK_EXECUTIONS
      : (selectedNodes ?? 0) > 1
        ? MENU_LABEL_CANCEL_TRADES
        : MENU_LABEL_CANCEL_TRADE;
  const menuItems = [
    {
      name: menuLabel,
      // eslint-disable-next-line max-lines-per-function
      action: async (params: IMenuActionParams<any, any>) => {
        // eslint-disable-next-line
        if (!params.api || typeof params.api.getSelectedNodes !== 'function') {
          return;
        }
        const selectedNodes = params.api.getSelectedNodes();

        const hasCancelled = selectedNodes.some(
          (node) =>
            node.data &&
            isTradeCancelled(node.data as TradeModel | ExecutionModel),
        );
        if (hasCancelled) {
          console.warn(
            'Cannot Cancel: One or more selected trades are already cancelled (XC/XA).',
          );
          return;
        }
        if (selectedNodes.length > 1) {
          if (openCancelDialog) {
            openCancelDialog();
          } else {
            const selectedData: EventData[] = selectedNodes
              .filter((node) => node.data)
              .map((node) => {
                const data = node.data as TradeModel | ExecutionModel;
                return {
                  data,
                  entityId:
                    selectedType === 'trade'
                      ? (data as TradeModel).entityId
                      : (data as ExecutionModel).executionId,
                  executionId:
                    selectedType === 'execution'
                      ? (data as ExecutionModel).executionId
                      : undefined,
                };
              });

            if (selectedData.length > 0) {
              try {
                const batchContext = createTradeListContext(selectedData);
                await harmonixService.raiseIntent(
                  'CancelAdjustBatchTrade',
                  toHarmonixContext(batchContext),
                );
                console.log(
                  `Raised batch intent for ${selectedData.length} ${selectedType}s`,
                );
              } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error raising batch intent:', error);
              }
            }
          }
        } else if (selectedNodes.length === 1) {
          if (openCancelDialog) {
            openCancelDialog();
          } else {
            const rowNode = params.node;
            if (rowNode) {
              let eventData: { data: unknown };
              if (rowNode.group && rowNode.childrenAfterFilter?.length === 1) {
                eventData = { data: rowNode.childrenAfterFilter[0].data };
              } else if (rowNode.data) {
                eventData = { data: rowNode.data };
              } else {
                console.warn('No valid data found in row node');
                return;
              }
              try {
                const context = contextItem(eventData);
                await harmonixService.raiseIntent(
                  'CancelAdjustSingleTrade',
                  toHarmonixContext(context),
                );
              } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error raising intent:', error);
              }
            } else {
              console.warn('No row data found for cancel action');
            }
          }
        } else {
          console.warn('No rows selected for cancel action');
        }
      },
    },
    {
      name: 'Cancel and Adjust',
      action: async (params: IMenuActionParams<TradeModel, ExecutionModel>) => {
        // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unnecessary-condition
        if (!params.api || typeof params.api.getSelectedNodes !== 'function') {
          return;
        }

        const selectedNodes = params.api.getSelectedNodes();

        if (selectedNodes.length > 1) {
          const selectedData: EventData[] = selectedNodes
            .filter((node) => node.data)
            .map((node) => {
              const data = node.data as TradeModel | ExecutionModel;
              return {
                data,
                entityId:
                  selectedType === 'trade'
                    ? (data as TradeModel).entityId
                    : (data as ExecutionModel).executionId,
                executionId:
                  selectedType === 'execution'
                    ? (data as ExecutionModel).executionId
                    : undefined,
              };
            });

          if (selectedData.length > 0) {
            try {
              const batchContext = createTradeListContext(selectedData);
              await harmonixService.raiseIntent(
                'CancelAdjustBatchTrade',
                toHarmonixContext(batchContext),
              );
              console.log(
                `Raised batch cancel/adjust intent for ${selectedData.length} ${selectedType}s`,
              );
            } catch (error) {
              console.error('Error raising batch intent:', error);
            }
          }
        } else if (selectedNodes.length === 1) {
          const rowNode = params.node;
          if (rowNode) {
            let eventData: { data: unknown };
            if (rowNode.group && rowNode.childrenAfterFilter?.length === 1) {
              eventData = { data: rowNode.childrenAfterFilter[0].data };
            } else if (rowNode.data) {
              eventData = { data: rowNode.data };
            } else {
              console.warn('No valid data found in row node');
              return;
            }
            try {
              const context = contextItem(eventData);

              await harmonixService.raiseIntent(
                'CancelAdjustSingleTrade',
                toHarmonixContext(context),
              );
            } catch (error) {
              console.error('Error raising intent:', error);
            }
          }
        } else {
          console.warn('No rows selected for cancel and adjust action');
        }
      },
    },
  ];
  if (selectedType === 'execution') {
    menuItems.push({
      name:
        (selectedNodes ?? 0) > 1
          ? MENU_LABEL_UPDATE_TRADER_NOTES
          : MENU_LABEL_UPDATE_TRADER_NOTE,
      action: async (params: IMenuActionParams<any, any>): Promise<void> => {
        if (typeof params.api.getSelectedNodes !== 'function') {
          return;
        }
        if (openUpdateNoteDialog) {
          openUpdateNoteDialog();
        } else {
          console.warn(WARN_UPDATE_NOTE_DIALOG_NOT_CONFIGURED);
        }
      },
    });
  }
  const menuItemsWithSeparators = [...menuItems, 'separator'];
  return menuItemsWithSeparators;
}

.exac-grid-container {
  display: flex;
  flex-direction: column;

  eqt-common-grid-component {

  afterEach(() => {

    (document as any).execCommand = originalExecCommand;
    jest.resetAllMocks();

  describe('Copy executionId and blockId from execution', () => {
    it('should copy selected Execution ids to clipboard using clipboard API when isExecutionsContext=true', async () => {
      // Arrange
      const writeTextMock = jest.fn().mockResolvedValue(undefined);
      (navigator as any).clipboard = { writeText: writeTextMock };

      component.isExecutionsContext = true;
      component.gridApi = {
        getSelectedNodes: jest.fn().mockReturnValue([
          { rowIndex: 1, data: { executionId: 'E1', blockId: 'B1' } },
          { rowIndex: 2, data: { executionId: 'E2', blockId: 'B2' } },
        ]),
        flashCells: jest.fn(),
        getDisplayedRowAtIndex: jest.fn().mockImplementation((idx) => {
          return { rowIndex: idx };
        }),
      } as any;

      const keyboardEvent = {
        key: 'i',
        ctrlKey: true,
        metaKey: false,
        preventDefault: jest.fn(),
      } as any;

      // Act
      await component.handleKeyboardEvent(keyboardEvent);

      // Assert
      expect(keyboardEvent.preventDefault).toHaveBeenCalled();
      expect(writeTextMock).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
        'ExecutionId=E1, BlockId=B1\nExecutionId=E2, BlockId=B2\n',
      );
    });

    it('should fallback to document.execCommand when clipboard throws an error and isExecutionsContext=true', async () => {
      // Arrange
      const writeTextMock = jest
        .fn()
        .mockRejectedValue(new Error('Clipboard error'));
      (navigator as any).clipboard = { writeText: writeTextMock };
      const execSpy = jest.fn().mockReturnValue(true);
      (document as any).execCommand = execSpy;

      component.isExecutionsContext = true;
      component.gridApi = {
        getSelectedNodes: jest
          .fn()
          .mockReturnValue([
            { rowIndex: 0, data: { executionId: 'E0', blockId: 'B0' } },
          ]),
        flashCells: jest.fn(),
        getDisplayedRowAtIndex: jest.fn().mockImplementation((idx) => {
          return { rowIndex: idx };
        }),
      } as any;

      const keyboardEvent = {
        key: 'i',
        ctrlKey: true,
        metaKey: false,
        preventDefault: jest.fn(),
      } as any;

      // Act
      component.handleKeyboardEvent(keyboardEvent);

      // Wait for the async rejection -> catch -> fallbackCopy to execute
      await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 0));

      // Assert
      expect(keyboardEvent.preventDefault).toHaveBeenCalled();
      expect(writeTextMock).toHaveBeenCalled();
      expect(execSpy).toHaveBeenCalledWith('copy');
    });

    it('should not attempt copy when no nodes selected but should prevent default (isExecutionsContext=true)', () => {
      // Arrange
      const writeTextMock = jest.fn().mockResolvedValue(undefined);
      (navigator as any).clipboard = { writeText: writeTextMock };
      const execSpy = jest.fn().mockReturnValue(true);
      (document as any).execCommand = execSpy;

      component.isExecutionsContext = true;
      component.gridApi = {
        getSelectedNodes: jest.fn().mockReturnValue([]),
        getDisplayedRowAtIndex: jest.fn(),
        flashCells: jest.fn(),
      } as any;

      const keyboardEvent = {
        key: 'i',
        ctrlKey: true,
        metaKey: false,
        preventDefault: jest.fn(),
      } as any;

      // Act
      component.handleKeyboardEvent(keyboardEvent);

      // Assert
      expect(keyboardEvent.preventDefault).toHaveBeenCalled();
      expect(writeTextMock).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
      expect(execSpy).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
    });
  });

  describe('Copy tradeId and executionId from trade', () => {
    it('should copy selected Trade ids to clipboard using clipboard API when isExecutionsContext=false', async () => {
      // Arrange
      const writeTextMock = jest.fn().mockResolvedValue(undefined);
      (navigator as any).clipboard = { writeText: writeTextMock };

      component.isExecutionsContext = false;
      component.gridApi = {
        getSelectedNodes: jest.fn().mockReturnValue([
          { rowIndex: 1, data: { entityId: 'T1', execId: 'E1' } },
          { rowIndex: 2, data: { entityId: 'T2', execId: 'E2' } },
        ]),
        flashCells: jest.fn(),
        getDisplayedRowAtIndex: jest.fn().mockImplementation((idx) => {
          // Return the node itself for simplicity
          return { rowIndex: idx };
        }),
      } as any;

      const keyboardEvent = {
        key: 'i',
        ctrlKey: true,
        metaKey: false,
        preventDefault: jest.fn(),
      } as any;

      // Act
      await component.handleKeyboardEvent(keyboardEvent);

      // Assert
      expect(keyboardEvent.preventDefault).toHaveBeenCalled();
      expect(writeTextMock).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
        'TradeId=T1, ExecutionId=E1\nTradeId=T2, ExecutionId=E2\n',
      );
    });

    it('should fallback to document.execCommand when clipboard throws an error and isExecutionsContext=false', async () => {
      // Arrange
      const writeTextMock = jest
        .fn()
        .mockRejectedValue(new Error('Clipboard error'));
      (navigator as any).clipboard = { writeText: writeTextMock };
      const execSpy = jest.fn().mockReturnValue(true);
      (document as any).execCommand = execSpy;

      component.gridApi = {
        getSelectedNodes: jest
          .fn()
          .mockReturnValue([
            { rowIndex: 0, data: { entityId: 'T0', execId: 'E0' } },
          ]),
        flashCells: jest.fn(),
        getDisplayedRowAtIndex: jest.fn().mockImplementation((idx) => {
          return { rowIndex: idx };
        }),
      } as any;
      component.isExecutionsContext = false;

      const keyboardEvent = {
        key: 'i',
        ctrlKey: true,
        metaKey: false,
        preventDefault: jest.fn(),
      } as any;

      // Act
      component.handleKeyboardEvent(keyboardEvent);

      // Wait for the async rejection -> catch -> fallbackCopy to execute
      await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 0));

      // Assert
      expect(keyboardEvent.preventDefault).toHaveBeenCalled();
      expect(writeTextMock).toHaveBeenCalled();
      expect(execSpy).toHaveBeenCalledWith('copy');
    });

    it('should not attempt copy when no nodes selected but should prevent default (isExecutionsContext=false)', () => {
      // Arrange
      const writeTextMock = jest.fn().mockResolvedValue(undefined);
      (navigator as any).clipboard = { writeText: writeTextMock };
      const execSpy = jest.fn().mockReturnValue(true);
      (document as any).execCommand = execSpy;

      component.gridApi = {
        getSelectedNodes: jest.fn().mockReturnValue([]),
        getDisplayedRowAtIndex: jest.fn(),
        flashCells: jest.fn(),
      } as any;
      component.isExecutionsContext = false;

      const keyboardEvent = {
        key: 'i',
        ctrlKey: true,
        metaKey: false,
        preventDefault: jest.fn(),
      } as any;

      // Act
      component.handleKeyboardEvent(keyboardEvent);

      // Assert
      expect(keyboardEvent.preventDefault).toHaveBeenCalled();
      expect(writeTextMock).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
      expect(execSpy).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
    });
  });
});

  handleContextMenuSelection,
} from './menu-utils';
import { createAggFunctions } from './grid-aggregations-utils';
import { formatAmountForExport, processDates } from './grid-export-utils';
import {
  createAllocationColumn,
  createCheckboxColumn,
  ensureColumnOrder,
  handleCopyTradeBlockAndExecutionId,
} from './grid-column-utils';
import {
  autoGroupColumnDef,
  createTradesGridOptions,
  defaultColDef,
} from '../column-definitions/shared-definition-options';

import { ExecutionModel, TradeModel } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';
import { GridOptions, RowClickedEvent } from 'ag-grid-community';
import { IprefName } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/trades-grid/data';
import { AllocationDetailRendererComponent } from '../allocation-detail-renderer/allocation-detail-renderer.component';
import { AllocationRenderComponent } from './cell-renderers/allocation-render.component';
import {
  CancelOutrightComponent,
  CancelResult,
  MultiCancelDialogData,
  UpdateTraderNoteComponent,
  UpdateTraderNoteDialogData,
  UpdateTraderNoteResult,
} from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/ui';
import { getTradesColumnDef } from '../column-definitions/trades-column-defs';
import { PersonCacheService } from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/data-access/person';
import { getExecutionsColumnDef } from '../column-definitions/executions-column-defs';

@Component({
  selector: 'exac-trades-grid',
  templateUrl: './trades-grid.component.html',
  styleUrls: ['./trades-grid.component.scss'],
  standalone: false,
})
export class TradesGridComponent implements OnInit, OnDestroy {
  @Input() public cancelAndAdjustServiceUrl = '/api/xa/service/cancel/%TYPE%';

  public data$!: Observable<TradeModel[] | ExecutionModel[]>;
  public isLoadingData$: Observable<boolean>;
  public gridApi!: GridApi;
  public expand: BehaviorSubject<boolean> = new BehaviorSubject<boolean>(false);
  public isGridLoading = true;
  public enablePivot = false;
  public hideIcons = [Icon.REFRESH];
  public title = 'Fund Executions';
  public retainSelectionOnGrouping = true;
  public additionalMenuItems: (string | MenuItemDef)[] = [];
  public isGrouped$ = new BehaviorSubject<boolean>(false);

  public aggFuncs = createAggFunctions();
  public isExecutionsContext = false;
  public iPrefAppName = IprefName.Trades;
  public detailCellRenderer = AllocationDetailRendererComponent;
  public currentlyExpandedRowId = '';
  public defaultColDef = defaultColDef;
  public gridOptions: GridOptions<TradeModel | ExecutionModel> =
    createTradesGridOptions(
      {
        onFirstDataRendered: (params: FirstDataRenderedEvent): void =>
          this.onFirstDataRendered(params),
        onRowClicked: (event: RowClickedEvent<TradeModel | ExecutionModel>) =>
          this.onRowClicked(event),
        onSelectionChanged: () => {
          this.updateAdditionalMenuItems();
        },
        onColumnRowGroupChanged: () => {
          // eslint-disable-next-line
          if (this.gridApi) {
            this.isGrouped$.next(this.gridApi.getRowGroupColumns().length > 0);

            this.isGrouped$.subscribe((isGrouped: boolean) => {
              this.gridApi.setColumnsVisible(
                ['checkbox', 'allocations'],
                !isGrouped,
              );
            });

            if (!this.retainSelectionOnGrouping) {
              this.gridApi.deselectAll();
            }
          }
        },
        onCellMouseDown: (event: CellMouseDownEvent) => {
          const evt = event.event;
          if (evt instanceof MouseEvent && evt.button === 2) {
            this.handleContextMenuSelection({ node: event.node });
          }
        },
        onColumnPinned: () => {
          // eslint-disable-next-line
          if (this.gridApi) {
            setTimeout(() => ensureColumnOrder(this.gridApi), 0);
          }
        },
      },
      {
        loadingOverlayComponent: LoadingOverlayComponent,
        processDates: processDates,
        formatAmountForExport: formatAmountForExport,
        aggFuncs: this.aggFuncs,
      },
    );

  public autoGroupColumnDef = {
    ...autoGroupColumnDef,
    headerCheckboxSelection: true,
    headerCheckboxSelectionFilteredOnly: true,
    suppressMovable: true,
    lockPosition: true,
    pinned: 'left' as const,
    cellRendererParams: {
      suppressCount: false,
      innerRenderer: AllocationRenderComponent,
    },
    checkboxSelection: (
      params: CheckboxSelectionCallbackParams<
        TradeModel | ExecutionModel,
        unknown
      >,
    ) => {
      const firstGroupColFId = this.gridApi
        .getRowGroupColumns()[0]
        ?.getColDef()?.colId;
      return params.colDef.colId === `ag-Grid-AutoColumn-${firstGroupColFId}`;
    },
    cellClass: (params: { colDef: ColDef }) => {
      const firstGroupColFId = this.gridApi
        .getRowGroupColumns()[0]
        ?.getColDef()?.colId;
      return params.colDef.colId === `ag-Grid-AutoColumn-${firstGroupColFId}`
        ? null
        : 'not-first-group-col';
    },
    showDisabledCheckboxes: true,
  };

  public columnDefs: ColDef[] = [];

  public readonly gridTheme = computed(() =>
    this.harmonixService.theme().name === 'dark'
      ? 'ag-theme-balham-dark'
      : 'ag-theme-balham',
  );

  private readonly destroy$ = new Subject();

  public constructor(
    private readonly route: ActivatedRoute,
    private readonly store: Store,
    private readonly harmonixService: HarmonixService,
    private readonly dialog: MatDialog,
    private readonly personCacheService: PersonCacheService,
  ) {}

  public get isGrouped(): boolean {
    return this.gridApi.getRowGroupColumns().length > 0;
  }

  /**
   * Listening to the key combo CTRL+I to allow
   * for copying of tradeId of the currently focused cell
   *
   * @param event Keyboard Event
   */
  @HostListener('document:keydown', ['$event'])
  public handleKeyboardEvent(event: KeyboardEvent): void {
    handleCopyTradeBlockAndExecutionId(
      this.gridApi,
      event,
      this.isExecutionsContext,
    );
  }

  public onRowClicked(
    event: RowClickedEvent<TradeModel | ExecutionModel>,
  ): void {
    const data = event.data;
    if (!data) {
      console.warn('Row clicked with no data:', event);
      return;
    }

    const entityId = this.isExecutionsContext
      ? (data as ExecutionModel).executionId
      : (data as TradeModel).entityId;

    if (!entityId) {
      console.warn('Row clicked without valid entityId or executionId:', data);
      return;
    }

    const eventData: EventData = { data, entityId };

    const context: Context = this.contextItem(eventData);
    setWorkspaceContext(this.harmonixService, context);
  }

  public ngOnInit(): void {
    this.route.queryParams
      .pipe(
        takeUntil(this.destroy$),
        switchMap((params: Params) => {
          if (params[gridViewQParams] === GridView.Executions) {
            this.initExecutionsContext();
          } else {
            this.initTradesContext();
            this.updateAdditionalMenuItems();
          }
          return this.isLoadingData$;
        }),
      )
      .subscribe((isLoading: boolean) => {
        this.showOverlay(isLoading);
      });
  }

  public onFirstDataRendered(params: FirstDataRenderedEvent): void {
    if (this.enablePivot) {
      params.api.createPivotChart({
        chartType: 'stackedColumn',
        chartContainer: document.querySelector('#myChart') as HTMLElement,
        chartThemeOverrides: {
          common: {
            navigator: {
              enabled: true,
              height: 10,
            },
          },
        },
      });
      // expand one row for demonstration purposes
      requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        params.api.getDisplayedRowAtIndex(2)?.setExpanded(true);
      });
    }
  }

  public onGridReady(grid: GridReadyEvent): void {
    this.gridApi = grid.api;
    ensureColumnOrder(this.gridApi);
    this.isGridLoading = false;

    // Check initial grouping state and update column visibility
    const initialGroupingState = this.gridApi.getRowGroupColumns().length > 0;
    this.isGrouped$.next(initialGroupingState);
    this.gridApi.setColumnsVisible(
      ['checkbox', 'allocations'],
      !initialGroupingState,
    );
  }

  public toggleRetainSelection(): void {
    this.retainSelectionOnGrouping = !this.retainSelectionOnGrouping;
  }

  private updateAdditionalMenuItems(): void {
    // eslint-disable-next-line
    const selectedCount = this.gridApi?.getSelectedNodes()?.length ?? 0;

    const selectedType: 'trade' | 'execution' = this.isExecutionsContext
      ? 'execution'
      : 'trade';
    this.additionalMenuItems = getAdditionalMenuItems(
      this.harmonixService,
      (event: { data: EventData }) => this.contextItem(event.data),
      selectedCount,
      () => this.openCancelDialog(),
      selectedType,
      () => this.openUpdateNoteDialog(),
    ) as (string | MenuItemDef)[];
  }

  private handleContextMenuSelection(params: { node: any }): void {
    handleContextMenuSelection(params.node as ClickNode);
  }

  public ngOnDestroy(): void {
    this.destroy$.next(true);
    this.destroy$.complete();
  }

  public openCancelDialog(): void {
    const selectedNodes = this.gridApi.getSelectedNodes();
    const selectedTrades: TradeModel[] = [];
    const selectedExecutions: ExecutionModel[] = [];

    selectedNodes.forEach((node) => {
      if (node.data) {
        if (this.isExecutionsContext) {
          selectedExecutions.push(node.data as ExecutionModel);
        } else {
          selectedTrades.push(node.data as TradeModel);
        }
      }
    });

    const cancelType: 'trades' | 'executions' | 'mixed' = this
      .isExecutionsContext
      ? 'executions'
      : selectedTrades.length > 0 && selectedExecutions.length > 0
        ? 'mixed'
        : selectedTrades.length > 0
          ? 'trades'
          : 'executions';

    const dialogData: MultiCancelDialogData = {
      selectedTrades,
      selectedExecutions,
      cancelType,
      cancelServiceUrl: this.cancelAndAdjustServiceUrl,
    };

    const dialogRef = CancelOutrightComponent.open(this.dialog, dialogData, {
      width: '600px',
    });

    dialogRef
      .afterClosed()
      .pipe(takeUntil(this.destroy$))
      .subscribe((result: CancelResult | undefined) => {
        if (result?.success) {
          console.log('Cancel operation completed successfully:', result);
          // Optionally refresh the grid data here
          // this.gridApi.refreshInfiniteCache();
        }
      });
  }

  public openUpdateNoteDialog(): void {
    const selectedNodes = this.gridApi.getSelectedNodes();
    const selectedExecutions: ExecutionModel[] = [];

    selectedNodes.forEach((node) => {
      if (node.data && this.isExecutionsContext) {
        selectedExecutions.push(node.data as ExecutionModel);
      }
    });

    if (selectedExecutions.length === 0) {
      return;
    }

    const dialogData: UpdateTraderNoteDialogData = {
      executions: selectedExecutions,
      changeServiceUrl: this.cancelAndAdjustServiceUrl,
    };

    const dialogRef = this.dialog.open<
      UpdateTraderNoteComponent,
      UpdateTraderNoteDialogData,
      UpdateTraderNoteResult
    >(UpdateTraderNoteComponent, {
      width: '600px',
      data: dialogData,
      disableClose: false,
      panelClass: 'cancel-dialog-container',
    });

    dialogRef.afterClosed().subscribe((result) => {
      if (result?.success) {
        console.log(
          `Successfully updated trader notes for ${result.updatedCount} execution(s)`,
        );
      } else if (result?.error) {
        console.error('Failed to update trader notes:', result.error);
      }
    });
  }

  private contextItem(eventData: EventData): Context {
    return createTradeContext(eventData);
  }

  private initExecutionsContext(): void {
    this.title = 'Block Executions';
    this.isExecutionsContext = true;
    this.iPrefAppName = IprefName.Executions;
    this.data$ = this.store.select(executionsSelectors.getAllExecutions);
    this.isLoadingData$ = this.store.select(
      executionsSelectors.isExecutionsLoading,
    );
    this.columnDefs = this.getColumnDefs(
      getExecutionsColumnDef(this.personCacheService),
    );
    this.enableMasterDetailAllocations();
    this.updateAdditionalMenuItems();
  }

  private initTradesContext(): void {
    this.data$ = this.store.select(tradesSelectors.getAllTrades);
    this.isLoadingData$ = this.store.select(tradesSelectors.isTradesLoading);
    this.columnDefs = this.getColumnDefs(
      getTradesColumnDef(this.personCacheService),
    );
  }

  private enableMasterDetailAllocations(): void {
    this.gridOptions = {
      ...this.gridOptions,
      masterDetail: true,
      keepDetailRows: false,
      detailCellRenderer: this.detailCellRenderer,
      embedFullWidthRows: false,
      groupDefaultExpanded: 0,
      detailCellRendererParams: {
        suppressCallback: (params: { node: { group: boolean } }) => {
          return params.node.group;
        },
      },
    };

    this.isGrouped$.subscribe((isGrouped: boolean) => {
      if (!isGrouped) {
        this.insertAllocationColumn();
      } else {
        this.gridApi.setColumnsVisible(['checkbox', 'allocations'], false);
      }
    });
  }

  private insertAllocationColumn(): void {
    const allocationCol = createAllocationColumn();
    const checkboxIndex = this.columnDefs.findIndex(
      (col) => col.colId === 'checkbox',
    );

    if (checkboxIndex >= 0) {
      this.columnDefs.splice(checkboxIndex + 1, 0, allocationCol);
    } else {
      this.columnDefs.unshift(allocationCol);
    }
  }

  private getColumnDefs(baseDefs: ColDef[]): ColDef[] {
    this.isGrouped$.subscribe((isGrouped: boolean) => {
      if (isGrouped) {
        return [...baseDefs];
      }
      return [createCheckboxColumn(), ...baseDefs];
    });
    return [createCheckboxColumn(), ...baseDefs];
  }

  private showOverlay(isLoading: boolean): void {
    if (isLoading) {
      this.gridApi.showLoadingOverlay();
    } else {
      // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unnecessary-condition
      this.gridApi?.hideOverlay();
    }
  }
}

File: trades-grid\feature\src\lib\trades-grid\cell-renderers\allocation-render.component.ts
import { Component, ChangeDetectorRef, OnDestroy, NgZone } from '@angular/core';

import { ICellRendererAngularComp } from '@ag-grid-community/angular';
import { ICellRendererParams } from '@ag-grid-community/core';

@Component({
  selector: 'exac-allocation-render',
  imports: [],
  templateUrl: './allocation-render.component.html',
  styleUrl: './allocation-render.component.scss',
})
export class AllocationRenderComponent
  implements ICellRendererAngularComp, OnDestroy
{
  public params!: ICellRendererParams;
  public isGroup = false;
  public isExpandable = false;
  public isExpanded = false;
  public label = '';

  private expansionCheckInterval: ReturnType<typeof setInterval> | null = null;

  public constructor(
    private readonly cd: ChangeDetectorRef,
    private readonly ngZone: NgZone,
  ) {}

  private updateState(params: ICellRendererParams): void {
    this.params = params;
    this.isGroup = !!params.node.group;

    const rowGroupColumns = params.api.getRowGroupColumns();
    const currentColId = params.colDef?.colId ?? params.colDef?.field;
    const lastGroupCol =
      rowGroupColumns.length > 0
        ? rowGroupColumns[rowGroupColumns.length - 1]
        : null;

    const isLastGroupColumn =
      !!lastGroupCol &&
      `ag-Grid-AutoColumn-${lastGroupCol.getColDef().colId}` === currentColId;

    const hasMasterDetail = !!params.api.getGridOption('masterDetail');
    const isLeafNode = !this.isGroup && !!params.node.data && isLastGroupColumn;
    const isMasterDetailNode = isLeafNode && hasMasterDetail;

    this.isExpandable = isMasterDetailNode;
    this.isExpanded = isMasterDetailNode ? params.node.expanded : false;

    this.label = this.isGroup
      ? typeof params.value === 'string'
        ? params.value
        : typeof params.node.key === 'string'
          ? params.node.key
          : 'Blank'
      : typeof params.value === 'string'
        ? params.value
        : '';
  }

  public agInit(params: ICellRendererParams): void {
    this.updateState(params);
    this.startExpansionTracking();
  }

  public refresh(params: ICellRendererParams): boolean {
    this.updateState(params);
    return true;
  }

  public ngOnDestroy(): void {
    this.stopExpansionTracking();
  }

  private startExpansionTracking(): void {
    this.ngZone.runOutsideAngular(() => {
      this.expansionCheckInterval = setInterval(() => {
        if (this.isExpandable) {
          const currentExpansion = this.params.node.expanded;
          if (currentExpansion !== this.isExpanded) {
            this.ngZone.run(() => {
              this.isExpanded = currentExpansion;
              this.cd.markForCheck();
            });
          }
        }
      }, 100);
    });
  }

  private stopExpansionTracking(): void {
    if (this.expansionCheckInterval) {
      clearInterval(this.expansionCheckInterval as unknown as number);
      this.expansionCheckInterval = null;
    }
  }

  public toggleExpand(event: MouseEvent): void {
    event.stopPropagation();
    event.preventDefault();
    this.params.node.setExpanded(!this.params.node.expanded);
    this.isExpanded = !this.isExpanded;
  }
}

File: trades-grid\feature\src\lib\trades-grid\utils\aggregation-helpers.spec.ts
import { aggregateUniqueValues } from './aggregation-helpers';

describe('aggregateUniqueValues', () => {
  it('should aggregate unique values with default options', () => {
    const values = ['text1', 'text2', 'text1', 'text3'];
    const result = aggregateUniqueValues(values);
    expect(result).toBe('text1, text2, text3');
  });

  it('should exclude empty strings by default', () => {
    const values = ['text1', '', 'text2', ''];
    const result = aggregateUniqueValues(values);
    expect(result).toBe('text1, text2');
  });
});

File: trades-grid\feature\src\lib\trades-grid\utils\aggregation-helpers.ts
/**
 * Aggregates unique non-empty values from an array of strings.
 * Handles comma-separated values by splitting them into individual items.
 * @param values - Array of string values to aggregate (may contain comma-separated values)
 * @param options - Optional configuration for formatting
 * @returns Comma-separated string of unique sorted values
 */
export function aggregateUniqueValues(
  values: string[],
  options?: {
    excludeEmpty?: boolean;
    excludeNull?: boolean;
    sort?: boolean;
    separator?: string;
  },
): string {
  const {
    excludeEmpty = true,
    excludeNull = true,
    sort = true,
    separator = ', ',
  } = options || {};

  const uniqueValues = new Set<string>();

  values.forEach((value: string) => {
    // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unnecessary-condition
    if (value == null) {
      return;
    }

    if (value.includes(',')) {
      value.split(',').forEach((v) => {
        const trimmed = v.trim();
        if (!excludeEmpty || trimmed !== '') {
          uniqueValues.add(trimmed);
        }
      });
    } else {
      const trimmed = value.trim();
      if (!excludeEmpty || trimmed !== '') {
        uniqueValues.add(trimmed);
      }
    }
  });

  const result = Array.from(uniqueValues);

  if (sort) {
    result.sort();
  }

  return result.join(separator);
}

  describe('cancelledTrades', () => {

    });
  });

  it('should track SearchClicked event on getTrades triggered', () => {
    // Arrange
    const dateVal = new Date('2023-09-26T22:38:39.819Z');
    service.areCancelledTradesEnabled = false;
    service.startDateValue = new Date(dateVal);
    service.endDateValue = new Date(dateVal);
    service.datePickingMethod = DateSelectionType.DatePicker;
    const searchRequest: TradeSearchRequest = {
      fmrIssueCusips: ['DDB509000'],
      fmrFundNumbers: undefined,
      startDate: '2023-09-26',
      endDate: '2023-09-26',
      parentTradingDeskShortNames: [fmreq, fmrcy],
      statuses: allStatusesTrades,
      traderPersonSourceIds: undefined,
      fmrSymbols: [],
      ivTypeCodes: ['sdsd', 'sd'],
      brokerFirmSourceIds: [2434, 123],
    };

    const trackingEvent: TrackingEvent = {
      action: TrackingEventName.SearchClicked,
      appModule: 'Trades Search',
      additionalAttributes: {
        includeCancelled: false,
        dateRange: service.getDateRangeLiteral(),
        dateRangeType: service.datePickingMethod,
        searchFields: service.getUsedSearchFieldsArray(searchRequest),
        interactionType: service.interactionType?.toString(),
      },
    };
    const trackEventSpy = jest.spyOn(trackingService, 'trackEvent');
    jest
      .spyOn(service, 'getTradesRequestPayload')
      .mockReturnValue(searchRequest);

    // Act
    service.getTrades();

    // Assert
    expect(trackEventSpy).toHaveBeenCalledWith(trackingEvent);
  });

  it('should track ClearParamsClicked event on clearTrades triggered', () => {
    // Arrange
    const dateVal = new Date('2023-09-26T22:38:39.819Z');
    service.areCancelledTradesEnabled = false;
    service.startDateValue = new Date(dateVal);
    service.endDateValue = new Date(dateVal);
    service.datePickingMethod = DateSelectionType.DatePicker;
    const searchRequest: TradeSearchRequest = {
      fmrIssueCusips: ['DDB509000'],
      fmrFundNumbers: undefined,
      startDate: '2023-09-26',
      endDate: '2023-09-26',
      parentTradingDeskShortNames: [fmreq, fmrcy],
      statuses: allStatusesTrades,
      traderPersonSourceIds: undefined,
      fmrSymbols: [],
      ivTypeCodes: ['sdsd', 'sd'],
      brokerFirmSourceIds: [2434, 123],
    };

    const trackingEvent: TrackingEvent = {
      action: TrackingEventName.ClearParamsClicked,
      appModule: 'Trades Search',
      additionalAttributes: {
        includeCancelled: false,
        dateRange: service.getDateRangeLiteral(),
        currentFields: service.getUsedSearchFieldsArray(searchRequest),
        interactionType: service.interactionType?.toString(),
      },
    };
    jest.spyOn(trackingService, 'trackEvent');
    jest
      .spyOn(service, 'getTradesRequestPayload')
      .mockReturnValue(searchRequest);

    // Act
    service.clearTrades();

    // Assert
    expect(trackingService.trackEvent).toHaveBeenCalledWith(trackingEvent);
  });
});

================================================================================

File: trades-search\data-access\src\lib\services\trades-search-facade.service.ts
/*
 * Copyright (c) 2023 FMR Corp.
 * All Rights Reserved.
 *
 * Fidelity Confidential Information.
 * Created on 6/20/23, 4:51 PM
 */
import { Injectable } from '@angular/core';
import { Store } from '@ngrx/store';
import * as fromTradesSearch from '../state';
import {
  executionGridActions,
  tradesGridActions,
} from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/trades-grid/data-access';
import {
  ExecutionSearchRequest,
  TradeSearchRequest,
} from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/trades-grid/data';
import { DatePipe } from '@angular/common';
import { MatSnackBar } from '@angular/material/snack-bar';
import {
  allStatusesExecutions,
  allStatusesTrades,
  defaultStatusesExecutions,
  defaultStatusesTrades,
  fmrcy,
  fmreq,
  fmrhi,
  noDeskError,
  snackBarDuration,
  wrongDeskError,
} from '../constants/trades-search-store.constants';
import {
  InteractionType,
  TrackingEvent,
  TrackingEventName,
  TrackingService,
} from '@fmr-pr000539/eqt-tracking-module';
import { ActivatedRoute, Params } from '@angular/router';
import { GridView, gridViewQParams } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/constants';
import { takeUntilDestroyed } from '@angular/core/rxjs-interop';
import { DateSelectionType } from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/data';

@Injectable()
export class TradesSearchFacadeService {
  public symbol$ = this.store.select(fromTradesSearch.getSymbol);
  public startDate$ = this.store.select(fromTradesSearch.getStartDate);
  public endDate$ = this.store.select(fromTradesSearch.getEndDate);
  public fmrCusips$ = this.store.select(fromTradesSearch.getCusip);
  public desk$ = this.store.select(fromTradesSearch.getDesk);
  public eqtConfig$ = this.store.select(fromTradesSearch.getCryptoCusip);
  public funds$ = this.store.select(fromTradesSearch.getFunds);
  public interactionType$ = this.store.select(
    fromTradesSearch.getInteractionTYpe,
  );
  public brokers$ = this.store.select(fromTradesSearch.getBrokers);
  public ivtypes$ = this.store.select(fromTradesSearch.getIVTypes);
  public traders$ = this.store.select(fromTradesSearch.getTraders);
  public datePickingMethod$ = this.store.select(
    fromTradesSearch.getDatePickingMethod,
  );

  public enteredSymbol = '';
  public enteredStartDate = new Date();
  public enteredEndDate = new Date();
  public startDateValue: Date | undefined;
  public endDateValue: Date | undefined;
  public fmrCusipValues: string[] | undefined;
  public desk: string[] | undefined;
  public eqtConfig: string | undefined;
  public funds: string[] | undefined;
  public areCancelledTradesEnabled = false;
  public interactionType: InteractionType | undefined;
  public brokers: number[] | undefined;
  public instrumentTypes: string[] | undefined;
  public traders: string[] | undefined;
  public datePickingMethod: DateSelectionType;

  public isExecutionsContext = false;
  private readonly MODULE_NAME = 'Trades Search';

  public constructor(
    private readonly store: Store,
    private readonly trackingService: TrackingService,
    private readonly datePipe: DatePipe,
    public readonly snackBar: MatSnackBar,
    private readonly route: ActivatedRoute,
  ) {
    this.startDate$.subscribe((date) => (this.startDateValue = date));
    this.endDate$.subscribe((date) => (this.endDateValue = date));
    this.symbol$.subscribe((symbol) => (this.enteredSymbol = symbol));
    this.fmrCusips$.subscribe((cusip) => (this.fmrCusipValues = cusip));
    this.desk$.subscribe((desk) => (this.desk = desk));
    this.eqtConfig$.subscribe((eqtConfig) => (this.eqtConfig = eqtConfig));
    this.funds$.subscribe((funds) => (this.funds = funds));
    this.interactionType$.subscribe(
      (interationType) => (this.interactionType = interationType),
    );
    this.brokers$.subscribe((brokers) => (this.brokers = brokers));
    this.ivtypes$.subscribe(
      (instrumentTypes) => (this.instrumentTypes = instrumentTypes),
    );
    this.traders$.subscribe((traders) => (this.traders = traders));
    this.datePickingMethod$.subscribe(
      (datePickingMethod) => (this.datePickingMethod = datePickingMethod),
    );
    this.setUpDataContext();
  }

  public updateSymbol(symbol: string): void {
    if (this.enteredSymbol !== symbol) {
      this.enteredSymbol = symbol;
      this.store.dispatch(
        fromTradesSearch.setSymbol({ symbol: this.enteredSymbol }),
      );
    }
  }

  public updateCusip(cusips: string[]): void {
    if (JSON.stringify(this.fmrCusipValues) !== JSON.stringify(cusips)) {
      this.fmrCusipValues = cusips;
      this.store.dispatch(
        fromTradesSearch.setCusip({ cusips: this.fmrCusipValues }),
      );
    }
  }

  public updateFunds(funds: string[]): void {
    this.funds = funds;
    this.store.dispatch(fromTradesSearch.setFunds({ funds: this.funds }));
  }

  public updateStartDate(startDate: Date): void {
    if (this.enteredStartDate !== startDate) {
      this.enteredStartDate = startDate;
      this.store.dispatch(
        fromTradesSearch.setStartDate({ startDate: this.enteredStartDate }),
      );
    }
  }

  public updateEndDate(endDate: Date): void {
    if (this.enteredEndDate !== endDate) {
      this.enteredEndDate = endDate;
      this.store.dispatch(
        fromTradesSearch.setEndDate({ endDate: this.enteredEndDate }),
      );
    }
  }

  public updateAreCancelledTradesEnabled(enabled: boolean): void {
    this.areCancelledTradesEnabled = enabled;
  }

  public updateInteractionType(interactionType: InteractionType): void {
    this.store.dispatch(
      fromTradesSearch.setInteractionType({ interactionType }),
    );
  }

  public updateBrokers(brokers: number[]): void {
    this.brokers = brokers;
    this.store.dispatch(fromTradesSearch.setBrokers({ brokers: this.brokers }));
  }

  public updateTraders(traders: string[]): void {
    this.traders = traders;
    this.store.dispatch(fromTradesSearch.setTraders({ traders: this.traders }));
  }

  public updateInstrumentTypes(instrumentTypes: string[]): void {
    this.instrumentTypes = instrumentTypes;
    this.store.dispatch(
      fromTradesSearch.setInstrumentTypes({
        instrumentTypes: this.instrumentTypes,
      }),
    );
  }

  public updateDatePickingMethod(dateSelectionType: DateSelectionType): void {
    this.store.dispatch(
      fromTradesSearch.setDatePickingMethod({
        datePickingMethod: dateSelectionType,
      }),
    );
  }

  public searchData(): void {
    if (this.isExecutionsContext) {
      this.getExecutions();
    } else {
      this.getTrades();
    }
  }

  public getTrades(): void {
    const searchRequest = this.getTradesRequestPayload();
    this.trackSearchClicked(searchRequest);
    if (this.isCusipValid()) {
      if (this.checkDeskCusip()) {
        this.dispatchGetTradesRequest(searchRequest);
      }
    } else {
      this.dispatchGetTradesRequest(searchRequest);
    }
  }

  public getExecutions(): void {
    const searchRequest = this.getExecutionsRequestPayload();
    this.trackSearchClicked(searchRequest);
    if (this.isCusipValid()) {
      if (this.checkDeskCusip()) {
        this.dispatchGetExecutionsRequest(searchRequest);
      }
    } else {
      this.dispatchGetExecutionsRequest(searchRequest);
    }
  }

  public clearTrades(): void {
    let searchRequest;
    if (this.isExecutionsContext) {
      searchRequest = this.getExecutionsRequestPayload();
    } else {
      searchRequest = this.getTradesRequestPayload();
    }
    this.trackClearParamsClicked(searchRequest);
    this.store.dispatch(tradesGridActions.clearTrades());
  }

  public checkDeskCusip(): boolean {
    const cusip = this.fmrCusipValues ? this.fmrCusipValues : [];
    if (
      (this.desk?.includes(fmreq) || this.desk?.includes(fmrhi)) &&
      this.desk.includes(fmrcy)
    )
      return true;
    else if (this.desk?.includes(fmreq) || this.desk?.includes(fmrhi)) {
      if (cusip.some((c) => this.eqtConfig?.includes(c))) {
        this.openSnackBar(wrongDeskError, 'snackbar-failure');
        return false;
      }
      return true;
    } else if (this.desk?.includes(fmrcy)) {
      if (!cusip.some((c) => this.eqtConfig?.includes(c))) {
        this.openSnackBar(wrongDeskError, 'snackbar-failure');
        return false;
      }
      return true;
    }
    this.openSnackBar(noDeskError, 'snackbar-failure');
    return false;
  }

  public openSnackBar(snackbarMessage: string, snackbarStyles: string): void {
    this.snackBar.open(snackbarMessage, '', {
      duration: snackBarDuration,
      verticalPosition: 'top',
      panelClass: snackbarStyles,
    });
  }

  public getExecutionsRequestPayload(): ExecutionSearchRequest {
    return {
      fmrIssueCusips: this.fmrCusipValues ?? [],
      startDate:
        this.datePipe.transform(this.startDateValue, 'yyyy-MM-dd') ?? '',
      endDate: this.datePipe.transform(this.endDateValue, 'yyyy-MM-dd') ?? '',
      parentTradingDeskShortNames: this.desk,
      ivTypeCodes: this.instrumentTypes,
      statuses: this.getStatuses(),
      brokerFirmSourceIds: this.brokers,
      fmrSymbols: [],
      traderPersonSourceIds: this.traders,
    };
  }

  public getTradesRequestPayload(): TradeSearchRequest {
    return {
      fmrIssueCusips: this.fmrCusipValues ?? [],
      startDate:
        this.datePipe.transform(this.startDateValue, 'yyyy-MM-dd') ?? '',
      endDate: this.datePipe.transform(this.endDateValue, 'yyyy-MM-dd') ?? '',
      parentTradingDeskShortNames: this.desk,
      ivTypeCodes: this.instrumentTypes,
      statuses: this.getStatuses(),
      fmrFundNumbers: this.funds,
      brokerFirmSourceIds: this.brokers,
      fmrSymbols: [],
      traderPersonSourceIds: this.traders,
    };
  }

  protected getDateRangeLiteral(): string {
    const tradeSearchRequest: TradeSearchRequest = this.isExecutionsContext
      ? this.getExecutionsRequestPayload()
      : this.getTradesRequestPayload();
    return `${tradeSearchRequest.startDate} - ${tradeSearchRequest.endDate}`;
  }

  protected getUsedSearchFieldsArray(
    searchRequest: TradeSearchRequest,
  ): string {
    const fieldMap: [keyof TradeSearchRequest, string][] = [
      ['fmrIssueCusips', 'Symbol'],
      ['fmrFundNumbers', 'Fund'],
      ['ivTypeCodes', 'Instrument'],
      ['brokerFirmSourceIds', 'Broker'],
      ['traderPersonSourceIds', 'Trader'],
    ];

    const searchFields = fieldMap
      .filter(([key]) => !!searchRequest[key]?.length)
      .map(([, label]) => label);

    return JSON.stringify(searchFields);
  }

  private setUpDataContext(): void {
    this.route.queryParams
      .pipe(takeUntilDestroyed())
      .subscribe((params: Params) => {
        if (params[gridViewQParams] === GridView.Executions) {
          this.isExecutionsContext = true;
        }
      });
  }

  private isCusipValid(): boolean {
    return (
      this.fmrCusipValues !== undefined && this.fmrCusipValues.length !== 0
    );
  }

  private dispatchGetTradesRequest(searchRequest: TradeSearchRequest): void {
    this.store.dispatch(
      tradesGridActions.getTrades({
        payload: { request: searchRequest },
      }),
    );
  }

  private dispatchGetExecutionsRequest(
    searchRequest: ExecutionSearchRequest,
  ): void {
    this.store.dispatch(
      executionGridActions.getExecutions({
        payload: { request: searchRequest },
      }),
    );
  }

  private getStatuses(): string[] {
    if (this.areCancelledTradesEnabled) {
      return this.isExecutionsContext
        ? allStatusesExecutions
        : allStatusesTrades;
    }
    return this.isExecutionsContext
      ? defaultStatusesExecutions
      : defaultStatusesTrades;
  }

  private trackSearchClicked(searchRequest: TradeSearchRequest): void {
    const additionalAttributes: Record<string, unknown> = {
      includeCancelled: this.areCancelledTradesEnabled,
      dateRange: this.getDateRangeLiteral(),
      dateRangeType: this.datePickingMethod,
      searchFields: this.getUsedSearchFieldsArray(searchRequest),
      interactionType: this.interactionType?.toString(),
    };

    if (searchRequest.fmrFundNumbers?.length) {
      additionalAttributes['fund'] = JSON.stringify(
        searchRequest.fmrFundNumbers,
      );
    }
    this.trackEvent(TrackingEventName.SearchClicked, additionalAttributes);
  }

  private trackClearParamsClicked(searchRequest: TradeSearchRequest): void {
    const additionalAttributes = {
      includeCancelled: this.areCancelledTradesEnabled,
      dateRange: this.getDateRangeLiteral(),
      currentFields: this.getUsedSearchFieldsArray(searchRequest),
      interactionType: this.interactionType?.toString(),
    };
    this.trackEvent(TrackingEventName.ClearParamsClicked, additionalAttributes);
  }

  private trackEvent(
    action: TrackingEventName,
    additionalAttributes: { [p: string]: any } | undefined,
  ): void {
    const trackingEvent: TrackingEvent = {
      action,
      additionalAttributes,
      appModule: this.MODULE_NAME,
    };
    // eslint-disable-next-line max-lines
    this.trackingService.trackEvent(trackingEvent);
  }
}

import { createAction, props } from '@ngrx/store';
import { TradesSearchStoreConstants } from '../constants/trades-search-store.constants';
import { InteractionType } from '@fmr-pr000539/eqt-tracking-module';
import { DateSelectionType } from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/data';

export const setSymbol = createAction(
  `${TradesSearchStoreConstants.ActionKey} ${TradesSearchStoreConstants.SetSymbol}`,
  props<{ symbol: string }>(),
);

export const setCusip = createAction(
  `${TradesSearchStoreConstants.ActionKey} ${TradesSearchStoreConstants.SetCusip}`,
  props<{ cusips: string[] }>(),
);

export const setStartDate = createAction(
  `${TradesSearchStoreConstants.ActionKey} ${TradesSearchStoreConstants.SetStartDate}`,
  props<{ startDate: Date }>(),
);

export const setEndDate = createAction(
  `${TradesSearchStoreConstants.ActionKey} ${TradesSearchStoreConstants.SetEndDate}`,
  props<{ endDate: Date }>(),
);

export const setViewOrdersDesk = createAction(
  `${TradesSearchStoreConstants.ActionKey} ${TradesSearchStoreConstants.SetViewOrdersDesk}`,
  props<{ desk: string[] }>(),
);

export const setFunds = createAction(
  `${TradesSearchStoreConstants.ActionKey} ${TradesSearchStoreConstants.SetFunds}`,
  props<{ funds: string[] }>(),
);

export const setInteractionType = createAction(
  `${TradesSearchStoreConstants.ActionKey} ${TradesSearchStoreConstants.SetSearchInteractionType}`,
  props<{ interactionType: InteractionType }>(),
);

export const setDatePickingMethod = createAction(
  `${TradesSearchStoreConstants.ActionKey} ${TradesSearchStoreConstants.SetDatePickingMethod}`,
  props<{ datePickingMethod: DateSelectionType }>(),
);

export const setBrokers = createAction(
  `${TradesSearchStoreConstants.ActionKey} ${TradesSearchStoreConstants.SetBrokers}`,
  props<{ brokers: number[] }>(),
);

export const setInstrumentTypes = createAction(
  `${TradesSearchStoreConstants.ActionKey} ${TradesSearchStoreConstants.SetInstrumentTypes}`,
  props<{ instrumentTypes: string[] }>(),
);

export const setTraders = createAction(
  `${TradesSearchStoreConstants.ActionKey} ${TradesSearchStoreConstants.SetTraders}`,
  props<{ traders: string[] }>(),
);

import * as searchActions from './trades-search.actions';
import { initialState, TradesSearchState } from './trades-search.state';
import { reducer } from './trades-search.reducer';

describe('tradesSearchReducer', () => {
  let state: TradesSearchState;
  beforeEach(() => {
    state = { ...initialState };
  });

  describe('setSymbol', () => {
    it('should set the symbol', () => {
      // Arrange
      const symVal = 'AA';
      const action = searchActions.setSymbol({ symbol: symVal });

      // Act
      const result: TradesSearchState = reducer(state, action);

      // Assert
      expect(result.symbol).toBe(symVal);
    });
  });

  describe('setCusip', () => {
    it('should set the symbol', () => {
      // Arrange
      const cusip = ['AA001'];
      const action = searchActions.setCusip({ cusips: cusip });

      // Act

      // Assert
      expect(result.fmrIssueCusips).toBe(cusip);
    });
  });

  describe('setStartDate', () => {
    it('should set the startDate', () => {
      // Arrange

      // Act
      const result: TradesSearchState = reducer(state, action);

      // Assert
      expect(result.startDate).toBe(dateVal);
    });
  });

  describe('setEndDate', () => {
    it('should set the endDate', () => {
      // Arrange

      // Act

      // Assert

    });

  describe('setViewOrdersDesk', () => {
    it('should set the desk', () => {
      // Arrange

      // Act

      // Assert

File: trades-search\data-access\src\lib\state\trades-search.reducer.ts
/*
 * Copyright (c) 2023 FMR Corp.
 * All Rights Reserved.
 *
 * Fidelity Confidential Information.
 * Created on 6/20/23, 4:51 PM
 */

import { Action, createReducer, on } from '@ngrx/store';
import * as tradesSearchActions from './trades-search.actions';
import { initialState, TradesSearchState } from './trades-search.state';

export const tradesSearchReducer = createReducer<TradesSearchState>(
  initialState,
  on(tradesSearchActions.setSymbol, (state, action): TradesSearchState => {
    return {
      ...state,
      symbol: action.symbol,
    };
  }),
  on(tradesSearchActions.setCusip, (state, action): TradesSearchState => {
    return {
      ...state,
      fmrIssueCusips: action.cusips,
    };
  }),
  on(tradesSearchActions.setStartDate, (state, action): TradesSearchState => {
    return {
      ...state,
      startDate: action.startDate,
    };
  }),
  on(tradesSearchActions.setEndDate, (state, action): TradesSearchState => {
    return {
      ...state,
      endDate: action.endDate,
    };
  }),
  on(
    tradesSearchActions.setViewOrdersDesk,
    (state, action): TradesSearchState => {
      return {
        ...state,
        desk: action.desk,
      };
    },
  ),
  on(tradesSearchActions.setFunds, (state, action): TradesSearchState => {
    return {
      ...state,
      funds: action.funds,
    };
  }),
  on(
    tradesSearchActions.setInteractionType,
    (state, action): TradesSearchState => {
      return {
        ...state,
        interactionType: action.interactionType,
      };
    },
  ),
  on(tradesSearchActions.setBrokers, (state, action): TradesSearchState => {
    return {
      ...state,
      brokers: action.brokers,
    };
  }),
  on(
    tradesSearchActions.setInstrumentTypes,
    (state, action): TradesSearchState => {
      return {
        ...state,
        ivTypeCodes: action.instrumentTypes,
      };
    },
  ),
  on(tradesSearchActions.setTraders, (state, action): TradesSearchState => {
    return {
      ...state,
      traders: action.traders,
    };
  }),
  on(
    tradesSearchActions.setDatePickingMethod,
    (state, action): TradesSearchState => {
      return {
        ...state,
        datePickingMethod: action.datePickingMethod,
      };
    },
  ),
);

export function reducer(
  state: TradesSearchState | undefined,
  action: Action,
): TradesSearchState {
  return tradesSearchReducer(state, action);
}

File: trades-search\data-access\src\lib\state\trades-search.selectors.spec.ts
/*
 * Copyright (c) 2023 FMR Corp.
 * All Rights Reserved.

 * Fidelity Confidential Information.
 * Created on 6/20/23, 4:51 PM
 */

import { initialState, TradesSearchState } from './trades-search.state';
import * as searchSelectors from './trades-search.selectors';
import {
  fmreq,
  iconfigCryptoCusip,
  TradesSearchStoreConstants,
} from '../constants/trades-search-store.constants';

describe('TradesSearchSelectors', () => {
  let searchState: TradesSearchState;
  let state: any;

  beforeEach(() => {
    searchState = initialState;
    state = {
      [TradesSearchStoreConstants.FeatureKey]: searchState,
    };
  });

  it('getCryptoCusip() should return the  "iconfigCryptoCusip" state', () => {
    // Arrange
    const configState = {
      [iconfigCryptoCusip]: fmreq,
    };

    // Act
    const result = searchSelectors.getCryptoCusip.projector(configState);

    // Assert
    expect(result).toBe(fmreq);
  });

  it('getSymbol() should return the current "symbol" state', () => {
    // Arrange
    const symVal = 'AA';
    searchState.symbol = symVal;

    // Act
    const result = searchSelectors.getSymbol(state);

    // Assert
    expect(result).toBe(symVal);
  });

  it('getCusip() should return the current "symbol" state', () => {
    // Arrange
    const cusip = ['AA001'];
    searchState.fmrIssueCusips = cusip;

    // Act
    const result = searchSelectors.getCusip(state);

    // Assert
    expect(result).toBe(cusip);
  });

  it('getStartDate() should return the current "date" state', () => {
    // Arrange
    const dateVal = new Date();
    searchState.startDate = dateVal;

    // Act
    const result = searchSelectors.getStartDate(state);

    // Assert
    expect(result).toBe(dateVal);
  });

  it('getEndDate() should return the current "date" state', () => {
    // Arrange
    const dateVal = new Date();
    searchState.endDate = dateVal;

    // Act
    const result = searchSelectors.getEndDate(state);

    // Assert
    expect(result).toBe(dateVal);
  });

  it('getDesk() should return the current "desk" state', () => {
    // Arrange
    const desk = ['FMREQ'];
    searchState.desk = desk;

    // Act
    const result = searchSelectors.getDesk(state);

    // Assert
    expect(result).toBe(desk);
  });

  it('getFunds() should return the current "funds" state', () => {
    // Arrange
    const funds = ['abc'];
    searchState.funds = funds;

    // Act
    const result = searchSelectors.getFunds(state);

    // Assert
    expect(result).toBe(funds);
  });

  it('getTraders() should return the current "traders" state', () => {
    // Arrange
    const traders = ['Trader1', 'Trader2'];
    searchState.traders = traders;

    // Act
    const result = searchSelectors.getTraders(state);

    // Assert
    expect(result).toBe(traders);
  });
});

/*

import { createFeatureSelector, createSelector } from '@ngrx/store';
import {
  iconfigCryptoCusip,
  iconfigCancelAndAdjustServiceUrl,
  TradesSearchStoreConstants,
} from '../constants/trades-search-store.constants';
import { TradesSearchState } from './trades-search.state';
import { getConfig } from '@fmr-pr000539/eqt-ngrx-config-module';

export const getCryptoCusip = createSelector(
  getConfig,
  (config) => config[iconfigCryptoCusip],
);

export const getCancelAndAdjustServiceUrl = createSelector(
  getConfig,
  (config) => config[iconfigCancelAndAdjustServiceUrl],
);

const getOrdersSearchState = createFeatureSelector<TradesSearchState>(
  TradesSearchStoreConstants.FeatureKey,
);

export const getSymbol = createSelector(
  getOrdersSearchState,
  (state: TradesSearchState) => state.symbol,
);

export const getCusip = createSelector(
  getOrdersSearchState,
  (state: TradesSearchState) => state.fmrIssueCusips,
);

export const getStartDate = createSelector(
  getOrdersSearchState,
  (state: TradesSearchState) => state.startDate,
);

export const getEndDate = createSelector(
  getOrdersSearchState,
  (state: TradesSearchState) => state.endDate,
);

export const getDesk = createSelector(
  getOrdersSearchState,
  (state: TradesSearchState) => state.desk,
);

export const getFunds = createSelector(
  getOrdersSearchState,
  (state: TradesSearchState) => state.funds,
);

export const getInteractionTYpe = createSelector(
  getOrdersSearchState,
  (state: TradesSearchState) => state.interactionType,
);

export const getBrokers = createSelector(
  getOrdersSearchState,
  (state: TradesSearchState) => state.brokers,
);

export const getIVTypes = createSelector(
  getOrdersSearchState,
  (state: TradesSearchState) => state.ivTypeCodes,
);
export const getTraders = createSelector(
  getOrdersSearchState,
  (state: TradesSearchState) => state.traders,
);

export const getDatePickingMethod = createSelector(
  getOrdersSearchState,
  (state: TradesSearchState) => state.datePickingMethod,
);

/*

import { InteractionType } from '@fmr-pr000539/eqt-tracking-module';
import { DateSelectionType } from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/data';

export interface TradesSearchState {
  symbol: string;
  fmrIssueCusips: string[];
  startDate: Date;
  endDate: Date;
  desk: string[];
  funds: string[];
  brokers: number[];
  ivTypeCodes: string[];
  traders: string[];
  interactionType: InteractionType | undefined;
  datePickingMethod: DateSelectionType;
}

export const initialState: TradesSearchState = {
  symbol: '',
  fmrIssueCusips: [],
  startDate: new Date(),
  endDate: new Date(),
  desk: [],
  funds: [],
  brokers: [],
  ivTypeCodes: [],
  traders: [],
  interactionType: undefined,
  datePickingMethod: DateSelectionType.DatePicker,
};
