File: trades-search\feature\src\lib\trades-search\trades-search.component.spec.ts
/*
 * Copyright (c) 2023 FMR Corp.
 * All Rights Reserved.
 *
 * Fidelity Confidential Information.
 * Created on 6/20/23, 4:51 PM
 */

/**
 * @author a526677@fmr.com
 */
import { ComponentFixture, TestBed } from '@angular/core/testing';

import { TradesSearchComponent } from './trades-search.component';
import {
  ExacTradesSearchDataAccessModule,
  TradesSearchFacadeService,
} from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/trades-search/data-access';
import { StoreModule } from '@ngrx/store';
import { of } from 'rxjs';
import { SuggestibleSearchSuggestion } from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/ui/suggestible-search';
import { MatSnackBar } from '@angular/material/snack-bar';
import { ArrowRestService } from '@fmr-pr000264/ames-arrow-rest-service';
import { HttpClient } from '@angular/common/http';
import { ArrowAuthDetails } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';
import {
  DatePickerComponent,
  DateRange,
  DateRangeEvent,
} from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/ui/date-picker';
import { Component } from '@angular/core';
import { MockComponent } from 'ng-mocks';
import { By } from '@angular/platform-browser';
import { DateSelectionType } from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/data';

describe('TradesSearchComponent', () => {
  let component: TradesSearchComponent;
  let fixture: ComponentFixture<TradesSearchComponent>;
  const arrowRestService = {} as ArrowRestService;

  const mockTradesSearchFacadeService = {
    updateSymbol: jest.fn(),
    updateFunds: jest.fn(),
    updateEndDate: jest.fn(),
    getTrades: jest.fn(),
    updateCusip: jest.fn(),
    updateAreCancelledTradesEnabled: jest.fn(),
    clearTrades: jest.fn(),
    updateStartDate: jest.fn(),
    updateInteractionType: jest.fn(),
    updateInstrumentTypes: jest.fn(),
    searchData: jest.fn(),
    updateTraders: jest.fn(),
    updateDatePickingMethod: jest.fn(),
  };

  beforeEach(async () => {
    await TestBed.configureTestingModule({
      imports: [
        ExacTradesSearchDataAccessModule,
        StoreModule.forRoot(
          {},
          {
            metaReducers: [],
            runtimeChecks: {
              strictActionImmutability: true,
              strictStateImmutability: true,
            },
          },
        ),
      ],
      declarations: [TradesSearchComponent, MockComponent(DatePickerComponent)],
      providers: [
        {
          provide: TradesSearchFacadeService,
          useValue: mockTradesSearchFacadeService,
        },
        {
          provide: ArrowRestService,
          useValue: arrowRestService,
        },
        {
          provide: DatePickerComponent,
          useClass: DatepickerMockComponent,
        },
        MatSnackBar,
        HttpClient,
      ],
    }).compileComponents();

    arrowRestService.getAuthorizedFunctionObjectNames = jest
      .fn()
      .mockReturnValue(of([]));

    fixture = TestBed.createComponent(TradesSearchComponent);
    component = fixture.componentInstance;
    fixture.detectChanges();
  });

  it('should create', () => {
    expect(component).toBeTruthy();
  });

  it('should access the date picker component', () => {
    const datepicker = fixture.debugElement.query(
      By.directive(DatePickerComponent),
    ).componentInstance;
    expect(datepicker).toBeTruthy();
  });

  describe('getAuthorizedFunctionObjectNames', () => {
    it('should retrieve authorized function object names', () => {
      // Act
      component.getAuthorizedFunctionObjectNames();

      // Assert
      expect(
        arrowRestService.getAuthorizedFunctionObjectNames,
      ).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
        ArrowAuthDetails.AppName as string,
        'Trade Activity',
        ArrowAuthDetails.ViewOrdersRole as string,
        ArrowAuthDetails.ObjectTypeName as string,
      );
    });
  });
  describe('symbolChanged', () => {
    it('should call facade service method updateSymbol with new symbol value', () => {
      // Arrange
      const value = 'aa';
      const tradeSearchFacadeSvcSpy =
        mockTradesSearchFacadeService.updateSymbol;

      // Act
      component.symbolChanged(value);

      // Assert
      expect(tradeSearchFacadeSvcSpy).toHaveBeenCalledWith('AA');
    });
  });

  describe('rangeDateChanged', () => {
    it('should call facade service method updateStartDate and updateEndDate with new date range value', () => {
      // Arrange
      const startDate = new Date();
      const endDate = new Date();
      const dateRange: DateRange = { startDate, endDate };
      const updateEndDateSpy = mockTradesSearchFacadeService.updateEndDate;
      const updateStartDateSpy = mockTradesSearchFacadeService.updateStartDate;
      const dateRangeEvent: DateRangeEvent = {
        dateSelectionType: DateSelectionType.DatePicker,
        dateRange,
      };
      // Act
      component.onDateRangeEventTriggered(dateRangeEvent);

      // Assert
      expect(updateStartDateSpy).toHaveBeenCalledWith(startDate);
      expect(updateEndDateSpy).toHaveBeenCalledWith(endDate);
    });
  });

  describe('getTradingData', () => {
    it('should call facade service getTrades method  ', () => {
      // Arrange
      const tradeSearchFacadeSvcSpy = mockTradesSearchFacadeService.searchData;
      const mockEvent = new MouseEvent('click');
      // Act
      component.getTradingData(mockEvent);

      // Assert
      expect(tradeSearchFacadeSvcSpy).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });
  });

  describe('clearAll', () => {
    it('should reset search and grid state and reset values in search bar and date picker ', () => {
      // Arrange
      const tradeSearchFacadeSvcSpy = mockTradesSearchFacadeService.clearTrades;
      const mockEvent = new MouseEvent('click');
      const clearDatePickerSpy = jest.spyOn(component, 'clearDateRange');

      // Act
      component.clearAll(mockEvent);

      // Assert
      expect(tradeSearchFacadeSvcSpy).toHaveBeenCalled();
      expect(component.clear).toEqual({});
      expect(clearDatePickerSpy).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });
  });

  describe('selectCompanySuggestion', () => {
    it('should call facade service methods to update symbol and cusip', () => {
      // Arrange
      const updateSymbolFacadeSvcSpy =
        mockTradesSearchFacadeService.updateSymbol;
      const updateCusipFacadeSvcSpy = mockTradesSearchFacadeService.updateCusip;
      const suggestion = { ticker: 'AAPL', issueCUSIP: 'aa001' };

      // Act
      component.selectCompanySuggestion(
        suggestion as SuggestibleSearchSuggestion,
      );

      // Assert
      expect(updateSymbolFacadeSvcSpy).toHaveBeenCalled();
      expect(updateCusipFacadeSvcSpy).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });
  });

  describe('selectFundSuggestion', () => {
    it('should call facade service methods to update funds', () => {
      // Arrange
      const updateFundsFacadeSvcSpy = mockTradesSearchFacadeService.updateFunds;

      const suggestion = [1];

      // Act
      component.selectFundSuggestion(suggestion);

      // Assert
      expect(updateFundsFacadeSvcSpy).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });
  });

  describe('removeFunds', () => {
    it('should call facade service methods to update funds when one is cleared', () => {
      // Arrange
      const updateFundsFacadeSvcSpy = mockTradesSearchFacadeService.updateFunds;

      const suggestion = { shortName: 'ALC', fundNumber: 1 };
      component.selectedFunds = [];

      // Act
      component.removeFunds();

      // Assert
      expect(updateFundsFacadeSvcSpy).toHaveBeenCalledWith([]);
    });
  });

  describe('removeSymbol', () => {
    it('should call facade service methods updateSymbol and updateCusip with empty value and  to remove symbol when is cleared', () => {
      // Arrange
      const updateCusipFacadeSpy = mockTradesSearchFacadeService.updateCusip;

      // Act
      component.removeSymbol();

      // Assert
      expect(updateCusipFacadeSpy).toHaveBeenCalledWith([]);
    });
  });

  describe('cancelled trades checkbox', () => {
    const updateAreCancelledTradesEnabledSpy =
      mockTradesSearchFacadeService.updateAreCancelledTradesEnabled;
    it('should call updateAreCancelledTradesEnabled with true if checked', () => {
      // Act
      component.onCancelledCheckboxClick({ checked: true });
      // Assert
      expect(updateAreCancelledTradesEnabledSpy).toHaveBeenCalledWith(true);
    });
    it('should call updateAreCancelledTradesEnabled with false if unchecked', () => {
      // Act
      component.onCancelledCheckboxClick({ checked: false });
      // Assert
      expect(updateAreCancelledTradesEnabledSpy).toHaveBeenCalledWith(false);
    });
  });
  describe('selectTraderSuggestion', () => {
    it('should call facade service methods to update traders', () => {
      // Arrange
      const updateTradersFacadeSvcSpy =
        mockTradesSearchFacadeService.updateTraders;
      const suggestion = ['Trader1', 'Trader2'];

      // Act
      component.selectTraderSuggestion(suggestion);

      // Assert
      expect(updateTradersFacadeSvcSpy).toHaveBeenCalledWith(suggestion);
    });
  });
});

@Component({
  selector: 'fmr-pr000539-date-picker',
  template: '',
})
class DatepickerMockComponent {
  clearDatePicker(): void {}
}

================================================================================

File: trades-search\feature\src\lib\trades-search\trades-search.component.ts
/*
 * Copyright (c) 2023 FMR Corp.
 * All Rights Reserved.
 *
 * Fidelity Confidential Information.
 * Created on 6/20/23, 4:51 PM
 */

import { ChangeDetectorRef, Component, OnInit, ViewChild } from '@angular/core';
import { combineLatest, Observable } from 'rxjs';
import { takeUntilDestroyed } from '@angular/core/rxjs-interop';
import * as fromTradesSearch from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/trades-search/data-access';
import { TradesSearchFacadeService } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/trades-search/data-access';
import {
  SearchContext as CommonSearchContext,
  SearchType,
  TreeNode,
} from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/ui/hds-common-search';
import { ArrowAuthDetails } from '@fmr-pr000539/exac/shared/data';
import { ArrowRestService } from '@fmr-pr000264/ames-arrow-rest-service';
import { Store } from '@ngrx/store';
import {
  DatePickerComponent,
  DateRangeEvent,
} from '@fmr-pr000539/shared/ui/date-picker';
import { getInteractionTypeFromEvent } from '@fmr-pr000539/eqt-tracking-module';
import { FormGroup } from '@angular/forms';

@Component({
  selector: 'fmr-pr000539-exac-trades-search',
  templateUrl: './trades-search.component.html',
  styleUrls: ['./trades-search.component.scss'],
  standalone: false,
})
export class TradesSearchComponent implements OnInit {
  public fmrCusips$!: Observable<string[]>;
  public funds$!: Observable<string[]>;
  public startDate$!: Observable<Date>;
  public endDate$!: Observable<Date>;
  public ivtypes$!: Observable<string[]>;
  public traders$!: Observable<string[]>;

  public clear: any;
  public selectedFunds: string[] = [];
  public selectedBrokers: any[] = [];
  public selectedInstrumentTypes: any[] = [];
  public isSearchActive = false;
  public fundSearchContext: CommonSearchContext | null;
  public brokerSearchContext: CommonSearchContext = {
    searchType: SearchType.Broker,
  };

  public symbolSearchContext: CommonSearchContext = {
    searchType: SearchType.Symbol,
  };

  public traderSearchContext: CommonSearchContext = {
    searchType: SearchType.Trader,
  };
  public selectedTraders: string[] = [];

  public instrumentTypeSearchContext: CommonSearchContext = {
    searchType: SearchType.InstrumentType,
    disableRules: {
      tree: (node: TreeNode) => {
        const item = node.items[0];
        const code = item.value as string;
        return code.toUpperCase() === 'CS';
      },
    },
  };
  public formGroup = new FormGroup({});
  public dateError = '';
  public brokers$!: Observable<number[]>;
  @ViewChild(DatePickerComponent) protected datePicker!: DatePickerComponent;
  private readonly searchState$: Observable<readonly unknown[]>;

  public constructor(
    private readonly tradesSearchFacadeService: TradesSearchFacadeService,
    private readonly arrowService: ArrowRestService,
    private readonly store: Store<fromTradesSearch.TradesSearchState>,
    private readonly cd: ChangeDetectorRef,
  ) {
    this.fmrCusips$ = this.tradesSearchFacadeService.fmrCusips$;
    this.funds$ = this.tradesSearchFacadeService.funds$;
    this.startDate$ = this.tradesSearchFacadeService.startDate$;
    this.endDate$ = this.tradesSearchFacadeService.endDate$;
    this.brokers$ = this.tradesSearchFacadeService.brokers$;
    // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unsafe-assignment
    this.ivtypes$ = this.tradesSearchFacadeService.ivtypes$;
    this.traders$ = this.tradesSearchFacadeService.traders$;

    this.searchState$ = combineLatest([
      this.fmrCusips$,
      this.funds$,
      this.startDate$,
      this.endDate$,
      this.ivtypes$,
      this.brokers$,
      this.traders$,
    ]).pipe(takeUntilDestroyed());
  }

  public ngOnInit(): void {
    this.searchState$.subscribe(
      ([fmrCusips, funds, startDate, endDate, ivtype]) => {
        this.isSearchActive =
          ((fmrCusips as string[]).length > 0 ||
            (funds as string[]).length > 0 ||
            (ivtype as string[]).length > 0) &&
          (startDate as Date).toDateString() !== 'Invalid Date' &&
          (endDate as Date).toDateString() !== 'Invalid Date';
        this.cd.detectChanges();
      },
    );
    this.getAuthorizedFunctionObjectNames();
    this.getFundContexts();
    // TODO: the if statement will be used when funds are available for executions again.
    // if(this.tradesSearchFacadeService.isExecutionsContext) {
    //   this.fundSearchContext.overrideContext = {
    //     emitField: 'fmr'
    //   }
    // }
  }

  public symbolChanged(symbol: string): void {
    this.tradesSearchFacadeService.updateSymbol(
      symbol ? symbol.toUpperCase() : '',
    );
  }

  public onDateRangeEventTriggered(dateRangeEvent: DateRangeEvent): void {
    this.tradesSearchFacadeService.updateDatePickingMethod(
      dateRangeEvent.dateSelectionType,
    );
    this.tradesSearchFacadeService.updateStartDate(
      dateRangeEvent.dateRange.startDate,
    );
    this.tradesSearchFacadeService.updateEndDate(
      dateRangeEvent.dateRange.endDate,
    );
  }

  public clearAll(event: MouseEvent): void {
    this.tradesSearchFacadeService.clearTrades();
    this.clearDateRange();
    this.clear = {};
  }

  public clearDateRange(): void {
    this.datePicker.clearDatePicker();
  }

  public getTradingData(event: MouseEvent): void {
    const interactionType = getInteractionTypeFromEvent(event);
    this.tradesSearchFacadeService.updateInteractionType(interactionType);
    if (!this.areThereErrors()) {
      this.tradesSearchFacadeService.searchData();
    }
  }

  public areThereErrors(): boolean {
    // previously we used to check that dates have no error but this is going to be checked by the
    // datePicker component itself. It will not emit unless valid
    return this.formGroup.invalid || this.dateError !== '';
  }

  public selectCompanySuggestion(selectedCusips: any): void {
    this.tradesSearchFacadeService.updateCusip(selectedCusips as string[]);
  }

  public removeSymbol(): void {
    this.tradesSearchFacadeService.updateCusip([]);
  }

  public selectFundSuggestion(selectedFunds: any): void {
    this.selectedFunds = selectedFunds as string[];
    this.tradesSearchFacadeService.updateFunds(this.selectedFunds);
  }

  public selectBrokerSuggestion(selectedBrokers: any): void {
    this.selectedBrokers = selectedBrokers as number[];
    this.tradesSearchFacadeService.updateBrokers(
      this.selectedBrokers as number[],
    );
  }

  public selectInstrumentTypesSuggestion(selectedInstrumentTypes: any): void {
    this.selectedInstrumentTypes = selectedInstrumentTypes as string[];
    this.tradesSearchFacadeService.updateInstrumentTypes(
      this.selectedInstrumentTypes as string[],
    );
  }

  public selectTraderSuggestion(selectedTraders: any): void {
    this.selectedTraders = selectedTraders as string[];
    this.tradesSearchFacadeService.updateTraders(
      this.selectedTraders as string[],
    );
  }

  public removeTraders(): void {
    this.tradesSearchFacadeService.updateTraders([]);
  }

  public removeBrokers(): void {
    this.tradesSearchFacadeService.updateBrokers([]);
  }

  public removeFunds(): void {
    this.tradesSearchFacadeService.updateFunds([]);
  }

  public removeIvTypes(): void {
    this.tradesSearchFacadeService.updateInstrumentTypes([]);
  }

  public onCancelledCheckboxClick(event: { checked: boolean }): void {
    this.tradesSearchFacadeService.updateAreCancelledTradesEnabled(
      event.checked,
    );
  }

  public getAuthorizedFunctionObjectNames(): void {
    this.arrowService
      .getAuthorizedFunctionObjectNames(
        ArrowAuthDetails.AppName as string,
        'Trade Activity',
        ArrowAuthDetails.ViewOrdersRole as string,
        ArrowAuthDetails.ObjectTypeName as string,
      )
      .subscribe((resp) => {
        this.store.dispatch(fromTradesSearch.setViewOrdersDesk({ desk: resp }));
      });
  }

  public setDateError(error: string): void {
    this.dateError = error;
  }

  protected getFundContexts(): void {
    if (this.tradesSearchFacadeService.isExecutionsContext) {
      this.fundSearchContext = null;
      // TODO: The fundSearchContext will be reassigned when funds are available for executions again.
      // this.fundSearchContext = {
      //   searchType: SearchType.FundPm,
      //   overrideContext: { emitField: 'shortName' },
      // };
    } else {
      this.fundSearchContext = { searchType: SearchType.FundPm };
    }
  }
}
